Dukapaṭṭhāna

[page 001]
                                                                                 1
           Namo tassa bhagavato arahato sammāsambuddhassa.
                         [I. DUKA-PAṬṬHĀNAṂ.
                               I.
                          HETU-DUKAṂ.]

                          [Anulomaṃ.]
     1. Hetuṃ dhammaṃ paṭicca hetu dhammo uppajjati hetupaccayā.
     Alobhaṃ paṭicca adoso amoho; adosaṃ paṭicca alobho amoho; amohaṃ paṭicca alobho adoso. Lobhaṃ paṭicca moho; mohaṃ paṭicca lobho; dosaṃ paṭicca moho; mohaṃ paṭicca doso. Paṭisandhikkhaṇe . . . pe . . .
     2. Hetuṃ dhammaṃ paṭicca nahetu dhammo uppajjati hetupaccayā.
     Hetuṃ dhammaṃ paṭicca sampayuttakā khandhā cittasamuṭṭhānañ ca rūpaṃ. Paṭisandhikkhaṇe . . . pe . . .
     3. Hetuṃ dhammaṃ paṭicca hetu ca nahetu ca dhammā uppajjanti hetupaccayā.
     Alobhaṃ paṭicca adoso amoho sampayuttakā ca khandhā cittasamuṭṭhānañ ca rūpaṃ . . . (cakkaṃ bandhitabbaṃ)


[page 002]
2                          Hetudukaṃ.
. . . Lobhaṃ paṭicca moho sampayuttakā ca khandhā cittasamuṭṭhānañ ca rūpaṃ . . . pe . . . Paṭisandhikkhaṇe . . . pe . . .
     4. Nahetuṃ dhammaṃ paṭicca nahetu dhammo uppajjati hetupaccayā.
     Nahetuṃ ekaṃ khandhaṃ paṭicca tayo khandhā cittasamuṭṭhānañ ca rūpaṃ. Paṭisandhikkhaṇe khandhe paṭicca vatthu, vatthuṃ paṭicca khandhā; ekaṃ mahābhūtaṃ . . .
pe . . .
     5. Nahetuṃ dhammaṃ paṭicca hetu dhammo uppajjati hetupaccayā.
     Nahetū khandhe paṭicca hetū. Paṭisandhikkhaṇe vatthuṃ paṭicca hetū.
     6. Nahetuṃ dhammaṃ paṭicca hetu ca nahetu ca dhammā uppajjanti hetupaccayā.
     Nahetuṃ ekaṃ khandhaṃ paṭicca tayo khandhā hetū ca cittasamuṭṭhānañ ca rūpaṃ; dve khandhe paṭicca dve khandhā hetu ca cittasamuṭṭhānañ ca rūpaṃ. Paṭisandhikkhaṇe vatthuṃ paṭicca hetū ca sampayuttakā ca khandhā.
     7. Hetuñ ca nahetuñ ca dhammaṃ paṭicca hetu dhammo uppajjati hetupaccayā.
     Alobhañ ca sampayuttake ca khandhe paṭicca adoso amoho . . . (cakkaṃ bandhitabbaṃ) . . . Lobhañ ca sampayuttake ca khandhe paṭicca moho, dosañ ca sampayuttake ca khandhe paṭicca moho. Paṭisandhikkhaṇe alobhañ ca vatthuñ ca paṭicca adoso amoho . . . pe . . .
     8. Hetuñ ca na hetuñ ca dhammaṃ paṭicca nahetu dhammo uppajjati hetupaccayā.
     Nahetuṃ ekaṃ khandhañ ca hetuñ ca paṭicca tayo khandhā cittasamuṭṭhānañ ca rūpaṃ. Dve khandhe ca hetuñ ca paṭicca dve khandhā cittasamuṭṭhānañ ca rūpaṃ. Paṭisandhikkhaṇe vatthuñ ca hetuñ ca paṭicca sampayuttakā khandhā.


[page 003]
                          Anekapaccayā.                3
[... content straddling page break has been moved to the page above ...]
     9. Hetuñ ca nahetuñ ca dhammaṃ paṭicca hetu ca nahetu ca dhammā uppajjanti hetupaccayā.
     Nahetuṃ ekaṃ khandhañ ca alobhañ ca paṭicca tayo khandhā adoso amoho cittasamuṭṭhānañ ca rūpaṃ; dve khandhe ca alobhañ ca paṭicca dve khandhā adoso amoho cittasamuṭṭhānañ ca rūpaṃ . . . (cakkaṃ bandhitabbaṃ) . . .
nahetuṃ ekaṃ khandhañ ca lobhañ ca paṭicca tayo khandhā moho ca cittasamuṭṭhānañ ca rūpaṃ . . . pe . . . dve khandhe . . . pe . . . Paṭisandhikkhaṇe vatthuñ ca alobhañ ca paṭicca adoso amoho sampayuttakā ca khandhā . . . pe . . .
     Hetuṃ dhammaṃ paṭicca hetu dhammo uppajjati ārammaṇapaccayā . . . (rūpaṃ chaḍḍetvā arūpe yeva nava pañhā) . . . adhipatipaccayā . . . (paṭisandhi natthi, paripuṇṇaṃ). Ekaṃ mahābhūtaṃ paṭicca . . . pe . . . mahābhūte paṭicca cittasamuṭṭhānaṃ rūpaṃ, upādā rūpaṃ (idaṃ ninnānaṃ) . . .
anantarapaccayā . . .
samanantarapaccayā . . .
sahajātapaccayā . . . (sabbe mahābhūtā yāva asaññasattā) . . .
aññamaññapaccayā . . .
nissayapaccayā . . .
upanissayapaccayā . . .
purejātapaccayā . . .
āsevanapaccayā . . . (dvīsu paṭisandhi natthi) . . .
kammapaccayā . . .
vipākapaccayā . . . (saṃkhittaṃ) . . .
avigatapaccayā . . .


[page 004]
4                          Hetudukaṃ.
          Hetuyā nava,                     sabbattha nava,
          ārammaṇe nava,                    avigate nava:--
     evaṃ gaṇetabbaṃ.
                          Anulomaṃ niṭṭhitaṃ.
                          [Paccaniyaṃ.]
     4. Nahetuṃ dhammaṃ paṭicca nahetu dhammo uppajjati nahetupaccayā.
     Ahetukaṃ nahetuṃ ekaṃ khandhaṃ paṭicca tayo khandhā cittasamuṭṭhānañ ca rūpaṃ; dve . . . Ahetukapaṭisandhikkhaṇe khandhe paṭicca vatthu, vatthuṃ paṭicca khandhā. Ekaṃ mahābhūtaṃ . . . pe . . . bāhiraṃ āhārasamuṭṭhānaṃ utusamuṭṭhānaṃ . . . pe . . .
     5. Nahetuṃ dhammaṃ paṭicca hetudhammo uppajjati nahetupaccayā.
     Vicikicchāsahagate uddhaccasahagate khandhe paṭicca vicikicchāsahagato uddhaccasahagato moho.
     2. Hetuṃ dhammaṃ paṭicca nahetu dhammo uppajjati nārammaṇapaccayā.
     Hetuṃ paṭicca cittasamuṭṭhānaṃ rūpaṃ. Paṭisandhikkhaṇe . . . pe . . .
     4. Nahetuṃ dhammaṃ paṭicca nahetu dhammo uppajjati nārammaṇapaccayā.
     Nahetū khandhe paṭicca cittasamuṭṭhānaṃ rūpaṃ.
Paṭisandhikkhaṇe . . . (sabbe mahābhūtā) . . .
     8. Hetuñ ca nahetuñ ca dhammaṃ paṭicca nahetu dhammo uppajjati nārammaṇapaccayā.
     Hetuñ ca nahetū ca khandhe paṭicca cittasamuṭṭhānaṃ rūpaṃ. Paṭisandhikkhaṇe . . . pe . . .
nādhipatipaccayā . . . (paripuṇṇaṃ) . . . nānantarapaccayā . . . nasamanantarapaccayā . . . na aññamaññapaccayā . . . na upanissayapaccayā . . .
     1. Hetuṃ dhammaṃ paṭicca hetu dhammo uppajjati napurejātapaccayā.


[page 005]
                Napurejātapaccayavāro. Arūpaṃ.     5
     Arūpe alobhaṃ paṭicca adoso amoho . . . (cakkaṃ bandhitabbaṃ) . . . Lobhaṃ paṭicca moho, mohaṃ paṭicca lobho . . . pe . . . Paṭisandhikkhaṇe . . . pe . . .
     2. Hetuṃ dhammaṃ paṭicca nahetu dhammo uppajjati napurejātapaccayā.
     Arūpe hetuṃ paṭicca sampayuttakā khandhā. Hetuṃ paṭicca cittasamuṭṭhānaṃ rūpaṃ. Paṭisandhikkhaṇe . . .
pe . . .
     3. Hetuṃ dhammaṃ paṭicca hetu ca nahetu ca dhammā uppajjanti napurejātapaccayā.
     Arūpe alobhaṃ paṭicca adoso amoho sampayuttakā ca khandhā . . . (cakkaṃ bandhitabbaṃ) . . . Lobhaṃ paṭicca moho sampayuttakā ca khandhā . . . pe . . . Paṭisandhikkhaṇe . . . pe . . .
     4. Nahetuṃ dhammaṃ paṭicca nahetu dhammo uppajjati napurejātapaccayā.
     Arūpe nahetuṃ ekaṃ khandhaṃ paṭicca tayo khandhā.
Dve khandhe paṭicca dve khandhā. Nahetū khandhe paṭicca cittasamuṭṭhānaṃ rūpaṃ. Paṭisandhikkhaṇe . . . pe . . .
     5. Nahetuṃ dhammaṃ paṭicca hetu dhammo uppajjati napurejātapaccayā.
     Arūpe nahetū khandhe paṭicca hetū. Paṭisandhikkhaṇe . . . pe . . .
     6. Nahetuṃ dhammaṃ paṭicca hetu ca nahetu ca dhammā uppajjanti napurejātapaccayā.
     Arūpe nahetuṃ ekaṃ khandhaṃ paṭicca tayo khandhā hetū ca; dve khandhe . . . pe . . . Paṭisandhikkhaṇe . . . pe . . .
     7. Hetuñ ca nahetuñ ca dhammaṃ paṭicca hetu dhammo uppajjati napurejātapaccayā.
     Arūpe alobhañ ca sampayuttake ca khandhe paṭicca adoso amoho, . . . (cakkaṃ bandhitabbaṃ) . . . arūpe lobhañ ca sampayuttake ca khandhe paṭicca moho . . . (cakkaṃ bandhitabbaṃ) . . . Paṭisandhikkhaṇe . . . pe . . .
     8. Hetuñ ca nahetuñ ca dhammaṃ paṭicca nahetu dhammo uppajjati napurejātapaccayā.


[page 006]
6                          Hetudukaṃ.
     Arūpe nahetuṃ ekaṃ khandhañ ca hetuñ ca paṭicca tayo khandhā . . . pe . . . dve khandhe . . . pe . . . nahetū khandhe ca hetuñ ca paṭicca cittasamuṭṭhānaṃ rūpaṃ.
Paṭisandhikkhaṇe . . . pe . . .
     9. Hetuñ ca nahetuñ ca dhammaṃ paṭicca hetu ca nahetu ca dhammā uppajjanti napurejātapaccayā.
     Arūpe nahetuṃ ekaṃ khandhañ ca alobhaṃ ca paṭicca tayo khandhā adoso amoho ca; . . . pe . . . dve khandhe . . . (cakkaṃ bandhitabbaṃ) . . . nahetuṃ ekaṃ khandhañ ca lobhañ ca paṭicca tayo khandhā moho ca; . . . (cakkaṃ bandhitabbaṃ) . . . Paṭisandhikkhaṇe . . . pe . . .
     1. Hetuṃ dhammaṃ paṭicca hetu dhammo uppajjati napacchājātapaccayā: . . . pe . . . nāsevanapaccayā . . . pe . . .
     2. Hetuṃ dhammaṃ paṭicca nahetu dhammo uppajjati nakammapaccayā.
     Hetuṃ paṭicca sampayuttakā cetanā.
     4. Nahetuṃ dhammaṃ paṭicca nahetu dhammo uppajjati nakammapaccayā.
     Nahetū khandhe paṭicca sampayuttakā cetanā. Bāhiraṃ āhārasamuṭṭhānaṃ utusamuṭṭhānaṃ.
     8. Heṭuñ ca nahetuñ ca dhammaṃ paṭicca nahetu dhammo uppajjati nakammapaccayā.
     Hetuñ ca sampayuttake ca khandhe paṭicca sampayuttakā cetanā.
     1. Hetuṃ dhammaṃ paṭicca hetu dhammo uppajjati navipākapaccayā: . . . pe . . .
     4. Nahetuṃ dhammaṃ paṭicca nahetu dhammo uppajjati nāhārapaccayā.
     Bāhiraṃ utusamuṭṭhānaṃ asaññasattānaṃ. Ekaṃ mahābhūtaṃ paṭicca tayo mahābhūtā.


[page 007]
                          Paccaniyaṃ.                          7
[... content straddling page break has been moved to the page above ...] Mahābhūte paṭicca kaṭattā-rūpaṃ upādā-rūpaṃ . . . pe . . .
. . . na indriyapaccayā . . . Bāhiraṃ āhārasamuṭṭhānaṃ utusamuṭṭhānaṃ. Ekaṃ mahābhūtaṃ . . . pe . . . Mahābhūte paṭicca upādā-rūpaṃ asaññasattānaṃ. Mahābhūte paṭicca rūpajīvitindriyaṃ.
. . . najhānapaccayā . . . Pañcaviññāṇasahagataṃ ekaṃ khandhaṃ . . . pe . . . bāhiraṃ āhārasamuṭṭhānaṃ utusamuṭṭhānaṃ . . . pe . . .
. . . namaggapaccayā . . . Ahetukaṃ nahetuṃ ekaṃ khandhaṃ paṭicca . . . pe . . . Paṭisandhikkhaṇe bāhiraṃ āhārasamuṭṭhānaṃ utusamuṭṭhānaṃ asaññasattānaṃ . . .
pe . . .
. . . nasampayuttapaccayā . . . navippayuttapaccayā . . .
(napurejātasadisaṃ, arūpe yeva.) . . .
. . . nonatthipaccayā . . .
. . . novigatapaccayā . . .
          Nahetuyā dve,                     nakamme tīṇi,
          nārammaṇe tīṇi,                navipāke nava,
          nādhipatiyā nava,                nāhāre ekaṃ,
          nānantare tīṇi,                na-indriye ekaṃ,
          nasamanantare tīṇi,           najhāne ekaṃ,
          na-aññamaññe tīṇi,               namagge ekaṃ,
          na-upanissaye tīṇi,               nasampayutte tīṇi,
          napurejāte nava,                navippayutte nava,
          napacchājāte nava,               nonatthiyā tīṇi,
          nāsevane nava.                novigate tīṇi:-- evaṃ gaṇetabbaṃ.
                         Paccaniyaṃ niṭṭhitaṃ.


[page 008]
8                          Hetudukaṃ.
          Hetupaccayā, nārammaṇe          nāsevane nava,
          tīṇi,                          nakamme tīṇi,
          nādhipatiyā nava,                navipāke nava,
          nānantare tīṇi,                nasampayutte tīṇi,
          (saṃkhittaṃ)                navippayutte nava,
          na upanissaye tīṇi,               nonatthiyā tīṇi,
          napurejāte nava,                novigate tīṇi.
          napacchājāte nava,
                     Anulomapaccaniyaṃ niṭṭhitaṃ.
          Nahetupaccayā, ārammaṇe          indriye dve,
          dve,                          jhāne dve,
          anantare dve (saṃkhittaṃ),      magge ekaṃ,
          kamme dve,                     sampayutte dve (saṃkhittaṃ),
          vipāke ekaṃ,
          āhāre dve,                     avigate dve.
                     Paccaniyānulomaṃ niṭṭhitaṃ.
     (Sahajātavāro pi paṭiccavārasadiso; paccayavāro pi nissayavāro pi paṭiccavārasadisā yeva pañhā. Mahābhūtesu niṭṭhitesu vatthuṃ paccayāti kātabbaṃ. Pañcāyatanāni anulome pi paccaniye pi yathā labbhanti tathā kātabbā.
Saṃsaṭṭhavāro pi sampayuttavāro pi paripuṇṇā. Rūpaṃ natthi, arūpam eva.)
                              [Anulomaṃ.]
     1. Hetu dhammo hetussa dhammassa hetupaccayena paccayo.
     Alobho adosassa amohassa hetupaccayena paccayo . . .


[page 009]
                          Ārammaṇavāro.                         9
(cakkaṃ bandhitabbaṃ) . . . Lobho mohassa hetupaccayena paccayo. Doso mohassa hetupaccayena paccayo. Paṭisandhikkhaṇe . . . pe . . .
     2. Hetu dhammo nahetussa dhammassa hetupaccayena paccayo.
     Hetu sampayuttakānaṃ khandhānaṃ cittasamuṭṭhānānañ ca rūpānaṃ hetupaccayena paccayo. Paṭisandhikkhaṇe . . . pe . . .
     3. Hetu dhammo hetussa ca nahetussa ca dhammassa hetupaccayena paccayo.
     Alobho adosassa amohassa sampayuttakānañ ca khandhānaṃ cittasamuṭṭhānānañ ca rūpānaṃ hetupaccayena paccayo . . . (cakkaṃ bandhitabbaṃ) . . . Lobho mohassa . . . pe . . . Paṭisandhikkhaṇe . . .
     1. Hetu dhammo hetussa dhammassa ārammaṇapaccayena paccayo.
     Hetuṃ ārabbha hetū khandhā uppajjanti.
     2. Hetu dhammo nahetussa dhammassa ārammaṇapaccayena paccayo.
     Hetuṃ ārabbha nahetū khandhā uppajjanti.
     3. Hetu dhammo hetussa ca nahetussa ca dhammassa ārammaṇapaccayena paccayo.
     Hetuṃ ārabbha hetū ca sampayuttakā ca khandhā uppajjanti.
     4. Nahetu dhammo nahetussa dhammassa ārammaṇapaccayena paccayo.
     Dānaṃ datvā sīlaṃ samādiyitvā uposathakammaṃ katvā taṃ paccavekkhati, pubbe suciṇṇāni paccavekkhati, jhānā vuṭṭhahitvā jhānaṃ paccavekkhati. Ariyā maggā vuṭṭhahitvā maggaṃ paccavekkhanti, phalaṃ, nibbāṇaṃ . . .
Nibbānaṃ gotrabhussa vodānassa maggassa phalassa āvajjanāya ārammaṇapaccayena paccayo. Ariyā nahetū pahīnakilese paccavekkhanti,


[page 010]
10                         Hetudukaṃ.
[... content straddling page break has been moved to the page above ...] vikkhambhitakilese, pubbe samudācinne kilese jānanti, cakkhuṃ . . . pe . . . vatthuṃ,
nahetū khandhe aniccato dukkhato anattato vipassanti,
. . . pe . . . domanassaṃ uppajjati, dibbena cakkhunā rūpaṃ passati, dibbāya sotadhātuyā saddaṃ suṇāti, cetopariyañāṇena nahetucittasamaṃgissa cittaṃ jānāti. Ākāsānañcāyatanakiriyaṃ viññāṇañcāyatanakiriyassa, ākiñcaññāyatanakiriyaṃ nevasaññānāsaññāyatanakiriyassa, rūpāyatanaṃ cakkhuviññāṇassa . . . pe . . . phoṭṭhabbāyatanaṃ kāyaviññāṇassa ārammaṇapaccayena paccayo. Nahetū khandhā iddhividhañāṇassa cetopariyañāṇassa pubbenivāsānussatiñāṇassa yathākammūpagañāṇassa anāgataṃsañāṇassa āvajjanāya ārammaṇapaccayena paccayo.
     5. Nahetu dhammo hetussa dhammassa ārammaṇapaccayena paccayo.
     Dānaṃ datvā . . . (paṭhamagamanaṃ yeva. Āvajjanā natthi. Rūpāyatanaṃ cakkhuviññāṇassa . . . pe . . .
phoṭṭhabbāyatanaṃ kāyaviññāṇassāti idaṃ natthi).
     6. Nahetu dhammo hetussa ca nahetussa ca dhammassa ārammaṇapaccayena paccayo.
     Dānaṃ datvā sīlaṃ . . . uposathakammaṃ taṃ paccavekkhati, taṃ ārabbha hetū ca sampayuttakā ca khandhā upajjanti . . . (tatthatatthaṭṭhitena imaṃ kātabbaṃ dutiyagamanasadisaṃ).
     7. Hetu ca nahetu ca dhammā hetussa dhammassa ārammaṇapaccayena paccayo.
     Hetuñ ca sampayuttake ca khandhe ārabbha hetū uppajjanti.


[page 011]
                          Adhipativāro.                11
     8. Hetu ca nahetu ca dhammā nahetussa dhammassa ārammaṇapaccayena paccayo.
     Hetuñ ca sampayuttake ca khandhe ārabbha nahetū khandhā uppajjanti.
     9. Hetu ca nahetu ca dhammā hetussa ca nahetussa ca dhammassa ārammaṇapaccayena paccayo.
     Hetuñ ca sampayuttake ca khandhe ārabbha hetū ca sampayuttakā ca khandhā uppajjanti.
     1. Hetu dhammo hetussa dhammassa adhipatipaccayena paccayo.
     Ārammaṇādhipati, sahajātādhipati. Ārammaṇādhipati:
-- hetuṃ garuṃ katvā hetū uppajjanti. Sahajātādhipati:
-- hetu adhipati sampayuttakānaṃ hetūnaṃ adhipatipaccayena paccayo.
     2. Hetu dhammo nahetussa dhammassa. . . .
     Ārammaṇādhipati, sahajātādhipati. Ārammaṇādhipati:
-- hetuṃ garuṃ katvā nahetū khandhā uppajjanti. Sahajātādhipati:-- hetu adhipati sampayuttakānaṃ khandhānaṃ cittasamuṭṭhānānañ ca rūpānaṃ adhipatipaccayena paccayo.
     3. Hetu dhammo hetussa ca nahetussa ca. . . .
     Ārammaṇādhipati . . . garuṃ katvā hetū ca sampayuttakā ca khandhā uppajjanti. Sahajātādhipati . . .
khandhānaṃ hetūnañ ca cittasamuṭṭhānānañ ca rūpānaṃ adhipatipaccayena paccayo.
     4. Nahetu dhammo nahetussa dhammassa. . . .
     Ārammaṇādhipati, sahajātādhipati. Ārammaṇādhipati:
-- (dānaṃ datvā ti vitthāretabbaṃ yāva nahetū khandhā).
Sahajātādhipati:-- nahetu adhipati sampayuttakānaṃ. . . .
     5. Nahetu dhammo hetussa dhammassa. . . .
     Ārammaṇādhipati, sahajātādhipati. Ārammaṇādhipati:
-- dānaṃ datvā . . . (saṃkhittaṃ yāva vatthu nahetū ca khandhā tāva kātabbaṃ). Sahajātādhipati:-- nahetu adhipati sampayuttakānaṃ. . . .


[page 012]
12                         Hetudukaṃ.
     6. Nahetu dhammo hetussa ca nahetussa ca. . . .
     Ārammaṇādhipati, sahajātādhipati. Ārammaṇādhipati:
-- dānaṃ datvā sīlaṃ uposathakammaṃ katvā taṃ paccavekkhati tam garuṃ katvā nahetū khandhā ca hetū ca uppajjanti. Pubbe suciṇṇāni . . . (yāva vatthu nahetū khandhā ca tāva kātabbam). Sahajātādhipati:-- nahetu adhipati sampayuttakānaṃ khandhānaṃ hetūnañ ca . . .
     7. Hetu ca nahetu ca dhammā hetussa. . . .
     Ārammaṇādhipati:-- hetuñ ca sampayuttake ca khandhe garuṃ katvā hetū uppajjanti.
     8. Hetu ca nahetu ca dhammā nahetussa. . . .
     Ārammaṇādhipati:-- hetuñ ca sampayuttake ca khandhe garuṃ katvā nahetū khandhā uppajjanti.
     9. Hetu ca nahetu ca dhammā hetussa ca. . . .
     Ārammaṇādhipati . . . katvā hetū ca sampayuttakā ca khandhā uppajjanti.
     1. Hetu dhammo hetussa dhammassa anantarapaccayena paccayo.
     Purimā purimā hetū pacchimānaṃ pacchimānaṃ hetūnaṃ anantarapaccayena paccayo.
     2. Hetu dhammo nahetussa dhammassa anantarapaccayena paccayo.
     Purimā . . . pacchimānaṃ nahetūnaṃ khandhānaṃ anantarapaccayena paccayo.
     3. Hetu dhammo hetussa ca nahetussa ca. . . .
     Purimā . . . hetūnaṃ sampayuttakānañ ca khandhānaṃ anantarapaccayena paccayo.
     4. Nahetu dhammo nahetussa dhammassa. . . .
     Purimā purimā nahetū khandhā pacchimānaṃ pacchimānaṃ nahetūnaṃ khandhānaṃ anantarapaccayena paccayo.
Anulomaṃ gotrabhussa . . . (saṃkhittaṃ) . . . Nevasaññānāsaññāyatanaṃ phalasamāpattiyā anantarapaccayena paccayo.

                          Upanissayavāro.               13
[... content straddling page break has been moved to the page above ...]
     5. Nahetu dhammo hetussa dhammassa . . .
     6. Nahetu dhammo hetussa ca nahetussa . . .
     (nahetumūlakaṃ tīṇi pi ekasadisaṃ.)
     7. Hetu ca nahetu ca dhammā hetussa. . . .
     Purimā purimā hetū ca sampayuttakā ca khandhā pacchimānaṃ pacchimānaṃ hetūnaṃ anantarapaccayena paccayo.
     8. Hetu ca nahetu ca dhammā nahetussa. . . .
     Purimā . . . pacchimānaṃ nahetūnaṃ khandhānaṃ anantarapaccayena paccayo.
     9. Hetu ca nahetu ca dhammā hetussa ca. . . .
     Purimā . . . pacchimānaṃ hetūnaṃ sampayuttakānañ ca khandhānaṃ anantarapaccayena paccayo.
     Hetu dhammo hetussa dhammassa samanantarapaccayena paccayo. . . . (anantarasadisaṃ) . . . sahajātapaccayena paccayo . . . aññamaññapaccayena paccayo . . . (ime dve paṭiccavārasadisā) . . . nissayapaccayena paccayo. . . . (paccayavāro nissayavārasadiso).
     1. Hetu dhammo hetussa dhammassa upanissayapaccayena paccayo.
     Ārammaṇūpanissayo, anantarūpanissayo pakatūpanissayo . . . pe . . . Pakatūpanissayo:-- hetū hetūnaṃ upanissayapaccayena paccayo.
     2. Hetu dhammo nahetussa dhammassa. . . .
     Ārammaṇūpanissayo . . . hetū nahetūnaṃ khandhānaṃ upanissayapaccayena paccayo.


[page 014]
14                         Hetudukaṃ.
     3. Hetu dhammo hetussa ca nahetussa ca. . . .
     Ārammaṇūpanissayo . . . hetūnaṃ sampayuttakānañ ca khandhānaṃ upanissayapaccayena paccayo.
     4. Nahetu dhammo nahetussa dhammassa. . . .
     Ārammaṇūpanissayo . . . pe . . . Pakatūpanissayo:-- saddhaṃ upanissāya dānaṃ deti . . . pe . . . samāpattiṃ uppādeti. . . . Mānaṃ jappeti diṭṭhiṃ gaṇhāti. Sīlaṃ . . . pe . . . senāsanaṃ upanissāya dānaṃ deti . . . pe . . .
saṃghaṃ bhindati; saddhā . . . pe . . . senāsanaṃ saddhāya . . . pe . . . catutthassa maggassa . . . pe . . . phalasamāpattiyā upanissayapaccayena paccayo.
     5. Nahetu dhammo hetussa dhammassa . . .
     Ārammaṇūpanissayo. . . . saddhaṃ . . . pe . . .
senāsanaṃ upanissāya dānaṃ deti . . . pe . . . saṃghaṃ bhindati; saddhā . . . pe . . . senāsanaṃ saddhāya . . .
pe . . . patthanāya maggassa phalasamāpattiyā upanissayapaccayena paccayo.
     6. Nahetu dhammo hetussa ca nahetussa ca. . . .

     7. Hetu ca nahetu ca dhammā hetussa. . . .
     Ārammaṇūpanissayo . . . pe . . . Pakatūpanissayo:-- hetū ca sampayuttakā ca khandhā hetūnaṃ upanissayapaccayena paccayo.
     8. Hetu ca nahetu ca dhammā nahetussa. . . .
     Ārammanūpanissayo . . . khandhā nahetūnaṃ khandhānaṃ upanissayapaccayena paccayo.
     9. Hetu ca nahetu ca dhammā hetussa ca. . . .
     Ārammaṇūpanissayo . . . hetūnañ ca sampayuttakānañ ca khandhānaṃ upanissayapaccayena paccayo.


[page 015]
                          Pacchājātavāro.               15
     4. Nahetu dhammo nahetussa dhammassa purejātapaccayena paccayo.
     Ārammaṇapurejātaṃ, vatthupurejātaṃ. Ārammaṇapurejātaṃ:-- arahā cakkhuṃ . . . pe . . . vatthuṃ aniccato dukkhato anattato vipassati; . . . pe . . . domanassaṃ uppajjati; dibbena cakkhunā rūpaṃ passati, dibbāya sotadhātuyā saddaṃ suṇāti; rūpāyatanaṃ cakkhuviññāṇassa . . .
pe . . . phoṭṭhabbāyatanaṃ kāyaviññāṇassa purejātapaccayena paccayo. Vatthupurejātaṃ:-- cakkhāyatanaṃ cakkhuviññāṇassa purejātapaccayena paccayo, . . . pe . . .
kāyāyatanaṃ kāyaviññāṇassa purejātapaccayena paccayo.
Vatthu nahetūnaṃ khandhānaṃ purejātapaccayena paccayo.
     5. Nahetu dhammo hetussa dhammassa. . . .
     Ārammaṇapurejātaṃ, vatthupurejātaṃ. Ārammaṇapurejātaṃ:-- cakkhuṃ . . . pe . . . vatthuṃ aniccato . . . pe . . .
domanassaṃ uppajjati; dibbena cakkhunā rūpaṃ passati,
dibbāya sotadhātuyā saddaṃ suṇāti. Vatthupurejātaṃ:-- vatthuṃ hetūnaṃ purejātapaccayena paccayo.
     6. Nahetu dhammo hetussa ca nahetussa ca. . . .
     Ārammaṇapurejātaṃ . . . pe . . . Vatthupurejātaṃ:-- vatthu hetūnaṃ sampayuttakānañ ca khandhānaṃ purejātapaccayena paccayo.
     2. Hetu dhammo nahetussa dhammassa pacchājātapaccayena paccayo.
     Pacchājātā hetū purejātassa imassa kāyassa pacchājātapaccayena paccayo.
     4. Nahetu dhammo nahetussa dhammassa pacchājātapaccayena paccayo.
     Pacchājātā nahetū khandhā purejātassa . . .
     8. Hetu ca nahetu ca dhammā nahetussa. . . .
     Pacchājātā hetū ca sampayuttakā ca khandhā purejātassa. . . .


[page 016]
16                         Hetudukaṃ.
     1. Hetu dhammo hetussa dhammassa āsevanapaccayena paccayo . . . (anantarasadisaṃ).
     4. Nahetu dhammo nahetussa dhammassa kammapaccayena paccayo.
     Sahajātā, nānākhaṇikā. Sahajātā:-- nahetu cetanā sampayuttakānaṃ khandhānaṃ cittasamuṭṭhānānañ ca rūpānaṃ kammapaccayena paccayo. Nānākhaṇikā:-- nahetu cetanā vipākānaṃ khandhānaṃ kaṭattā ca rūpānaṃ kammapaccayena paccayo.
     5. Nahetu dhammo hetussa dhammassa. . . .
     Sahajātā . . . sampayuttakānaṃ hetūnaṃ kammapaccayena paccayo. Nānākhaṇikā:-- nahetu cetanā vipākānaṃ hetūnaṃ kammapaccayena paccayo.
     6. Nahetu dhammo hetussa ca nahetussa ca. . . .
     Sahajātā: . . . khandhānaṃ hetūnañ ca cittasamuṭṭhānānañ ca . . . khandhānaṃ hetūnañ ca kaṭattā ca rūpānaṃ kammapaccayena paccayo.
     1. Hetu dhammo hetussa dhammassa vipākapaccayena paccayo.
     Vipāko alobho adosassa amohassa vipākapaccayena paccayo . . . (paṭiccavārasadisaṃ. Vipākavibhaṃge nava pañhā).
     4. Nahetu dhammo nahetussa dhammassa āhārapaccayena paccayo.
     Nahetū āhārā sampayuttakānaṃ khandhānaṃ cittasamuṭṭhānānañ ca rūpānaṃ āhārapaccayena paccayo. Paṭisandhikkhaṇe kabaḷiṃkāro āhāro imassa kāyassa āhārapaccayena paccayo.
     5. Nahetu dhammo hetussa dhammassa āhārapaccayena paccayo.
     Nahetū āhārā sampayuttakānaṃ hetūnaṃ āhārapaccayena paccayo. Paṭisandhikkhaṇe . . . pe . . .
     6. Nahetu dhammo hetussa ca nahetussa ca dhammassa āhārapaccayena paccayo.


[page 017]
                         Vippayuttapaccayo.           17
     Nahetū āhārā sampayuttakānaṃ khandhānam hetūnaṃ ca cittasamuṭṭhānānañ ca rūpānaṃ āhārapaccayena paccayo.
Paṭisandhikkhaṇe . . . pe . . .
     1. Hetu dhammo hetussa dhammassa indriyapaccayena paccayo . . . (hetumūlake tīṇi).
     4. Nahetu dhammo nahetussa dhammassa indriyapaccayena paccayo.
     Nahetū indriyā sampayuttakānaṃ khandhānaṃ cittasamuṭṭhānānañ ca rūpānaṃ indriyapaccayena paccayo. Paṭisandhikkhaṇe rūpajīvitindriyaṃ kaṭattā rūpānaṃ indriyapaccayena paccayo. . . . (evaṃ indriyapaccayo vitthāretabbo,
nava).
     4. Nahetu dhammo nahetussa dhammassa jhānapaccayena paccayo . . . (tīṇi).
     1. Hetu dhammo hetussa dhammassa maggapaccayena paccayo . . . sampayuttapaccayena paccayo . . . (imesu dvīsu nava).
     2. Hetu dhammo nahetussa dhammassa vippayuttapaccayena paccayo.
     Sahajātaṃ, pacchājātaṃ. Sahajātā:-- hetū cittasamuṭṭhānānaṃ rūpānaṃ vippayuttapaccayena paccayo. Paṭisandhikkhaṇe hetū kaṭattā rūpānaṃ vippayuttapaccayena paccayo. Hetū vatthussa vippayuttapaccayena paccayo.
Pacchājātā:-- hetū purejātassa imassa kāyassa vippayuttapaccayena paccayo.
     4. Nahetu dhammo nahetussa dhammassa vippayuttapaccayena paccayo.
     Sahajātaṃ, purejātaṃ, pacchājātaṃ. Sahajātā:-- nahetū khandhā cittasamuṭṭhānānaṃ . . . Paṭisandhikkhaṇe nahetū khandhā kaṭattā rūpānaṃ vippayuttapaccayena paccayo.


[page 018]
18                         Hetudukaṃ.
[... content straddling page break has been moved to the page above ...] Khandhā vatthussa, vatthu khandhānaṃ vippayuttapaccayena paccayo. Purejātaṃ:-- cakkhāyatanaṃ . . . pe . . . kāyāyatanaṃ . . . pe . . . vatthu nahetūnaṃ khandhānaṃ vippayuttapaccayena paccayo. Pacchājātā nahetū khandhā purejātassa imassa kāyassa vippayuttapaccayena paccayo.
     5. Nahetu dhammo hetussa dhammassa . . .
     Sahajātaṃ, purejātaṃ. Sahajātaṃ:-- paṭisandhikkhaṇe vatthu hetūnaṃ vippayuttapaccayena paccayo. Purejātaṃ:-- vatthu hetūnaṃ vippayuttapaccayena paccayo.
     6. Nahetu dhammo hetussa ca nahetussa ca . . .
     Sahajātaṃ . . . hetūnaṃ sampayuttakānañ ca khandhānaṃ vippayuttapaccayena paccayo. Purejātaṃ:-- vatthu hetūnaṃ sampayuttakānañ ca khandhānaṃ vippayuttapaccayena paccayo.
     8. Hetu ca nahetu ca dhammā nahetussa . . .
     Sahajātaṃ, pacchājātaṃ. Sahajātā:-- hetū ca sampayuttakā ca khandhā cittasamuṭṭhānānaṃ rūpānaṃ vippayuttapaccayena paccayo. Paṭisandhikkhaṇe hetū ca sampayuttakā ca khandhā kaṭattā rūpānaṃ vippayuttapaccayena paccayo. Pacchājātā:-- hetū ca sampayuttakā ca khandhā purejātassa imassa kāyassa vippayuttapaccayena paccayo.
     1. Hetu dhammo hetussa dhammassa atthipaccayena paccayo.
     Alobho adosassa amohassa atthipaccayena paccayo . . .
(cakkaṃ bandhitabbaṃ) . . . Lobho mohassa atthipaccayena paccayo . . . (cakkaṃ bandhitabbaṃ) . . . Paṭisandhikkhaṇe . . . pe . . .
     2. Hetu dhammo nahetussa dhammassa . . .
     Sahajātaṃ, pacchājātaṃ. Sahajātā hetū sampayuttakānaṃ khandhānaṃ cittasamuṭṭhānānañ ca rūpānaṃ atthipaccayena paccayo.


[page 019]
                          Atthipaccayo.                19
[... content straddling page break has been moved to the page above ...] Paṭisandhikkhaṇe . . . Pacchājātā hetū purejātassa imassa kāyassa atthipaccayena paccayo.
     3. Hetu dhammo hetussa ca nahetussa ca. . . .
     Alobho adosassa amohassa sampayuttakānañ ca khandhānaṃ cittasamuṭṭhānānañ ca rūpānaṃ atthipaccayena paccayo . . . (cakkaṃ bandhitabbaṃ) . . . Lobho mohassa sampayuttakānañ ca khandhānaṃ cittasamuṭṭhānānañ ca rūpānaṃ atthipaccayena paccayo . . . (cakkaṃ bandhitabbaṃ) . . . Paṭisandhikkhaṇe . . . pe . . .
     4. Nahetu dhammo nahetussa dhammassa . . .
     Sahajātaṃ, purejātaṃ, pacchājātaṃ āhāraṃ indriyaṃ.
Sahajāto nahetu eko khandho tiṇṇannaṃ khandhānaṃ cittasamuṭṭhānānañ ca rūpānaṃ atthipaccayena paccayo;
dve khandhā . . . pe . . . Paṭisandhikkhaṇe nahetu eko khandho tiṇṇannaṃ khandhānaṃ . . . (cakkaṃ bandhitabbaṃ) . . . Khandhā vatthussa atthipaccayena paccayo. Vatthu khandhānaṃ kaṭattā ca rūpānaṃ atthipaccayena paccayo.
Ekaṃ mahābhūtaṃ . . . pe . . . bāhiraṃ āhārasamuṭṭhānaṃ utusamuṭṭhānaṃ asaññasattānaṃ . . . pe . . . Purejātaṃ cakkhuṃ . . . pe . . . vatthuṃ . . . pe . . . dibbena cakkhunā rūpaṃ passati, dibbāya sotadhātuyā saddaṃ suṇāti; rūpāyatanaṃ . . . pe . . . phoṭṭhabbāyatanaṃ . . . pe . . . cakkhāyatanaṃ . . . pe . . . kāyāyatanaṃ kāyaviññāṇassa atthipaccayena paccayo. Vatthu nahetūnaṃ khandhānaṃ atthipaccayena paccayo. Pacchājātā nahetū khandhā purejātassa imassa kāyassa atthipaccayena paccayo. Kabaliṃkāro āhāro imassa . . . Rūpajīvitindriyaṃ kaṭattā rūpānaṃ atthipaccayena paccayo.
     5. Nahetu dhammo hetussa dhammassa. . . .
     Sahajātaṃ, purejātaṃ. Sahajātā -- nahetū khandhā sampayuttakānaṃ hetūnaṃ atthipaccayena paccayo. Paṭisandhikkhaṇe vatthu hetūnaṃ atthipaccayena paccayo.

20                         Hetudukaṃ.
[... content straddling page break has been moved to the page above ...]
Purejātaṃ cakkhuṃ . . . vatthuṃ aniccato . . . domanassaṃ uppajjati . . . dibbena cakkhunā . . . pe . . . saddaṃ suṇāti . . . Vatthu hetūnaṃ atthipaccayena paccayo.
     6. Nahetu dhammo hetussa ca nahetussa ca. . . .
     Sahajātaṃ, purejātaṃ. Sahajāto nahetu eko khandho tiṇṇannaṃ khandhānaṃ hetūnaṃ cittasamuṭṭhānānañ ca rūpānaṃ atthipaccayena paccayo. Paṭisandhikkhaṇe vatthu hetūnaṃ sampayuttakānañ ca khandhānaṃ atthipaccayena paccayo. Purejātaṃ cakkhuṃ . . . pe . . .
saddaṃ suṇāti. . . . Vatthuṃ hetūnaṃ sampayuttakānañ ca khandhānaṃ atthipaccayena paccayo.
     7. Hetu ca nahetu ca dhammā hetussa. . . .
     Sahajātaṃ, purejātaṃ. Sahajāto alobho ca sampayuttakā ca khandhā adosassa amohassa atthipaccayena paccayo . . . (cakkaṃ bandhitabbaṃ) . . . Lobho ca sampayuttakā ca khandhā mohassa atthipaccayena paccayo . . . (cakkaṃ bandhitabbaṃ) . . . Paṭisandhikkhaṇe alobho ca vatthu ca adosassa amohassa atthipaccayena paccayo . . . (cakkaṃ).
     8. Hetu ca nahetu ca dhammā nahetussa. . . .
     Sahajātaṃ . . . pe . . . Paṭisandhikkhaṇe hetū ca vatthu ca nahetūnaṃ khandhānaṃ atthipaccayena paccayo. Sahajātā hetū ca mahābhūtā ca cittasamuṭṭhānānaṃ rūpānaṃ atthipaccayena paccayo. Pacchājātā hetū ca kabaḷiṃkāro āhāro ca imassa kāyassa atthipaccayena paccayo. Pacchājātā hetū ca rūpajīvitindriyaṃ ca kaṭattā rūpānaṃ atthipaccayena paccayo.
     9. Hetu ca nahetu ca dhammā hetussa ca. . . .
     Sahajātaṃ, purejātaṃ. Sahajāto nahetu eko khandho ca alobho ca tiṇṇannaṃ khandhānaṃ adosassa amohassa ca cittasamuṭṭhānānañ ca rūpānaṃ atthipaccayena paccayo


[page 021]
                          Paccaniyaṃ.                21
. . . (cakkaṃ bandhitabbaṃ) . . . Nahetu eko khandho ca lobho ca tiṇṇannaṃ khandhānaṃ mohassa ca cittasamuṭṭhānānañ ca rūpānaṃ atthipaccayena paccayo . . .
cakkaṃ bandhitabbaṃ) . . . Paṭisandhikkhaṇe nahetu eko khandho ca alobho ca vatthu ca adosassa amohassa sampayuttakānaṃ ca khandhānaṃ atthipaccayena paccayo . . . pe . . .
     natthipaccayena paccayo. . . .
     vigatapaccayena paccayo. . . .
     avigatapaccayena paccayo. . . .
          Hetuyā tīṇi,                     kamme tīṇi,
          ārammaṇe nava,                    vipāke nava,
          adhipatiyā nava,                āhāre tīṇi,
          anantare nava,                    indriye nava,
          samanantare nava,                jhāne tīṇi,
          sahajāte nava,                    magge nava,
          aññamaññe nava,                sampayutte nava,
          nissaye nava,                     vippayutte pañca,
          upanissaye nava                atthiyā nava,
          purejāte tīṇi,                    natthiyā nava,
          pacchājāte tīṇi,                vigate nava,
          āsevane nava,                     avigate nava:--
     Evaṃ anumajjantena gaṇetabbaṃ. Anulomaṃ niṭṭhitaṃ.
                          [Paccaniyaṃ.]
     1. Hetu dhammo hetussa dhammassa ārammaṇapaccayena paccayo . . . sahajāta- . . . upanissayapaccayena paccayo. . . .
     2. Hetu dhammo nahetussa dhammassa ārammaṇa. . . sahajāta- . . . upanissaya- . . . purejāta- . . .
pacchājātapaccayena paccayo. . . .
     3. Hetu dhammo hetussa ca . . . dhammassa. . . .
     4. Nahetu . . . nahetussa . . . ārammaṇa- . . . sahajāta. .

     1. Sahetukaṃ dhammaṃ paṭicca sahetuko dhammo uppajjati hetupaccayā.

pe . . .
     2. Sahetukaṃ dhammaṃ paṭicca ahetuko dhammo uppajjati hetupaccayā.
     Sahetuke khandhe paṭicca cittasamuṭṭhānaṃ rūpaṃ.
Paṭisandhikkhaṇe . . . pe . . .
     3. Sahetukaṃ dhammaṃ paṭicca sahetuko ca. . . .
     Sahetukaṃ ekaṃ khandhaṃ paṭicca tayo khandhā cittasamuṭṭhānañ ca rūpaṃ; dve . . . pe . . . Paṭisandhikkhaṇe . . . pe . . .
     4. Ahetukaṃ dhammaṃ paṭicca ahetuko . . .
     Vicikicchāsahagataṃ uddhaccasahagataṃ mohaṃ paṭicca cittasamuṭṭhānaṃ rūpaṃ. Ekaṃ mahābhūtaṃ paṭicca tayo mahābhūtā . . . pe . . . mahābhūte paṭicca cittasamuṭṭhānaṃ rūpaṃ kaṭattā rūpaṃ upādā rūpaṃ.
     5. Ahetukaṃ dhammaṃ paṭicca sahetuko . . .
     Vicikicchāsahagataṃ uddhaccasahagataṃ mohaṃ paṭicca sampayuttakā khandhā. Paṭisandhikkhaṇe vatthuṃ paṭicca sahetukā khandhā.

     Vicikicchāsahagataṃ . . . khandhā cittasamuṭṭhānañ ca rūpaṃ.

          purejātapaccayā . . .           sahajātavārasadisā. Bāhirā
          āsevanapaccayā . . .           mahābhūtā natthi.)

          indriye nava,                     atthiyā nava,
          jhāne nava,                     natthiyā cha,

          vippayutte nava,
     evaṃ gaṇetabbaṃ.

30                Sahetukadukaṃ.
     1. Sahetukaṃ dhammaṃ paṭicca sahetuko dhammo uppajjati nādhipatipaccayā . . . (anulome sahajātasadisā) . . .

     2. Sahetukaṃ dhammaṃ paṭicca ahetuko dhammo uppajjati napurejātapaccayā.
     Arūpe vicikicchāsahagate uddhaccasahagate khandhe paṭicca vicikicchāsahagato uddhaccasahagato moho. Sahetuke khandhe paṭicca cittasamuṭṭhānaṃ rūpaṃ. Paṭisandhikkhaṇe . . . pe . . .
     3. Sahetukaṃ dhammaṃ paṭicca sahetuko ca . . .
     Arūpe vicikicchāsahagataṃ uddhaccasahagataṃ ekaṃ khandhaṃ paṭicca tayo khandhā moho ca, . . . pe . . .
dve khandhe . . . pe . . . Paṭisandhikkhaṇe . . .
     4. Ahetukaṃ dhammaṃ paṭicca ahetuko . . .
     Arūpe ahetukaṃ ekaṃ khandhaṃ . . . pe . . . dve ahetuke khandhe paṭicca cittasamuṭṭhānaṃ rūpaṃ. Vicikicchāsahagataṃ uddhaccasahagataṃ mohaṃ paṭicca cittasamuṭṭhānaṃ rūpaṃ. Paṭisandhikkhaṇe . . . (yāva asaññasattā tāva vitthāro).
     5. Ahetukaṃ dhammaṃ paṭicca sahetuko . . .
     Arūpe vicikicchāsahagataṃ uddhaccasahagataṃ mohaṃ paṭicca sampayuttakā khandhā. Paṭisandhikkhaṇe vatthuṃ paṭicca sahetukā khandhā.
     6. Ahetukaṃ dhammaṃ paṭicca sahetuko ca ahetuko . . .
     Paṭisandhikkhaṇe vatthuṃ paṭicca sahetukā khandhā,
mahābhūte paṭicca kaṭattā rūpaṃ.


[page 031]
                          Anekapaccayā.                    31
     7. Sahetukañ ca ahetukañ ca . . . sahetuko. . . .
     Arūpe vicikicchāsahagataṃ uddhaccasahagataṃ ekaṃ khandhañ ca mohañ ca paṭicca tayo khandhā . . . pe . . .
Paṭisandhikkhaṇe sahetukaṃ ekaṃ khandhañ ca vatthuñ
     ca paṭicca tayo khandhā; dve . . . pe . . .
     8. Sahetukañ ca ahetukañ ca . . . ahetuko . . .
     Sahetuke khandhe ca mahābhūte ca paṭicca cittasamuṭṭhānaṃ rūpaṃ. Vicikicchāsahagate uddhaccasahagate khandhe ca mohaṃ ca paṭicca cittasamuṭṭhānaṃ rūpaṃ.
     9. Sahetukañ ca ahetukañ ca . . . sahetuko ca . . .
     Paṭisandhikkhaṇe . . . dve khandhe . . . pe . . .
Sahetuke khandhe ca mahābhūte ca paṭicca kaṭattā rūpaṃ.
     1. Sahetukaṃ dhammaṃ paṭicca sahetuko dhammo uppajjati napacchājātapaccayā . . . nāsevanapaccayā . . .
nakammapaccayā.
     Sahetuke khandhe paṭicca sahetukā cetanā.
     4. Ahetukaṃ dhammaṃ paṭicca ahetuko dhammo uppajjati nakammapaccayā.
     Ahetuke khandhe paṭicca ahetukā cetanā, bāhiraṃ āhārasamuṭṭhānaṃ utusamuṭṭhānaṃ . . . pe . . .
     5. Ahetukaṃ dhammaṃ paṭicca sahetuko dhammo uppajjaṭi nakammapaccayā.
     Vicikicchāsahagataṃ uddhaccasahagataṃ mohaṃ paṭicca sampayuttakā cetanā.
     7. Sahetukañ ca ahetukañ ca dhammaṃ sahetuko . . .
     Vicikicchāsahagate uddhaccasahagate khandhe ca mohañ ca paṭicca sampayuttakā cetanā.
     . . . na vipākapaccayā . . . (paṭisandhi natthi).
     4. Ahetukaṃ dhammaṃ paṭicca ahetuko dhammo uppajjati nāhārapaccayā . . . na-indriyapaccayā . . . najhānapaccayā . . . namaggapaccayā . . . nasampayuttapaccayā . . .

32                          Sahetukadukaṃ.
     1. Sahetukaṃ dhammaṃ paṭicca sahetuko dhammo uppajjati navippayuttapaccayā.
     Arūpe sahetukaṃ ekaṃ khandhaṃ . . . pe . . .
     2. Sahetukaṃ dhammaṃ paṭicca ahetuko dhammo . . .
     Arūpe vicikicchāsahagate uddhaccasahagate khandhe paṭicca vicikicchāsahagato uddhaccasahagato moho.
     3. Sahetukaṃ dhammaṃ paṭicca sahetuko ca ahetuko . . .
     Arūpe vicikicchāsahagataṃ uddhaccasahagataṃ ekaṃ khandhaṃ paṭicca tayo khandhā moho ca; dve khandhe . . . pe . . .
     4. Ahetukaṃ dhammaṃ paṭicca ahetuko dhammo uppajjati navippayuttapaccayā.
     Arūpe ahetukaṃ ekaṃ khandhaṃ paṭicca tayo khandhā;
dve . . . pe . . .
     5. Ahetukaṃ dhammaṃ paṭicca sahetuko . . .
     Arūpe vicikicchāsahagataṃ uddhaccasahagataṃ mohaṃ paṭicca sampayuttakā khandhā.
     7. Sahetukañ ca ahetukañ ca . . . sahetuko . . .
     Arūpe vicikicchāsahagataṃ uddhaccasahagataṃ ekaṃ khandhañ ca mohañ ca paṭicca tayo khandhā; dve . . .
pe . . . nonatthipaccayā . . . novigatapaccayā . . .
     Nahetuyā dve,                     nakamme cattāri,
     nārammaṇe tīṇi,                    navipāke nava,
     nadhipatiyā nava,                nāhāre ekaṃ,
     nānantare tīṇi,                    na-indriye ekaṃ,
     nasamanantare tīṇi,                najhāne ekaṃ,
     na-aññamaññe tīṇi,                namagge ekaṃ,
     na-upanissaye tīṇi,                nasampayutte tīṇi,
     napurejāte nava,                navippayutte cha,
     napacchājāte nava,                nonatthiyā tīṇi,
     nāsevane nava,                     novigate tīṇi:--
     evaṃ gaṇetabbaṃ.
                     Paccaniyaṃ niṭṭhitaṃ.


[page 033]
                          Paccayavāro.                     33
          Hetupaccayā,                     napacchājāte nava,
          nārammaṇe tīṇi,                nāsevane nava,
          nādhipatiyā nava,                nakamme tīṇi,
          nānantare tīṇi,                navipāke nava,
          nasamanantare tīṇi,               nasampayutte tīṇi,
          na-aññamaññe tīṇi,                navippayutte tīṇi,
          na-upanissaye tīṇi,               nonatthiyā tīṇi,
          napurejāte nava,                novigate tīṇi:--
     evaṃ gaṇetabbaṃ.
                     Anulomapaccaniyaṃ niṭṭhitaṃ.
          Nahetupaccayā,                indriye dve,
          ārammaṇe dve,                     jhāne dve,
          anantare dve,                     magge ekaṃ,
          sabbattha dve,                    sampayutte dve,
          vipāke ekaṃ,                     avigate dve:--
          āhāre dve,
     evaṃ gaṇetabbaṃ.
                     Paccaniyānulomaṃ niṭṭhitaṃ.
                     (Sahajātavāro paṭiccavārasadiso.)
     1. Sahetukaṃ dhammaṃ paccayā sahetuko dhammo uppajjati hetupaccayā . . . (sahetukamūlakaṃ paṭiccasadisaṃ.
Ahetukamūlakaṃ paṭiccasadisaṃ yeva).
     5. Ahetukaṃ dhammaṃ paccayā sahetuko dhammo uppajjati hetupaccayā.
     Vatthuṃ paccayā sahetukā khandhā. Vicikicchāsahagataṃ uddhaccasahagataṃ mohaṃ paccayā sampayuttakā khandhā. Paṭisandhikkhaṇe vatthuṃ paccayā sahetukā khandhā.
     6. Ahetukaṃ dhammaṃ paccayā sahetuko ca. . . .
     Vatthuṃ paccayā sahetukā khandhā. Mahābhūte paccayā cittasamuṭṭhānaṃ rūpaṃ.

pe . . .
     7. Sahetukañ ca ahetukañ ca . . . sahetuko. . . .
     Sahetukaṃ ekaṃ khandhañ ca vatthuñ ca paccayā tayo khandhā, dve . . . pe . . . Vicikicchāsahagataṃ uddhaccasahagataṃ ekaṃ khandhañ ca mohañ ca paccayā tayo khandhā, dve. . . . Paṭisandhikkhaṇe . . . pe. . . .

     Sahetuke khandhe ca mahādhūte ca paccayā cittasamuṭṭhānaṃ rūpaṃ. Vicikicchāsahagate uddhaccasahagate khandhe mohañ ca paccayā cittasamuṭṭhānaṃ rūpaṃ.
Paṭisandhikkhaṇe . . .

Vicikicchāsahagataṃ uddhaccasahagataṃ ekaṃ khandhañ ca mohañ ca paccayā tayo khandhā cittasamuṭṭhānañ ca rūpaṃ; dve . . . Paṭisandhikkhaṇe sahetukaṃ ekaṃ khandhañ ca vatthuñ ca paccayā tayo khandhā; dve . . .

pe . . . Paṭisandhikkhaṇe . . . pe . . .

[page 035]
                          Sahajātavāro.                     35
     4. Ahetukaṃ dhammaṃ paccayā ahetuko. . . .
     Ahetukaṃ ekaṃ khandhaṃ . . . pe . . . dve. . . . Paṭisandhikkhaṇe vatthuṃ paccayā khandhā, cakkhāyatanaṃ paccayā cakkhuviññāṇaṃ . . . pe . . . kāyāyatanaṃ paccayā kāyaviññāṇaṃ; vatthuṃ paccayā ahetukā khandhā.
     5. Ahetukaṃ dhammaṃ paccayā sahetuko . . .
     Vatthuṃ paccayā sahetukā khandhā. Vicikicchāsahagataṃ uddhaccasahagataṃ mohaṃ paccayā sampayuttakā khandhā. Paṭisandhikkhaṇe . . . pe . . .
     6. Ahetukaṃ dhammaṃ paccayā sahetuko ca ahetuko ca dhammā uppajjanti ārammaṇapaccayā.
     Vatthuṃ paccayā vicikicchāsahagatā uddhaccasahagatā khandhā ca moho ca.
     7. Sahetukañ ca ahetukañ ca dhammaṃ paccayā sahetuko dhammo uppajjati ārammaṇapaccayā.
     Saketukaṃ ekaṃ khandhañ ca vatthuñ ca paccayā tayo khandhā. Vicikicchāsahagataṃ uddhaccasahagataṃ ekaṃ khandhañ ca mohañ ca paccayā tayo khandhā; dve . . .
Paṭisandhikkhaṇe . . . pe . . .
     8. Sahetukañ ca ahetukañ ca . . . ahetuko. . . .
     Vicikicchāsahagate uddhaccasahagate khandhe ca vatthuñ ca paccayā vicikicchāsahagato uddhaccasahagato moho.
     9. Sahetukañ ca ahetukañ ca dhammaṃ paccayā sahetuko ca ahetuko ca dhammā uppajjanti ārammaṇapaccayā.
     Vicikicchā . . . khandhañ ca vatthuñ ca paccayā tayo khandhā moho ca, . . . pe . . . Dve khandhe paccayā dve khandhā moho ca.
     1. Sahetukaṃ dhammaṃ paccayā sahetuko dhammo uppajjati adhipatipaccayā . . . (adhipatiyā nava pañhā pavatte yeva) . . . anantarapaccayā . . . samanantarapaccayā . . . sahajātapaccayā (tīṇi paṭiccavārasadisā).
     4. Ahetukaṃ dhammaṃ paccayā ahetuko dhammo uppajjati sahajātapaccayā.
     Ahetukaṃ ekaṃ khandhaṃ paccayā tayo khandhā cittasamuṭṭhānañ ca rūpaṃ . . . pe . . . dve, . . . (paṭisandhi yāva asaññasattā).

36                    Sahetukadukaṃ.
[... content straddling page break has been moved to the page above ...] Cakkhāyatanaṃ paccayā cakkhuviññāṇaṃ; kāyāyatanaṃ paccayā kāyaviññāṇaṃ; vatthuṃ paccayā ahetukā khandhā.
     5. Ahetukaṃ dhammaṃ paccayā sahetuko. . . .
     Vatthuṃ paccayā sahetukā khandhā. Vicikicchāsaha gataṃ uddhaccasahagataṃ mohaṃ paccayā sampayuttakā khandhā. Paṭisandhikkhaṇe . . . pe . . .
     6. Ahetukaṃ dhammaṃ paccayā sahetuko ca. . . .
     Vatthuṃ paccayā sahetukā khandhā, mahābhūte paccayā cittasamuṭṭhānaṃ rūpaṃ. Vicikicchāsahagataṃ. . . .
khandhā cittasamuṭṭhānañ ca rūpaṃ. Paṭisandhikkhaṇe vatthuṃ . . . pe. . . .
     7. Sahetukañ ca ahetukañ ca dhammaṃ paccayā sahetuko dhammo uppajjati sahajātapaccayā.
     Sahetukaṃ ekaṃ khandhañ ca vatthuñ ca paccayā tayo khandhā; dve . . . pe . . . Vicikicchāsahagataṃ uddhaccasahagataṃ ekaṃ khandhañ ca mohañ ca paccayā tayo khandhā; dve . . . Paṭisandhikkhaṇe . . . pe . . .
     8. Sahetukañ ca ahetukañ ca . . . ahetuko. . . .
     Sahetuke khandhe ca mahābhūte ca paccayā cittasamuṭṭhānaṃ rūpaṃ. Vicikicchāsahagate uddhaccasahagate khandhe ca mohañ ca paccayā cittasamuṭṭhānaṃ rūpaṃ.
Vicikicchāsahagate uddhaccasahagate khandhe ca vatthuñ ca paccayā vicikicchāsahagato uddhaccasahagato moho.
     9. Sahetukañ ca ahetukañ ca dhammaṃ paccayā sahetuko ca ahetuko ca dhammā uppajjanti sahajātapaccayā.


[page 037]
                          Nahetupaccayavāro.                37
     Vicikicchāsahagataṃ uddhaccasahagataṃ ekaṃ khandhañ ca mohañ ca paccayā tayo khandhā cittasamuṭṭhānañ ca rūpaṃ; dve . . . Sahetukaṃ ekaṃ khandhañ ca vatthuñ ca paccayā tayo khandhā moho ca; dve . . . Paṭisandhikkhaṇe sahetukaṃ ekaṃ khandhañ ca vatthuñ ca paccayā . . . pe . . .
     1. Sahetukaṃ dhammaṃ paccayā sahetuko dhammo uppajjati aññamaññapaccayā . . . (saṃkhittaṃ) avigatapaccayā . . .
          Hetuyā nava,                     sabbattha nava,
          ārammaṇe nava,                    avigate nava,
          adhipatiyā nava,
     evaṃ gaṇetabbaṃ.
                          Anulomaṃ niṭṭhitaṃ.
                          [Paccaniyaṃ.]
     2. Sahetukaṃ dhammaṃ paccayā ahetuko dhammo uppajjati nahetupaccayā.
     Vicikicchāsahagate uddhaccasahagate khandhe paccayā vicikicchāsahagato uddhaccasahagato moho.
     4. Ahetukaṃ dhammaṃ paccayā ahetuko dhammo uppajjati nahetupaccayā.
     Ahetukaṃ ekaṃ khandhaṃ . . . pe . . . Paṭisandhikkhaṇe . . . (yāva asaññasattā). Cakkhāyatanaṃ paccāyā cakkhuviññāṇaṃ; kāyāyatanaṃ paccayā kāyaviññāṇaṃ;
vatthuṃ paccayā ahetukā khandha moho ca.
     8. Sahetukañ ca ahetukañ ca . . . ahetuko . . .
     Vicikicchāsahagate uddhaccasahagate khandhe ca vatthuñ ca paccayā vicikicchāsahagato uddhaccasahagato moho .

38                Sahetukadukaṃ.
[... content straddling page break has been moved to the page above ...] . .
(saṃkhittaṃ).
          Nahetuyā tīṇi,                    na kamme cattāri,
          nārammaṇe tīṇi,                navipāke nava,
          nādhipatiyā nava,                nāhāre ekaṃ,
          nānantare tīṇi,                na-indriye ekaṃ,
          nasamanantare tīṇi,           na jhāne ekaṃ,
          na-aññamaññe tīṇi,               namagge ekaṃ,
          [nanissaye tīṇi,3]                nasampayutte tīṇi,
          na-upanissaye tīṇi,               navippayutte cha,
          napurejāte nava,                nonatthiyā tīṇi,
          napacchājāte nava,                novigate tīṇi:--
          nāsevane nava,
     evaṃ gaṇetabbaṃ.
                         Paccaniyaṃ niṭṭhitaṃ.
          Hetupaccayā, nārammaṇe           napacchājāte nava,
          tīṇi,                          nāsevane nava,
          nādhipatiyā nava,                nakamme tīṇi,
          nānantare tīṇi,                navipāke nava,
          nasamanantare tīṇi,               nasampayutte tīṇi,
          na-aññamaññe tīṇi,               navippayutte tīṇi,
          na-upanissaye tīṇi,               nonatthiyā tīṇi,
          napurejāte nava,                novigate tīṇi:--
     evaṃ gaṇetabban.
                     Anulomapaccaniyaṃ niṭṭhitaṃ.
          Nahetupaccayā, ārammaṇe           magge tīṇi,
          tīṇi,                          sampayutte tīṇi,
          anantare tīṇi,                    [vippayutte tīṇi,7]
          (saṃkhittaṃ)                avigate tīṇi:--
          evaṃ gaṇetabbaṃ.
                     Paccaniyānulomaṃ niṭṭhitaṃ.


[page 039]
                          Ārammaṇavāro.                     39
                (Nissayavāro paṭiccavārasadiso.)
                          [Anulomaṃ.]
     1. Sahetukaṃ dhammaṃ saṃsaṭṭho sahetuko dhammo uppajjati hetupaccayā.
     Sahetukaṃ ekaṃ khandhaṃ saṃsaṭṭhā tayo khandhā; dve . . . Paṭisandhikkhaṇe . . . pe . . .
     5. Ahetukaṃ dhammaṃ saṃsaṭṭho sahetuko dhammo uppajjati hetupaccayā.
     Vicikicchāsahagataṃ uddhaccasahagataṃ mohaṃ saṃsaṭṭhā vicikicchāsahagatā uddhaccasahagatā khandhā.
     7. Sahetukañ ca ahetukañ ca dhammaṃ saṃsaṭṭho sahetuko dhammo uppajjati hetupaccayā.
     Vicikicchāsahagataṃ uddhaccasahagataṃ ekaṃ khandhañ ca mohañ ca saṃsaṭṭhā tayo khandhā; dve . . . pe . . .
     1. Sahetukaṃ dhammaṃ saṃsaṭṭho sahetuko dhammo uppajjati ārammaṇapaccayā.
     Sahetukaṃ ekaṃ khandhaṃ saṃsaṭṭhā tayo khandhā; dve . . . pe . . . Paṭisandhikkhaṇe . . . pe . . .
     2. Sahetukaṃ dhammaṃ saṃsaṭṭho ahetuko dhammo uppajjati ārammaṇapaccayā.
     Vicikicchāsahagate uddhaccasahagate khandhe saṃsaṭṭho vicikicchāsahagato uddhaccasahagato moho.
     3. Sahetukaṃ dhammaṃ saṃsaṭṭho sahetuko ca . . .
     Vicikicchāsahagataṃ uddhaccasahagataṃ ekaṃ khandhaṃ saṃsaṭṭhā tayo khandhā moho ca . . . pe . . . dve . . . pe . . .
     4. Ahetukaṃ dhammaṃ saṃsaṭṭho ahetuko . . .
     Ahetukaṃ ekaṃ . . . pe . . .
     5. Ahetukaṃ dhammaṃ saṃsaṭṭho sahetuko . . .
     Vicikicchāsahagataṃ uddhaccasahagataṃ mohaṃ saṃsaṭṭhā vicikicchāsahagatā uddhaccasahagatā khandhā.
     Sahetukañ ca ahetukañ ca dhammaṃ saṃsaṭṭho sahetuko dhammo uppajjati ārammaṇapaccayā.


[page 040]
40                Sahetukadukaṃ.
     Vicikicchāsahagataṃ uddhaccasahagataṃ ekaṃ khandhañ ca mohañ ca saṃsaṭṭhā tayo khandhā; dve . . . pe . . .
     1. Sahetukaṃ dhammaṃ saṃsaṭṭho sahetuko dhammo uppajjati adhipatipaccayā.
     Sahetukaṃ ekaṃ khandhaṃ saṃsaṭṭhā tayo khandhā; dve . . . pe . . .
     Sahetukaṃ dhammaṃ saṃsaṭṭho sahetuko dhammo uppajjati anantarapaccayā . . . samanantarapaccayā . . .
sahajātapaccayā . . . (saṃkhittaṃ) . . . vipākapaccayā.
     Vipākaṃ sahetukaṃ ekaṃ khandhaṃ . . . dve . . . pe . . . Paṭisandhikkhaṇe . . . pe . . .
     4. Ahetukaṃ dhammaṃ saṃsaṭṭho ahetuko dhammo uppajjati vipākapaccayā.
     Vipākaṃ ahetukaṃ ekaṃ khandhaṃ saṃsaṭṭhā tayo khandhā; dve . . . pe . . . paṭisandhikkhaṇe. . . .
pe . . .
. . . jhānapaccayā . . . (saṃkhittaṃ) . . . avigatapaccayā . . .
          Hetuyā tīṇi,                upanissaye cha,
          ārammaṇe cha,                purejāte cha . . . (samkhittaṃ) . . .
          adhipatiyā ekaṃ,
          anantare cha,                vipāke dve,
          samanantare cha,           āhāre cha,
          sahajāte cha,                magge pañca,
          aññamaññe cha,                avigate cha:--
          nissaye cha,
     evaṃ gaṇetabbaṃ.
                          Anulomaṃ niṭṭhitaṃ.
                          [Paccaniyaṃ.]
     2. Sahetukaṃ dhammaṃ saṃsaṭṭho ahetuko dhammo uppajjati nahetupaccayā.
     Vicikicchāsahagate uddhaccasahagate khandhe saṃsaṭṭho vicikicchāsahagato uddhaccasahagato moho.


[page 041]
                     Hetupaccayavāro.                     41
     4. Ahetukaṃ dhammaṃ saṃsaṭṭho ahetuko dhammo uppajjati nahetupaccayā.

                          Vippayuttavāro.                51
     Ahetukā āhārā sampayuttakānaṃ khandhānaṃ cittasamuṭṭhānānañ ca rūpānaṃ āhārapaccayena paccayo. Paṭisandhikkhaṇe kabaḷiṃkāro āhāro imassa kāyassa āhārapaccayena paccayo.
     1. Sahetuko dhammo sahetukassa dhammassa indriyapaccayena paccayo . . . (tīṇi).
     4. Ahetuko dhammo ahetukassa dhammassa . . .
     Ahetukā indriyā sampayuttakānaṃ khandhānaṃ cittasamuṭṭhānānañ ca rūpānaṃ indriyapaccayena paccayo.
Paṭisandhikkhaṇe cakkhundriyaṃ cakkhuviññāṇassa . . .
pe . . . kāyindriyaṃ kāyaviññāṇassa, indriyapaccayena paccayo. Rūpajīvitindriyaṃ kaṭattā rūpānaṃ indriyapaccayena paccayo.
     1. Sahetuko dhammo sahetukassa dhammassa jhānapaccayena paccayo . . . (tīṇi).
     4. Ahetuko dhammo ahetukassa dhammassa . . .
     Ahetukāni jhānaṃgāni sampayuttakānaṃ khandhānaṃ cittasamuṭṭhānānañ ca rūpānaṃ jhānapaccayena paccayo.
Paṭisandhikkhaṇe . . . pe . . .
     1. Sahetuko dhammo sahetukassa dhammassa maggapaccayena paccayo . . . (tīṇi).
     1. Sahetuko dhammo sahetukassa dhammassa sampayuttapaccayena paccayo . . .
     (Paṭiccavāre sampayuttavārasadisaṃ cha pañhā.)
     2. Sahetuko dhammo ahetukassa dhammassa vippayuttapaccayena paccayo.
     Sahajātaṃ, pacchājātaṃ. Sahajātā sahetukā khandhā cittasamuṭṭhānānaṃ rūpānaṃ vippayuttapaccayena paccayo.
Paṭisandhikkhaṇe sahetukā khandhā kaṭattā rūpānaṃ vippayuttapaccayena paccayo. Pacchājātā:-- sahetukā khandhā purejātassa imassa kāyassa vippayuttapaccayena paccayo.


[page 052]
52                               Sahetukadukaṃ.
[... content straddling page break has been moved to the page above ...]
     4. Ahetuko dhammo ahetukassa dhammassa. . . .
     Sahajātaṃ, purejātaṃ, pacchājātaṃ. Sahajātā ahetukā khandhā cittasamuṭṭhānānaṃ rūpānaṃ vippayuttapaccayena paccayo. Paṭisandhikkhaṇe ahetukā khandhā kaṭattā rūpānaṃ vippayuttapaccayena paccayo. Khandhā vatthussa . . . pe . . . vatthu khandhānaṃ vippayuttapaccayena paccayo. Purejātaṃ:-- cakkhāyatanaṃ cakkhuviññāṇassa . . . pe . . . kāyāyatanaṃ kāyaviññāṇassa . . . pe . . .
vatthu ahetukānaṃ khandhānaṃ mohassa ca vippayuttapaccayena paccayo. Pacchājātā ahetukā khandhā ca moho ca purejātassa. . . .
     5. Ahetuko dhammo sahetukassa dhammassa. . . .
     Sahajātaṃ, purejātaṃ. Sahajātaṃ:-- paṭisandhikkhaṇe vatthu sahetukānaṃ khandhānaṃ vippayuttapaccayena paccayo. Purejātaṃ:-- vatthu . . .
     6. Ahetuko dhammo sahetukassa ca ahetukassa. . . .
     Purejātaṃ vatthu vicikicchāsahagatānaṃ uddhaccasahagatānaṃ khandhānaṃ mohassa ca vippayuttapaccayena paccayo.
     8. Sahetuko ca ahetuko ca dhammā ahetukassa. . . .
     Sahajātaṃ, pacchājātaṃ. Sahajātā vicikicchāsahagatā uddhaccasahagatā khandhā ca moho ca cittasamuṭṭhānānaṃ rūpānaṃ vippayuttapaccayena paccayo. Pacchājātā vicikicchāsahagatā . . . moho ca purejātassa imassa kāyassa vippayuttapaccayena paccayo.
     1. Sahetuko dhammo sahetukassa dhammassa atthipaccayena paccayo.
     Sahetuko eko khandho tiṇṇannaṃ khandhānaṃ; dve . . . Paṭisandhikkhaṇe . . . pe . . .
     2. Sahetuko dhammo ahetukassa dhammassa. . . .
     Sahajātaṃ, pacchājātaṃ. Sahajātā sahetukā khandhā cittasamuṭṭhānānaṃ rūpānaṃ atthipaccayena paccayo.


[page 053]
                                   Atthivāro                     53
Vicikicchāsahagatā uddhaccasahagatā khandhā mohassa cittasamuṭṭhānānañ . . . paccayo. Paṭisandhikkhaṇe pacchājātā sahetukā khandhā purejātassa imassa kāyassa atthipaccayena paccayo.
     3. Sahetuko dhammo sahetukassa ca ahetukassa. . . .
     Sahetuko eko khandho tiṇṇannaṃ khandhānaṃ cittasamuṭṭhānānañ . . . paccayo. Vicikicchāsahagato uddhaccasahagato eko khandho tiṇṇannaṃ khandhānaṃ mohassa ca cittasamuṭṭhānānañ ca; dve. . . . Paṭisandhikkhaṇe . . . pe . . .
     4. Ahetuko dhammo ahetukassa dhammassa. . . .
     Sahajātaṃ, purejātaṃ, pacchājātaṃ āhāraṃ indriyaṃ.
Sahajāto ahetuko eko . . . pe . . . dve . . . Paṭisandhikkhaṇe vicikicchāsahagato uddhaccasahagato moho cittasamuṭṭhānānañ ca rūpānaṃ atthipaccayena paccayo . . .
(paṭisandhi yāva asaññasattā kātabbaṃ.) Purejātaṃ:-- cakkhuṃ . . . pe . . . vatthuṃ aniccato . . . pe . . . domanassaṃ uppajjati. Kusalākusale niruddhe ahetuko vipāko tad-ārammaṇatā uppajjati. Rūpāyatanaṃ cakkhuviññāṇassa . . . pe . . . phoṭṭhabbāyatanaṃ kāyaviññāṇassa . . . pe . . . cakkhāyatanaṃ cakkhuviññāṇassa . . . pe . . . kāyāyatanaṃ kāyaviññāṇassa atthipaccayena paccayo. Vatthu ahetukānaṃ khandhānaṃ mohassa ca atthipaccayena paccayo. Pacchājātā ahetukā khandhā ca moho ca purejātassa imassa kāyassa atthipaccayena paccayo. Kabaḷiṃkāro āhāro imassa. . . . Rūpajīvitindriyaṃ kaṭattā rūpānaṃ atthipaccayena paccayo.
     5. Ahetuko dhammo sahetukassa dhammassa . . .
     Sahajātaṃ, purejātaṃ. Sahajāto vicikicchāsahagato uddhaccasahagato moho sampayuttakānaṃ khandhānaṃ atthipaccayena paccayo. Patisandhikkhaṇe vatthu sahetukānaṃ khandhānaṃ atthipaccayena paccayo. Purejātaṃ cakkhuṃ . . . pe . . . vatthuṃ . . . niruddhe sahetuko vipāko tad-ārammaṇatā uppajjati;

54                Sahetukadukaṃ.

     6. Ahetuko dhammo sahetukassa ca ahetukassa. . . .
     Sahajātaṃ . . . khandhānaṃ cittasamuṭṭhānānañ ca rūpānaṃ atthipaccayena paccayo. Purejātaṃ:-- cakkhuṃ . . .
pe . . . vatthuṃ ārabbha vicikicchāsahagatā uddhaccasahagatā khandhā ca moho ca uppajjanti. Vatthu vicikicchāsahagatānaṃ uddhaccasahagatānaṃ khandhānaṃ mohassa ca atthipaccayena paccayo.
     7. Sahetuko ca ahetuko ca dhammā sahetukassa. . . .
     Sahajātaṃ, purejātaṃ. Sahajāto vicikicchāsahagato uddhaccasahagato eko khandho ca moho ca tiṇṇannaṃ khandhānaṃ atthipaccayena paccayo; dve . . . pe . . .
Paṭisandhikkhaṇe sahetuko eko khandho ca vatthu ca tiṇṇannaṃ . . . dve . . . pe . . . Purejāto sahetuko . . . dve . . . pe . . .
     8. Sahetuko ca ahetuko ca dhammā ahetukassa. . . .
     Sahajātaṃ, purejātaṃ, pacchājātaṃ āhāraṃ indriyaṃ.
Sahajātā:-- sahetukā khandhā ca mahābhūtā ca cittasamuṭṭhānānaṃ rūpānaṃ atthipaccayena paccayo. Vicikicchāsahagatā uddhaccasahagatā khandhā ca moho ca cittasamuṭṭhānānaṃ. . . . Paṭisandhikkhaṇe sahetukā khandhā ca mahābhūtā ca kaṭattā rūpānaṃ atthipaccayena paccayo.
Purejātā vicikicchāsahagatā uddhaccasahagatā khandhā ca vatthu ca mohassa atthipaccayena paccayo. Pacchājātā vicikicchāsahagatā uddhaccasahagatā khandhā ca moho ca purejātassa imassa kāyassa atthipaccayena pāccayo. Pacchājātā sahetukā khandhā ca kabaḷiṃkāro āhāro ca imassa kāyassa atthipaccayena paccayo. Pacchājātā sahetukā khandhā ca rūpajīvitindriyañ ca kaṭattā rūpānaṃ atthipaccayena paccayo.
     9. Sahetuko ca ahetuko ca dhammā sahetukassa ca . . .
     Sahajātaṃ . . . khandhānaṃ cittasamuṭṭhānānañ ca rūpānaṃ atthipaccayena paccayo. Purejāto vicikicchāsahagato uddhaccasahagato eko khandho ca vatthu ca tiṇṇannaṃ khandhānaṃ mohassa ca atthipaccayena paccayo;

          Hetuyā cha,                     kamme cattāri,

          nissaye nava,                     vippayutte pañca,
          upanissaye nava,                atthiyā nava,
          purejāte tīṇi,                    natthiyā nava,

          āsevane nava,                     avigate nava:--
     evaṃ gaṇetabbaṃ.

kammapaccayena paccayo.

pacchājāta- . . . āhāra- . . . indriyapaccayena paccayo.

no-avigate nava:-- evaṃ gaṇetabbaṃ.

Lobhaṃ paṭicca moho . . . (cakkaṃ bandhitabbaṃ). Paṭisandhikkhaṇe alobhaṃ paṭicca adoso amoho . . . (cakkaṃ).

Paṭisandhikkhaṇe . . . pe. . . .

[page 061]
                     Arammaṇavāro.                          61
     (Sahajātavāro pi paccayavāro pi nissayavāro pi saṃsaṭṭhavāro pi sampayuttavāro pi paṭiccavārasadisā.)
     1. Hetu ceva sahetuko dhammo hetussa ceva sahetukassa dhammassa hetupaccayena paccayo.
     Alobho adosassa amohassa hetupaccayena paccayo . . .
(paṭiccavārasadisaṃ) . . .
     2. Hetu ceva . . . sahetukassa ceva na ca hetussa . . .
     Hetū sampayuttakānaṃ khandhānaṃ hetupaccayena paccayo. Paṭisandhikkhaṇe . . . pe . . .
     3. Hetu ceva . . . hetussa ceva sahetukassa ca sahetukassa ceva na ca hetussa ca dhammassa hetupaccayena paccayo.
     Alobho adosassa amohassa sampayuttakānañ ca khandhānaṃ hetupaccayena paccayo . . . (vitthāretabbaṃ).
     1. Hetu ceva sahetuko ca hetussa ceva sahetukassa dhammassa ārammaṇapaccayena paccayo.
     Hetuṃ ārabbha hetū uppajjanti.
     2. Hetu ceva.. na ca hetussa . . .
     Hetuṃ ārabbha sahetukā ceva na ca hetū khandhā uppajjanti.
     3. Hetu ceva . . . hetussa ceva sahetukassa ca sahetukassa ceva na ca hetussa . . .
     Hetuṃ arabbha hetū ca sampayuttakā ca khandhā uppajjanti.
     4. Sahetuko ceva na ca hetu dhammo sahetukassa ceva na ca hetussa . . .
     Dānaṃ datvā sīlaṃ uposathakammaṃ taṃ paccavekkhati,
pubbe suciṇṇāni paccavekkhati, jhānā vuṭṭhahitvā jhānaṃ paccavekkhati. Ariyā maggā vuṭṭhahitvā maggaṃ paccavekkhanti, phalaṃ paccavekkhanti, pahīnakilese paccavekkhanti, vikkhambhitakilese paccavekkhanti, pubbe samudāciṇṇe kilese jānanti.


[page 062]
62                          Hetucevasahetukadukaṃ.
[... content straddling page break has been moved to the page above ...] Sahetuke ceva na ca hetū khandhe aniccato . . . pe . . . domanassaṃ uppajjati; cetopariyañāṇena sahetukañ ceva na ca hetu cittasamaṃgissa cittaṃ jānāti; ākāsānañcāyatanaṃ viññāṇañcāyatanassa,
ākiñcaññāyatanaṃ nevasaññānāsaññāyatanassa ārammaṇapaccayena paccayo. Sahetukā ceva na ca hetū khandhā iddhividhañāṇassa cetopariyañāṇassa pubbenivāsānussatiñāṇassa yathākammūpagañāṇassa anāgataṃsañāṇassa ārammaṇapaccayena paccayo.
     5. Sahetuko ceva na ca hetu dhammo hetussa ceva sahetukassa . . .
     Dānaṃ datvā . . . (paṭhamagamanaṃ; ninnānaṃ).
     6. Sahetuko ceva na ca hetu dhammo hetussa ceva sahetukassa ca sahetukassa ceva na ca heṭussa ca . . .
     Dānaṃ datvā . . . (yathā paṭhamagamanaṃ; evaṃ ninnānaṃ).
     7. Hetu ceva sahetuko ca sahetuko ceva na ca hetu ca dhammā hetussa ceva sahetukassa ca . . .
     Hetuñ ca sampayuttake ca khandhe ārabbha hetū uppajjanti.
     8. Hetu ceva . . . dhammā sahetukassa ceva na ca hetussa dhammassa ārammaṇapaccayena paccayo.
     Hetuñ ca sampayuttake ca khandhe ārabbha sahetukā ceva na ca hetu khandhā uppajjanti.
     9. Hetu ceva . . . dhammā hetussa ceva sahetukassa ca sahetukassa ceva na ca hetussa ca dhammassa ārammaṇapaccayena paccayo.
     Hetuñ ca sampayuttake ca khandhe ārabbha hetū ca sampayuttakā ca khandhā uppajjanti.
     1. Hetu ceva sahetuko dhammo hetussa ceva sahetukassa dhammassa adhipatipaccayena paccayo.
     Ārammaṇādhipati, sahajātādhipati. Ārammaṇādhipati:


[page 063]
                          Adhipativāro.                     63
[... content straddling page break has been moved to the page above ...]-- hetuṃ garuṃ katvā hetū uppajjanti. Sahajātādhipati:-- hetu ceva sahetukādhipati sampayuttakānaṃ hetūnaṃ adhipatipaccayena paccayo.
     2. Hetu ceva . . . sahetukassa ceva na ca hetussa . . .
     Ārammaṇādhipati . . . katvā sahetukā ceva na ca hetū khandhā uppajjanti. Sahajātādhipati:-- hetu ceva sahetukādhipati sampayuttakānaṃ khandhānaṃ adhipatipaccayena paccayo.
     3. Hetu ceva . . . hetussa ceva sahetukassa ca sahetukassa ceva na ca hetussa ca . . .
     Ārammaṇādhipati . . . katvā hetū ca sampayuttakā ca khandhā uppajjanti. Sahajātādhipati:-- hetu ceva . . .
khandhānaṃ hetūnañ ca adhipatipaccayena paccayo.
     4. Sahetuko ceva na ca hetu . . . na ca hetussa . . .
     Ārammaṇādhipati . . . dānaṃ datvā sīlaṃ uposathākammaṃ katvā, taṃ garuṃ katvā paccavekkhati, pubbe . . .
pe . . . jhānā . . . pe . . . Ariyā maggā vuṭṭhahitvā maggaṃ garuṃ katvā . . . pe . . . phalaṃ garuṃ katvā paccavekkhanti. Sahetuke ceva na ca hetū khandhe garuṃ katvā assādeti abhinandati, taṃ garuṃ katvā rāgo uppajjati, diṭṭhi uppajjati. Sahajātādhipati:-- sahetuko ceva na ca hetu adhipati sampayuttakānaṃ khandhānaṃ adhipatipaccayena paccayo.
     5. Sahetuko ceva na ca hetu sahetukassa . . .
     Ārammaṇādhipati, sahajātādhipati. Ārammaṇādhipati:


[page 064]
64                          Hetucevasahetukadukaṃ.
--dānaṃ datvā . . . (paṭhamagamanaṃ yeva). Sahajātādhipati:-- . . . sampayuttakānaṃ hetūnaṃ adhipatipaccayena paccayo.
     6. Sahetuko ceva na ca hetu dhammo hetussa ceva sahetukassa ca sahetukassa ceva na ca hetussa ca . . .
     Ārammaṇādhipati . . . dānaṃ datvā . . . (paṭhamagamanaṃ yeva). Sahajātādhipati:-- sahetuko . . . khandhānaṃ hetūnañ ca adhipatipaccayena paccayo.
     7. Hetu ceva sahetuko ca sahetuko ceva na ca hetu ca dhammā hetussa ceva sahetukassa dhammassa adhipatipaccayena paccayo.
     Ārammaṇādhipati:-- hetuñ ca sampayuttake ca khandhe garuṃ katvā hetū uppajjanti.
     8. Hetu ceva . . . sahetukassa ceva na ca hetussa . . .
     Ārammaṇādhipati:-- hetuñ ca . . . katvā sahetukā ceva na ca hetū khandhā uppajjanti.
     9. Hetu ceva . . . hetussa ceva sahetukassa ca sahetukassa ceva na ca hetussa ca dhammassa adhipatipaccayena paccayo.
     Ārammaṇādhipati:-- hetuñ ca . . . hetū ca sampayuttakā ca khandhā uppajjanti.
     1. Hetu ceva sahetuko . . . sahetukassa dhammassa anantarapaccayena paccayo.
     Purimā purimā hetū pacchimānaṃ pacchimānaṃ hetūnaṃ anantarapaccayena paccayo.
     2. Hetu ceva sahetuko . . . na ca hetussa . . .
     Purimā . . . pacchimānaṃ sahetukānañ ceva na ca hetūnaṃ khandhānaṃ anantarapaccayena paccayo.
     3. Hetu ceva sahetuko . . . sahetukassa ca sahetukassa ceva na ca hetussa . . .


[page 065]
                          Anantaravāro.                     65
     Purimā . . . hetūnaṃ sampayuttakānañ ca khandhānaṃ anantarapaccayena paccayo.
     4. Sahetuko ceva na ca hetu . . .
     Purimā purimā sahetukā ceva na ca hetū khandhā pacchimānaṃ . . . Anulomaṃ gotrabhussa anulomaṃ vodānassa . . . (saṅkhittaṃ). Nirodhā vuṭṭhahantassa nevasaññānāsaññāyatanaṃ phalasamāpattiyā anantarapaccayena paccayo.
     5. Sahetuko ceva na ca hetu dhammo hetussa ceva sahetukassa . . .
     Purimā purimā sahetukā ceva na ca hetū khandhā pacchimānaṃ . . . Anulomaṃ gotrabhussa . . . (saṃkhittaṃ).
     6. Sahetuko ceva na ca hetu ca . . . sahetukassa ceva na ca hetussa ca . . .
     Purimā . . . pacchimānaṃ hetūnaṃ sampayuttakānañ ca khandhānaṃ anantarapaccayena paccayo. Anulomaṃ gotrabhussa . . . pe . . . (sahetuko ceva na ca hetumūlakaṃ, tīṇi pi ekasadisā).
     7. Hetu ceva sahetuko ca sahetuko ceva na ca hetu ca dhammā hetussa ceva sahetukassa dhammassa anantarapaccayena paccayo.
     Purimā purimā hetū ca sampayuttakā ca khandhā pacchimānaṃ pacchimānaṃ hetūnaṃ anantarapaccayena paccayo.
     8. Hetu ceva . . . sahetukassa ceva na ca hetussa . . .
     Purimā . . . pacchimānaṃ sahetukānañ ceva na ca hetūnaṃ khandhānaṃ anantarapaccayena paccayo.
     9. Hetu ceva . . . hetussa ceva sahetukassa ca sahetukassa ceva na ca hetussa ca dhammassa anantarapaccayena paccayo.
     Purimā . . . hetūnaṃ sampayuttakānañ ca khandhānaṃ anantarapaccayena paccayo.
     1. Hetu ceva . . . sahetuko dhammo uppajjati sahajātapaccayena paccayo .


[page 066]
66                          Hetucevasahetukadukaṃ.
[... content straddling page break has been moved to the page above ...] . . aññamaññapaccayena paccayo . . . nissayapaccayena paccayo . . . (tīṇi pi paccayā paṭiccavāre hetusadisā) . . . upanissayapaccayena paccayo.
     Ārammaṇūpanissayo, anantarūpanissayo, pakatūpanissayo . . . pe . . . Pakatūpanissayo:-- hetū hetūnaṃ upanissayapaccayena paccayo. Hetū sahetukānañ ceva na ca hetūnaṃ khandhānaṃ upanissayapaccayena paccayo.
Hetū hetūnaṃ sampayuttakānañ ceva khandhānaṃ upanissayapaccayena paccayo. (Imesaṃ dvinnam pi pañhānaṃ mūlāni pucchitabbāni.)
     4. Sahetuko ceva na ca hetu . . .
     Ārammaṇūpanissayo . . . pe . . . Pakatūpanissayo:-- saddhaṃ upanissāya dānaṃ deti . . . pe . . . samāpattiṃ uppādeti . . . pe . . . mānaṃ jappeti, . . . pe . . . diṭṭhiṃ gaṇhāti. Sīlaṃ . . . pe . . . patthanaṃ upanissāya dānaṃ deti, . . . pe . . . saṃghaṃ bhindati. Saddhā . . . pe . . .
patthanā saddhāya . . . pe . . . patthanāya upanissayapaccayena paccayo. (Sahetuko ceva na ca hetu-mūlakaṃ iminā kāraṇena vitthāretabbaṃ3; avasesā dve pañhā.)
     7. Hetu ceva sahetuko ca sahetuko ceva na ca hetu ca dhammā hetussa ceva sahetukassa . . .
     Ārammaṇūpanissayo . . . pe . . . Pakatūpanissayo:-- hetū ca sampayuttakā ca khandhā hetūnaṃ upanissayapaccayena paccayo . . . (mūlaṃ pucchitabbaṃ).
     Hetū ca sampayuttakā ca khandhā hetūnaṃ sampayuttakānañ ca khandhānaṃ upanissayapaccayena paccayo.
     1. Hetu ceva sahetuko . . . āsevanapaccayena paccayo . . . (anantarasadisaṃ).
     4. Sahetuko ceva na ca hetu . . . kammapaccayena paccayo.
     Sahajātā, nānākhaṇikā. Sahajātā:-- sahetukā ceva na ca hetū cetanā sampayuttakānaṃ khandhānaṃ kammapaccayena paccayo. Nānākhaṇikā:-- sahetukā ceva na ca hetū cetanā vipākānaṃ sahetukānaṃ ceva na ca hetūnaṃ khandhānaṃ kammapaccayena paccayo.


[page 067]
                                    Anulomaṃ.           67
[... content straddling page break has been moved to the page above ...]
     5. Sahetuko ceva na ca hetu . . . sahetukassa dhammassa kammapaccayena paccayo.
     Sahajātā, nānākhanikā. Sahajātā:-- sahetukā . . .
sampayuttakānaṃ hetūnaṃ kammapaccayena paccayo.
Nānākhaṇikā:-- sahetukā . . . vipākānaṃ hetūnaṃ kammapaccayena paccayo.
     6. Sahetuko ceva . . . na ca hetussa ca . . .
     Sahajātā, nānākhaṇikā. Sahajātā:-- sahetukā . . .
khandhānaṃ hetūnañ ca kammapaccayena paccayo.
Nānākhaṇikā . . . vipākānaṃ khandhānaṃ hetūnañ ca kammapaccayena paccayo.
     1. Hetu ceva . . . vipākapaccayena paccayo.
     Vipāko alobho adosassa amohassa vipākapaccayena paccayo. (Paṭisandhikkhaṇe alobho yathā hetupaccayā evaṃ vitthāretabbaṃ. Nava pi vipākan ti niyāmetabbaṃ.)
     4. Sahetuko ceva na ca hetu . . . āhārapaccayena paccayo . . . (tīṇi).
     1. Hetu ceva . . . indriyapaccayena paccayo . . .
(indriyan ti niyāmetabbaṃ. Paripuṇṇaṃ).
     4. Sahetuko ceva na ca hetu . . . jhānapaccayena paccayo . . . (tīṇi).
     1. Hetu ceva . . . maggapaccayena paccayo . . . pe . . .
sampayutta- . . . atthi- . . . natthi- . . . vigata- . . .
avigatapaccayena paccayo.

          ārammaṇe nava,                    nissaye nava,

     1. Hetu ceva sahetuko dhammo hetussa ceva . . .

     1. Nahetu-sahetukaṃ dhammaṃ paṭicca nahetu-sahetuko dhammo uppajjati hetupaccayā.

     3. Nahetu-sahetukaṃ . . . nahetu-sahetuko ca nahetuahetuko ca . . .
     Nahetu-sahetukaṃ . . . (cf. 1) khandhā cittasamuṭṭhānañ ca rūpaṃ, . . . pe . . . dve . . . pe . . . Paṭisandhikkhaṇe . . . pe . . .
     4. Nahetu-ahetukaṃ . . . nahetu-ahetuko. . . .
     Ekaṃ mahābhūtaṃ paṭicca tayo mahābhūtā . . . pe . . .
mahābhūte paṭicca cittasamuṭṭhānaṃ rūpaṃ, kaṭattā rūpaṃ upādā rūpaṃ.
     5. Nahetu-ahetukaṃ . . . nahetu-sahetuko. . . .
     Paṭisandhikkhaṇe vatthuṃ paṭicca nahetu-sahetukā khandhā.
     6. Nahetu-ahetukaṃ . . . nahetu-ahetuko ca. . . .
     Paṭisandhikkhaṇe vatthuṃ paṭicca nahetu-sahetukā khandhā; mahābhūte paṭicca kaṭattā rūpaṃ upādā rūpaṃ.

     Paṭisandhikkhaṇe nahetu-sahetukaṃ ekaṃ khandhañ ca vatthuñ ca paṭicca tayo khandhā .

72                          Nahetusahetukadukaṃ.

     Nahetu-sahetuke khandhe paṭicca cittasamuṭṭhānaṃ rūpaṃ.

          Nahetuyā ekaṃ,                    na-upanissaye tīṇi,

Cakkhuṃ . . . pe . . . vatthuṃ . . . nahetu-ahetuke khandhe aniccato . . . pe . . . domanassaṃ uppajjati.
Kusalākusale niruddhe nahetu-sahetuko vipāko tad-ārammaṇatā uppajjati; dibbena cakkhunā rūpaṃ passati; dibbāya sotadhātuyā saddaṃ suṇāti, cetopariyañāṇena nahetuahetuka-cittasamaṃgissa cittaṃ jānāti; nahetu-ahetukā khandhā iddhividhañāṇassa cetopariyañāṇassa pubbe nivāsānussatiñāṇassa yathākammūpagañāṇassa anāgataṃsañāṇassa ārammaṇapaccayena paccayo. Nahetu-ahetuke khandhe ārabbha nahetu-sahetukā khandhā uppajjanti.
     1. Nahetu-sahetuko . . . adhipatipaccayena paccayo.
     Ārammaṇādhipati, sahajātādhipati. Ārammaṇādhipati:
-- dānaṃ datvā sīlaṃ samādiyitvā uposathakammaṃ karitvā taṃ garuṃ katvā paccavekkhati, pubbe suciṇṇāni paccavekkhati, jhānā vuṭṭhahitvā jhānaṃ garuṃ katvā paccavekkhati. Ariyā maggā vuṭṭhahitvā maggaṃ garuṃ katvā paccavekkhanti, phalaṃ garuṃ katvā paccavekkhanti.
Nahetu-sahetuke khandhe garuṃ katvā assādeti abhinandati taṃ garuṃ katvā rāgo uppajjati . . . pe . . . diṭṭhi uppajjati. Sahajātādhipati:-- nahetu-sahetukādhipati sampayuttakānaṃ khandhānaṃ adhipatipaccayena paccayo.
     2. Nahetu-sahetuko . . . nahetu-ahetukassa. . . .
     Sahajātādhipati:-- nahetu-sahetukādhipati cittasamuṭṭhānaṃ rūpānaṃ adhipatipaccayena paccayo.
     3. Nahetu-sahetuko . . . nahetu-sahetukassa ca nahetuahetukassa ca. . . .

     5. Nahetu-ahetuko . . . nahetu-sahetukassa. . . .
     Ārammaṇādhipati:-- ariyā nibbānaṃ garuṃ katvā paccavekkhanti, nibbānaṃ gotrabhussa vodānassa maggassa phalassa adhipatipaccayena paccayo. Cakkhuṃ . . . pe

     1. Nahetu-sahetuko dhammo nahetu-sahetukassa dhammassa kammapaccayena paccayo.

     2. Nahetu-sahetuko . . . nahetu-ahetukassa. . . .
     Sahajātā, nānākhaṇikā. Sahajātā:-- nahetu-sahetukā cetanā cittasamuṭṭhānānaṃ rūpānaṃ kammapaccayena paccayo. Nānākhaṇikā:-- nahetu-sahetukā cetanā vipākānaṃ nahetu-ahetukānaṃ khandhānaṃ kaṭattā ca rūpānaṃ kammapaccayena paccayo.
     3. Nahetu-sahetuko . . . nahetu-sahetukassa ca . . .

nahetu-sahetukānaṃ khandhānaṃ. . . .

     Nahetu-sahetuko eko khandho tiṇṇannaṃ . . . pe . . .
Paṭisandhikkhaṇe . . . pe . . .
     2. Nahetu-sahetuko . . . nahetu-ahetukassa . . .
     Sahajātaṃ, pacchajātaṃ . . . pe . . .
     3. Nahetu-sahetuko . . . nahetu-sahetukassa ca . . .
     Nahetu-sahetuko eko khandho tiṇṇannaṃ khandhānaṃ cittasamuṭṭhānānañ ca rūpānaṃ atthipaccayena paccayo.
Paṭisandhikkhaṇe . . . pe . . .
     4. Nahetu-ahetuko . . . nahetu-ahetukassa . . .
     Sahajātaṃ, purejātaṃ, pacchājātaṃ āhāraṃ indriyaṃ.
Sahajāto nahetu-ahetuko eko khandho . . . (yāva asaññasattā). Purejātaṃ:-- cakkhuṃ, vatthuṃ aniccato . . .
pe . . . domanassaṃ uppajjati; rūpāyatanaṃ cakkhuviññāṇassa . . . phoṭṭhabbāyatanaṃ kāyaviññāṇassa, cakkhāyatanaṃ cakkhuviññāṇassa . . . kāyāyatanaṃ kayaviññāṇassa, vatthu nahetu-ahetukānaṃ khandhānaṃ atthipaccayena paccayo. Pacchājātā nahetu-ahetukā khandhā purejātassa imassa kāyassa, kabaḷiṃkāro āhāro imassa kāyassa, rūpājīvitindriyaṃ kaṭattā rūpānaṃ atthipaccayena paccayo.
     5. Nahetu-ahetuko . . . nahetu-sahetukassa . . .
     Sahajātaṃ, purejātaṃ. Sahajātaṃ:-- paṭisandhikkhaṇe vatthu nahetu-sahetukānaṃ khandhānaṃ atthipaccayena paccayo. Purejātaṃ:-- cakkhuṃ . . . pe . . . uppajjati.
Kusalākusale niruddhe nahetu-sahetuko vipāko tad-ārammaṇatā uppajjati.
     7. Nahetu-sahetuko ca nahetu-ahetuko ca . . .


[page 083]
                          Paccaniyaṃ.                          83
     Sahajātaṃ, purejātaṃ. Sahājāto nahetu-sahetuko eko khandho ca vatthu ca tiṇṇannaṃ khandhānaṃ . . . pe . . .
Paṭisandhikkhaṇe nahetu-sahetuko eko khandho ca vatthuñ ca tiṇṇannaṃ . . . pe . . .
     8. Nahetu-sahetuko ca . . . nahetu-ahetukassa . . .
     Sahajātaṃ, pacchājātaṃ āhāraṃ indriyaṃ. Sahajātā nahetu-sahetukā khandhā ca mahābhūtā ca cittasamuṭṭhānānaṃ rūpānaṃ atthipaccayena paccayo. Pacchājātā nahetu-sahetukā khandhā ca kabaḷiṃkāro āhāro ca imassa kāyassa atthipaccayena paccayo. Pacchājātā nahetu-sahetukā khandhā ca rūpajīvitindriyañ ca kaṭattā rūpānaṃ atthipaccayena paccayo.
          Ārammaṇe cattāri,                vipāke cattāri,
          adhipatiyā cattāri,               āhāre cattāri,
          anantare cattāri,                indriye cattāri,
          samanantare cattāri,           jhāne cattāri,
          sahajāte satta,                magge tīṇi,
          aññamaññe cha,                    sampayutte dve,
          nissaye satta,                    vippayutte tīṇi,
          upanissaye cattāri,               atthiyā satta,
          purejāte dve,                     natthiyā cattāri,
          pacchājāte dve,                vigate cattāri,
          āsevane dve,                     avigate satta:--
          kamme cattāri,
     evaṃ gaṇetabbaṃ.
                               Anulomaṃ niṭṭhitaṃ.
                               [Paccaniyaṃ.]
     1. Nahetu-sahetuko dhammo nahetu-sahetukassa dhammassa ārammaṇapaccayena paccayo . . . sahajāta-, upanissaya-, kammapaccayena paccayo.
     2. Nahetu-sahetuko dhammo . . . ārammaṇa-, sahajāta-, upanissaya-, pacchājāta-, kammapaccayena paccayo.
     3. Nahetu-sahetuko . . . nahetu-sahetukassa ca . . .
sahajāta-, kammapaccayena paccayo.
     4. Nahetu-ahetuko . . . ārammaṇa-sahajāta-, upanissaya-, purejāta-, pacchājāta-, āhāra-, indriyapaccayena paccayo.
--------------------------------------------------------------------------

84                          Nahetusahetukadukaṃ.
     5. Nahetu-ahetuko . . . nahetu-sahetukassa . . . ārammaṇa-sahajāta-, upanissaya-, purejātapaccayena paccayo.
     7. Nahetu-sahetuko ca . . . nahetu-sahetukassa dhammassa sahajāta-, purejātapaccayena paccayo.
     8. Nahetu-sahetuko ca . . . nahetu-ahetukassa . . .
sahajāta-, pacchājātā-, āhāra-, indriyapaccayena paccayo.
          Nahetuyā satta,                sabbattha satta;
          nārammaṇe satta . . .           nasampayutte cha,
           (saṃkhittaṃ) . . .           navippayutte pañca,
          sabbattha satta;                no-atthiyā pañca,
          nasahajāte cha,                nonatthiyā satta,
          na-aññamaññe cha,                novigate satta,
          nanissaye cha,                    no-avigate pañca:--
     evaṃ gaṇetabbaṃ.
                          Paccaniyaṃ niṭṭhitaṃ.
          Ārammaṇapaccayā, nādhi-           nonatthiyā cattāri,

          nānantare cattāri,                no-avigate cattāri:--
          sabbattha cattāri;
     evaṃ gaṇetabbaṃ.
                          Anulomapaccaniyaṃ niṭṭhitaṃ.
     Nahetupaccayā, ārammaṇe cattāri, adhipatiyā cattāri,
avigate satta:-- evaṃ gaṇetabbaṃ.

     1. Sappaccayaṃ dhammaṃ paṭicca sappaccayo dhammo uppajjati hetupaccayā.

Paṭisandhikkhaṇe khandhe paṭicca vatthu, vatthuṃ paṭicca khandhā, ekaṃ mahābhūtaṃ . . . pe . . . mahābhūte paṭicca cittasamuṭṭhānaṃ rūpaṃ kaṭattā rūpaṃ upādā rūpaṃ.

avigate ekaṃ.

     1. Sappaccayo dhammo sappaccayassa dhammassa hetupaccayena paccayo.
     Sappaccayā hetū sampayuttakānaṃ khandhānaṃ cittasamuṭṭhānānañ ca rūpānaṃ hetupaccayena paccayo. Paṭisandhikkhaṇe . . . pe . . .
     1. Sappaccayo dhammo sappaccayassa dhammassa ārammaṇapaccayena paccayo.
     Dānaṃ datvā, sīlaṃ . . . uposathakammaṃ . . . taṃ paccavekkhati, pubbe suciṇṇāni paccavekkhati, jhānā vuṭṭhahitvā jhānaṃ paccavekkhati. Ariyā maggā vuṭṭhahitvā maggaṃ paccavekkhanti, phalaṃ paccavekkhanti, pahīnakilese vikkhambhitakilese paccavekkhanti,

                          Adhipativāro                          87

Cakkhuṃ . . . pe . . . vatthuṃ sappaccaye khandhe aniccato . . . pe . . . domanassaṃ uppajjati; dibbena cakkhunā rūpaṃ passati, dibbāya sotadhātuyā saddaṃ suṇāti, cetopariyañāṇena sappaccayacittasamaṃgissa cittaṃ jānāti; ākāsānañcāyatanaṃ viññāṇañcāyatanassa, ākiñcaññāyatanaṃ nevasaññānāsaññāyatanassa,
rūpāyatanaṃ cakkhuviññāṇassa . . . pe . . . phoṭṭhabbāyatanaṃ kāyaviññāṇassa sappaccayā khandhā iddhividhañāṇassa cetopariyañāṇassa pubbenivāsānussatiñāṇassa yathākammūpagañāṇassa anāgataṃsañāṇassa āvajjanāya ārammaṇapaccayena paccayo.
     5. Appaccayo dhammo sappaccayassa dhammassa ārammaṇapaccayena paccayo.
     Ariyā nibbānaṃ paccavekkhanti, nibbānaṃ gotrabhussa vodānassa maggassa phalassa āvajjanāya ārammaṇapaccayena paccayo.
     1. Sappaccayo dhammo sappaccayassa dhammassa adhipatipaccayena paccayo.
     Ārammaṇādhipati, sahajātādhipati. Ārammaṇādhipati:-- dānaṃ datvā sīlaṃ uposathakammaṃ taṃ garuṃ katvā paccavekkhati, pubbe . . . pe . . . jhānaṃ . . . pe . . . Ariyā maggā vuṭṭhahitvā maggaṃ garuṃ katvā paccavekkhanti,
phalaṃ garuṃ . . . pe . . . Cakkhuṃ . . . pe . . . vatthuṃ sappaccaye khandhe garuṃ katvā assādeti abhinandati, taṃ garuṃ katvā rāgo uppajjati, diṭṭhi uppajjati. Sahajātādhipati:-- sappaccayādhipati sampayuttakānaṃ khandhānaṃ cittasamuṭṭhānānañ ca rūpānaṃ adhipatipaccayena paccayo.
     5. Appaccayo dhammo sappaccayassa . . .
     Ārammaṇādhipati:-- ariyā nibbānaṃ garuṃ katvā paccavekkhanti, nibbānaṃ gotrabhussa vodānassa maggassa phalassa adhipatipaccayena paccayo.
     1. Sappaccayo dhammo sappaccayassa dhammassa anantarapaccayena paccayo . . . (saṃkhittaṃ) . . . upanissayapaccayena paccayo .

                                    90
                                    [VIII.
                               SAṂKHATA-DUKAṂ.]
     1. Saṃkhataṃ dhammaṃ paṭicca saṃkhato dhammo uppajjati hetupaccayā.
     Saṃkhataṃ ekaṃ khandhaṃ paṭicca tayo khandhā cittasamuṭṭhānañ ca rūpaṃ. Paṭisandhikkhaṇe khandhe paṭicca vatthu, vatthuṃ paṭicca khandhā; ekaṃ mahābhūtaṃ . . .
pe . . . mahābhūte paṭicca cittasamuṭṭhānaṃ rūpaṃ kaṭattā rūpaṃ upādā rūpaṃ. (Imaṃ dukaṃ yathā Sappaccayadukaṃ evaṃ kātabbaṃ; ninnānākaraṇaṃ.)
                          SAṂKHATA-DUKAṂ niṭṭhitaṃ.

                                    91
                                    [IX.
                               SANIDASSANA-DUKAṂ.]
     4. Anidassanaṃ dhammaṃ paṭicca anidassano dhammo uppajjati hetupaccayā.
     Anidassanaṃ ekaṃ khandhaṃ paṭicca tayo khandhā anidassanaṃ cittasamuṭṭhānañ ca rūpaṃ; dve . . . Paṭisandhikkhaṇe anidassanaṃ ekaṃ khandhaṃ paṭicca tayo khandhā anidassanaṃ kaṭattā ca rūpaṃ . . . dve . . .
khandhe paṭicca vatthu, vatthuṃ paṭicca khandhā; ekaṃ mahābhūtaṃ . . . pe . . . mahābhūte paṭicca anidassanaṃ cittasamuṭṭhānaṃ rūpaṃ kaṭattā rūpaṃ upādā rūpaṃ.
     5. Anidassanaṃ dhammaṃ paṭicca sanidassano . . .
dhammo uppajjati hetupaccayā.
     Anidassane khandhe paṭicca sanidassanaṃ cittasamuṭṭhānaṃ rūpaṃ. Paṭisandhikkhaṇe mahābhūte paṭicca sanidassanaṃ cittasamuṭṭhānaṃ rūpaṃ kaṭattā rūpaṃ upādā rūpaṃ.
     6. Anidassanaṃ dhammaṃ paṭicca sanidassano ca anidassano ca dhammā uppajjanti hetupaccayā.
     Anidassanaṃ ekaṃ khandhaṃ paṭicca tayo khandhā.
Sanidassanañ ca anidassanañ ca cittasamuṭṭhānañ ca rūpaṃ; dve . . . pe . . . Paṭisandhikkhaṇe mahābhūte paṭicca sanidassanañ ca anidassanañ ca cittasamuṭṭhānaṃ rūpaṃ kaṭattā rūpaṃ upādā rūpaṃ.
     4. Anidassanaṃ dhammaṃ paṭicca anidassano dhammo uppajjati ārammaṇapaccayā.


[page 092]
92                               Sanidassanadukaṃ.
     Anidassanaṃ ekaṃ khandhaṃ paṭicca tayo khandhā;
dve . . . Paṭisandhikkhaṇe khandhe paṭicca vatthu,
vatthuṃ paṭicca khandhā.
     4. Anidassanaṃ dhammaṃ paṭicca anidassano dhammo uppajjati adhipatipaccayā.
