ekaṃ mahābhūtaṃ paṭicca tayo mahābhūtā; dve . . . pe . . . mahābhūte paṭicca anidassanaṃ cittasamuṭṭhānaṃ rūpaṃ upādā rūpaṃ.
     5. Anidassanaṃ dhammaṃ paṭicca sanidassano . . .
     Anidassane khandhe paṭicca sanidassanaṃ cittasamuṭṭhānaṃ rūpaṃ, mahābhūte paṭicca sanidassanaṃ cittasamuṭṭhānaṃ rūpaṃ upādā rūpaṃ.
     6. Anidassanaṃ . . . sanidassano ca anidassano ca . . .
     Anidassanaṃ ekaṃ khandhaṃ paṭicca tayo khandhā sanidassanañ ca anidassanañ ca cittasamuṭṭhānaṃ rūpaṃ; dve . . . pe . . .; mahābhūte paṭicca sanidassanañ ca anidassanañ ca cittasamuṭṭhānaṃ rūpaṃ upādā rūpaṃ . . .
(saṃkhittaṃ sabbe kātabbā).
          Hetuyā tīṇi,                     Kamme tīṇi,
          ārammaṇe ekaṃ,                    vipāke tīṇi,
          adhipatiyā tīṇi,                sabbattha tīṇi;
          anantare ekaṃ,                    magge tīṇi,
          samanantare ekaṃ,                sampayutte ekaṃ,
          sahajāte tīṇi,                    vippayutte tīṇi,
          aññamaññe ekaṃ,                atthiyā tīṇi,
          nissaye tīṇi,                     natthiyā ekaṃ,
          upanissaye ekaṃ,                vigate ekaṃ,
          purejāte ekaṃ,                    avigate tīṇi:--
          āsevane ekaṃ,
     evaṃ gaṇetabbaṃ.
                          Anulomaṃ niṭṭhitaṃ.
     4. Anidassanaṃ dhammaṃ paṭicca anidassano dhammo uppajjati nahetupaccayā.


[page 093]
                          Paccaniyaṃ                              93
     Ahetukaṃ anidassanaṃ ekaṃ khandhaṃ paṭicca tayo khandhā, anidassanaṃ cittasamuṭṭhānañ ca rūpaṃ; dve . . . pe . . . Ahetuka paṭisandhikkhaṇe khandhe paṭicca vatthu, vatthuṃ paṭicca khandhā; ekaṃ mahābhūtaṃ . . .
pe . . . mahābhūte paṭicca anidassanaṃ cittasamuṭṭhānaṃ rūpaṃ katattā rūpaṃ upādā rūpaṃ. Bāhiraṃ āhārasamuṭṭhānaṃ utusamuṭṭhānaṃ asaññasattānaṃ. Vicikicchāsahagate uddhaccasahagate khandhe paṭicca vicikicchāsahagato uddhaccasahagato moho.
     5. Anidassanaṃ . . . sanidassano . . . nahetupaccayā.
     Ahetuke anidassane khandhe paṭicca sanidassanaṃ cittasamuṭṭhānaṃ rūpaṃ. Paṭisandhikkhaṇe mahābhūte paṭicca sanidassanaṃ cittasamuṭṭhānaṃ rūpaṃ kaṭattā rūpaṃ upādā rūpaṃ . . . Bāhiraṃ āhārasamuṭṭhānaṃ utusamuṭṭhānaṃ asaññasattānaṃ . . . pe . . . mahābhūte paṭicca sanidassanaṃ cittasamuṭṭhānaṃ rūpaṃ kaṭattā rūpaṃ upādā rūpaṃ.
     6. Anidassanaṃ . . . sanidassano ca anidassano . . .
     Ahetukaṃ anidassanaṃ ekaṃ khandhaṃ paṭicca sanidassanañ ca anidassanañ ca cittasamuṭṭhānaṃ rūpaṃ . . . dve . . .
Paṭisandhikkhaṇe mahābhūte paṭicca . . . pe . . . Bāhiraṃ āhārasamuṭṭhānaṃ utusamuṭṭhānaṃ asaññasattānaṃ . . . pe . . . mahābhūte paṭicca sanidassanañ ca anidassanañ ca katattā rūpaṃ upādā rūpaṃ . . . (evaṃ sabbe kātabbā).
          Nahetuyā tīṇi,                    navipāke tīṇi.
          nārammaṇe tīṇi,                nāhāre tīṇi,
          nadhipatiyā tīṇi,                na-indriye tīṇi,
          nānantare tīṇi,                najhāne tīṇi,
          nasamanantare tīṇi,               namagge tīṇi,
          na-aññamaññe tīṇi,                nasampayutte tīṇi,
          na-upanissaye tīṇi,               navippayutte tīṇi,
          napurejāte tīṇi,                nonatthiyā tīṇi,
          napacchājāte tīṇi,                novigate tīṇi.
          nakamme tīṇi.
                              Paccaniyaṃ niṭṭhitaṃ.

94                          Sanidassanadukaṃ.

     2. Sanidassano dhammo anidassanassa dhammassa ārammaṇapaccayena paccayo.
     Sanidassane rūpe aniccato . . . pe . . . domanassaṃ uppajjati; dibbena cakkhunā . . . pe . . . rūpāyatanaṃ cakkhuviññāṇassa ārammaṇapaccayena paccayo. Sanidassanā khandhā ca iddhividhañāṇassa pubbenivāsānussatiñāṇassa yathakammūpagañāṇassa anāgataṃsañāṇassa āvajjanāya ārammaṇapaccayena paccayo.
     4. Anidassano dhammo anidassanassa . . .
     Dānaṃ, sīlaṃ, uposathakammaṃ taṃ paccavekkhati, pubbe suciṇṇāni paccavekkhati, jhānā vuṭṭhahitvā jhānaṃ paccavekkhati. Ariyā maggā vuṭṭhahitvā maggaṃ paccavekkhanti, phalaṃ paccavekkhanti, nibbānaṃ paccavekkhanti. Nibbānaṃ gotrabhussa vodānassa maggassa phalassa āvajjanāya ārammaṇapaccayena paccayo. Ariyā pahīnakilese paccavekkhanti vikkhambhitakilese . . . pe . . .
Pubbe cakkhuṃ . . . pe . . . kāyaṃ vatthuṃ anidassane khandhe aniccato . . . pe . . . domanassaṃ uppajjati;

                          Anantaravāro.                          97
dibbāya sotadhātuyā saddaṃ suṇāti, cetopariyañāṇena anidassanacittasamaṃgissa cittaṃ jānāti, ākāsānañcāyatanaṃ viññāṇañcāyatanassa ākiñcaññāyatanaṃ nevasaññānāsaññāyatanassa saddāyatanaṃ sotaviññāṇassa . . . pe . . .
phoṭṭhabbāyatanaṃ kāyaviññāṇassa, anidassanā khandhā iddhividhañāṇassa cetopariyañāṇassa pubbenivāsānussatiñāṇassa yathākammūpagañāṇassa anāgataṃsañāṇassa āvajjanāya ārammaṇapaccayena paccayo.
     2. Sanidassano dhammo anidassanassa dhammassa adhipatipaccayena paccayo.
     Ārammaṇādhipati:-- sanidassanaṃ rūpaṃ garuṃ katvā assādeti abhinandati, taṃ garuṃ katvā rāgo uppajjati diṭṭhi uppajjati.
     4. Anidassano dhammo anidassanassa . . .
     Ārammaṇādhipati, sahajātādhipati. Ārammaṇādhipati:
-- dānaṃ datvā sīlaṃ uposathakammaṃ, taṃ garuṃ katvā . . . pe . . . pubbe suciṇṇāni . . . jhānā vuṭṭhahitvā . . . pe . . . Ariyā maggā vuṭṭhahitvā maggaṃ garuṃ katvā phalaṃ garuṃ katvā . . . Nibbānaṃ gotrabhussa vodānassa maggassa phalassa adhipatipaccayena paccayo. Cakkhuṃ . . .
vatthuṃ anidassane khandhe garuṃ katvā assādeti abhinandati, taṃ garuṃ katvā rāgo uppajjati, diṭṭhi uppajjati.
Sahajātādhipati:-- anidassanādhipati sampayuttakānaṃ khandhānaṃ anidassanānaṃ cittasamuṭṭhānānañ ca rūpānaṃ adhipatipaccayena paccayo.
     5. Anidassano dhammo sanidassanassa . . .
     Sahajātādhipati:-- anidassanādhipati sanidassanānaṃ cittasamuṭṭhānānaṃ rūpānaṃ adhipatipaccayena paccayo.
     6. Anidassano dhammo sanidassanassa ca . . .
     Sahajātādhipati:-- anidassanādhipati sampayuttakānaṃ khandhānaṃ sanidassanānañ ca anidassanānañ ca cittasamuṭṭhānānañ ca rūpānaṃ adhipatipaccayena paccayo.

pe . . . patthanāya kāyikassa sukhassa kāyikassa dukkhassa maggassa phalasamāpattiyā upanissayapaccayena paccayo.

pe . . . phalasamāpattiyā upanissayapaccayena paccayo.

     4. Anidassano dhammo anidassanassa dhammassa vipākapaccayena paccayo . . . (tīṇi) . . . āhārapaccayena paccayo . . . (tīṇi, tīsu pi kabaḷiṃkāro āhāro kātabbo) . . .

     4. Anidassano dhammo anidassanassa dhammassa vippayuttapaccayena paccayo.
     Sahajātaṃ, purejātaṃ, pacchājātaṃ. Sahajātā anidassanā khandhā anidassanānaṃ cittasamuṭṭhānānaṃ rūpānaṃ vippayuttapaccayena paccayo. Paṭisandhikkhaṇe anidassanā khandhā anidassanānaṃ kaṭattā rūpānaṃ vippayuttapaccayena paccayo. Khandhā vatthussa vippayuttapaccayena paccayo, vatthu khandhānaṃ vippayuttapaccayena paccayo.
Purejātaṃ:-- cakkhāyatanaṃ cakkhuviññāṇassa . . . kāyāyatanaṃ kāyaviññāṇassa, vatthu anidassanānaṃ khandhānaṃ vippayuttapaccayena paccayo. Pacchājātā anidassanā khandhā purejātassa imassa anidassanassa kāyassa vippayuttapaccayena paccayo.
     5. Anidassano dhammo sanidassanassa dhammassa vippayuttapaccayena paccayo.
     Sahajātaṃ, pacchājātaṃ. Sahajātā anidassanā khandhā sanidassanānaṃ cittasamuṭṭhānānaṃ rūpānaṃ vippayuttapaccayena paccayo. Paṭisandhikkhaṇe pacchājātā anidassanā khandhā purejātassa imassa sanidassanassa kāyassa vippayuttapaccayena paccayo.

[page 101]
                          Atthivāro.                              101
     Sahajātaṃ, pacchājātaṃ. Sahājātā anidassanā khandhā sanidassanānañ ca anidassanānañ ca cittasamuṭṭhānānaṃ rūpānaṃ vippayuttapaccayena paccayo. Paṭisandhikkhaṇe pacchājātā anidassanā khandhā purejātassa imassa sanidassanassa ca anidassanassa ca kāyassa vippayuttapaccayena paccayo.
     2. Sanidassano dhammo anidassanassa dhammassa atthipaccayena paccayo.
     Sanidassane rūpe aniccato . . . pe . . . domanassaṃ uppajjati; dibbena cakkhunā rūpaṃ passati; rūpāyatanaṃ cakkhuviññāṇassa atthipaccayena paccayo.
     4. Anidassano dhammo anidassanassa . . .
     Sahajātaṃ, purejātaṃ, pacchājātaṃ āhāraṃ indriyaṃ.
Sahajāto anidassano eko khandho tiṇṇannaṃ khandhānaṃ anidassanānañ ca cittasamuṭṭhānānaṃ rūpānaṃ atthipaccayena paccayo. Dve . . . (saṃkhittaṃ, yāva asaññasattā).
Purejātaṃ cakkhuṃ . . . pe . . . vatthuṃ aniccato . . .
pe . . . domanassaṃ uppajjati; dibbāya sotadhātuyā saddaṃ suṇāti, saddāyatanaṃ sotaviññāṇassa . . . phoṭṭhabbāyatanaṃ kāyaviññāṇassa; cakkhāyatanaṃ cakkhuviññāṇassa . . . kāyāyatanaṃ kāyaviññāṇassa, vatthu anidassanānaṃ khandhānaṃ atthipaccayena paccayo. Pacchājātā anidassanā khandhā purejātassa imassa anidassanassa kāyassa atthipaccayena paccayo. Kabaḷiṃkāro āhāro imassa anidassanassa kāyassa atthipaccayena paccayo. Rūpajīvitindriyaṃ anidassanānaṃ kaṭattā rūpānaṃ atthipaccayena paccayo.
     5. Anidassano dhammo sanidassanassa . . .
     Sahajātaṃ, pacchājātaṃ āhāraṃ indriyaṃ. Sahajātā anidassanā khandhā sanidassanānaṃ cittasamuṭṭhānānaṃ rūpānaṃ atthipaccayena paccayo. Paṭisandhikkhaṇe mahābhūtā sanidassanānaṃ cittasamuṭṭhānānaṃ rūpānaṃ kaṭaṭṭā rūpānaṃ upādā rūpānaṃ atthipaccayena paccayo. Bāhiraṃ āhārasamuṭṭhānaṃ utusamuṭṭhānaṃ asaññasattānaṃ mahābhūtā sanidassanassa . . . Pacchājātā anidassanā khandhā purejātassa imassa sanidassanassa kāyassa atthipaccayena paccayo.


[page 102]
102                               Sanidassanadukaṃ
[... content straddling page break has been moved to the page above ...] Kabaḷiṃkāro āhāro imassa sanidassanassa kāyassa atthipaccayena paccayo. Rūpajīvitindriyaṃ sanidassanānaṃ kaṭattā rūpānaṃ atthipaccayena paccayo.
     6. Anidassano dhammo sanidassanassa ca . . .
     Sahajātaṃ, pacchājātaṃ āhāraṃ indriyaṃ. Sahajāto anidassano eko khandho tiṇṇannaṃ khandhānaṃ sanidassanānañ ca anidassanānañ ca cittasamuṭṭhānānaṃ rūpānaṃ atthipaccayena paccayo; dve khandhā . . . Paṭisandhikkhaṇe mahābhūtā sanidassanānañ ca anidassanānañ ca cittasamuṭṭhānānañ . . . Bāhiraṃ mahābhūtā sanidassanānañ ca anidassanānañ ca kaṭattā-rūpānaṃ upādā-rūpānaṃ atthipaccayena paccayo.
     8. Sanidassano ca . . . anidassanassa . . .
     Purejātaṃ rūpāyatanañ ca vatthu ca anidassanānaṃ khandhānaṃ atthipaccayena paccayo. Rūpāyatanañ ca cakkhāyatanañ ca cakkhuviññāṇassa atthipaccayena paccayo . . . natthi- . . . vigata- . . . avigatapaccayena paccayo.
          Hetuyā tīṇi,                     Kamme tīṇi,
          ārammaṇe dve,                     vipāke tīṇi,
          adhipatiyā cattāri,               āhāre tīṇi,
          anantare ekaṃ,                    indriye tīṇi,
          samanantare ekaṃ,                jhāne tīṇi,
          sahajāte tīṇi,                    magge tīṇi,
          aññamaññe ekaṃ,                sampayutte ekaṃ,
          nissaye tīṇi,                     vippayutte tīṇi,
          upanissaye dve,                atthiyā pañca,
          purejāte tīṇi,                    natthiyā ekaṃ,
          pacchājāte tīṇi,                vigate ekaṃ,
          āsevane ekaṃ,                     avigate pañca:--
     evaṃ gaṇetabbaṃ.
                          Anulomaṃ niṭṭhitaṃ.

domanassaṃ uppajjati; dibbena cakkhunā rūpaṃ passati,
dibbāya sotadhātuyā saddaṃ suṇāti. Rūpāyatanaṃ cakkhuviññāṇassa . . . phoṭṭhabbāyatanaṃ kāyaviññāṇassa sappaṭighā khandhā iddhividhañāṇassa pubbenivāsānussatiñāṇassa yathākammūpagañāṇassa anāgataṃsañāṇassa āvajjanāya ārammaṇapaccayena paccayo.

112                          Sappaṭighadukaṃ.
[... content straddling page break has been moved to the page above ...]
     4. Appaṭigho dhammo appatighassa dhammassa ārammaṇapaccayena paccayo.
     Dānaṃ sīlaṃ uposathakammaṃ katvā taṃ paccavekkhati,
pubbe suciṇṇāni paccavekkhati, jhānā vuṭṭhahitvā jhānaṃ paccavekkhati. Ariyā maggā vuṭṭhahitvā maggaṃ paccavekkhanti, phalaṃ paccavekkhanti. Nibbānaṃ gotrabhussa vodānassa maggassa phalassa āvajjanāya ārammaṇapaccayena paccayo. Ariyā pahīnakilese paccavekkhanti,
vikkhambhitakilese paccavekkhanti, pubbe samudāciṇṇe kilese jānanti. Vatthuṃ itthindriyaṃ purisindriyaṃ jīvitindriyaṃ āpodhātuṃ kabaḷiṃkāraṃ āhāraṃ aniccato . . . pe . . . domanassaṃ uppajjati, cetopariyañāṇena appaṭighacittasamaṃgissa cittaṃ jānāti; ākāsānañcāyatanaṃ viññāṇañcāyatanassa, ākiñcaññāyatanaṃ nevasaññānāsaññāyatanassa,
appaṭighā khandhā iddhividhañāṇassa cetopariyañāṇassa pubbenivāsānussatiñāṇassa yathākammūpagañāṇassa anāgataṃsañāṇassa āvajjanāya ārammaṇapaccayena paccayo.
     2. Sappaṭigho dhammo appaṭighassa dhammassa adhipatipaccayena paccayo.
     Ārammaṇādhipati:-- cakkhuṃ phoṭṭhabbe garuṃ katvā assādeti abhinandati . . . (saṃkhittaṃ) . . . taṃ garuṃ katvā rāgo uppajjati diṭṭhi uppajjati.
     4. Appaṭigho dhammo appaṭighassa . . .
     Ārammaṇādhipati, sahajātādhipati. Ārammaṇādhipati:
-- dānaṃ sīlaṃ uposathakammaṃ taṃ garuṃ katvā pubbe suciṇṇāni . . . jhānā vuṭṭhahitvā jhānaṃ garuṃ katvā paccavekkhati. Ariyā maggā vuṭṭhahitvā maggaṃ garuṃ katvā paccavekkhanti, phalaṃ garuṃ katvā . . . Nibbānaṃ gotrabhussa vodānassa maggassa phalassa adhipatipaccayena paccayo. Vatthuṃ itthindriyaṃ purisindriyaṃ jīvitindriyaṃ āpodhātuṃ kabaḷiṃkāraṃ āhāraṃ garuṃ katvā assādeti abhinandati taṃ garuṃ katvā rāgo uppajjati diṭṭhi uppajjati.

     5. Appaṭigho dhammo sappaṭighassa . . .
     Sahajātādhipati:-- appaṭighādhipati sappaṭighānaṃ cittasamuṭṭhānānaṃ . . .
     6. Appaṭigho dhammo sappaṭighassa ca . . .

     Purimā purimā appaṭighā . . . pe . . . phalasamāpattiyā anantarapaccayena paccayo.
     4. Appaṭigho dhammo appaṭighassa dhammassa samanantarapaccayena paccayo.
     Sappaṭigho dhammo sappaṭighassa dhammassa sahajātapaccayena paccayo . . . (nava) . . . aññamaññapaccayena paccayo . . . (cha) . . . nissayapaccayena paccayo . . . (nava).
     2. Sappaṭigho dhammo appaṭighassa dhammassa upanissayapaccayena paccayo.

utu . . . pe . . . senāsanaṃ saddhāya . . . pe . . .
phalasamāpattiyā upanissayapaccayena paccayo.

pe . . . domanassaṃ uppajjati, dibbena cakkhunā rūpaṃ passati, dibbāya sotadhātuyā saddaṃ suṇāti; rūpāyatanaṃ cakkhuviññāṇassa, . . . phoṭṭhabbāyatanaṃ kāyaviññāṇassa purejātapaccayena paccayo.      2. Sappaṭigho dhammo appaṭighassa dhammassa vippayuttapaccayena paccayo.

kāyāyatanaṃ kāyaviññāṇassa vippayuttappaccayena paccayo.

Paṭisandhikkhaṇe khandhā vatthussa, vatthu khandhānaṃ vippayuttapaccayena paccayo. Purejātaṃ vatthu appaṭighānaṃ khandhānaṃ vippayuttapaccayena paccayo.      Sahajātaṃ, pacchājātaṃ. Sahajātā appaṭighā khandhā sappaṭighānaṃ cittasamuṭṭhānānaṃ rūpānaṃ vippayuttapaccayena paccayo . . . (paṭisandhi). Pacchājātā appaṭighā khandhā purejātassa imassa sappaṭighassa kāyassa vippayuttapaccayena paccayo.

                          Atthivāro.                117
     Sahajātaṃ, pacchājātaṃ. Sahajātā appaṭighā khandhā sappaṭighānañ ca appaṭighānañ ca cittasamuṭṭhānānaṃ rūpānaṃ vippayuttapaccayena paccayo. Paṭisandhikkhaṇe pacchājātā . . . imassa sappaṭighassa ca appaṭighassa ca kāyassa vippayuttapaccayena paccayo.
     1. Sappaṭigho dhammo sappaṭighassa dhammassa atthipaccayena paccayo . . . (ekaṃ paṭiccasadisā paṭhamapañhā).
     2. Sappaṭigho dhammo appaṭighassa . . .
     Sahajātaṃ, purejātaṃ. Sahajātā sappaṭighā mahābhūtā apodhātuyā atthipaccayena paccayo. Sappaṭighā mahābhūtā appaṭighānaṃ cittasamuṭṭhānānaṃ rūpānaṃ kaṭattā rūpānaṃ upādā rūpānaṃ atthipaccayena paccayo. Phoṭṭhabbāyatanaṃ itthindriyassa . . . kabaḷiṃkārassa āhārassa atthipaccayena paccayo. Bāhiraṃ utusamuṭṭhānaṃ asaññasattānaṃ . . . Purejātaṃ:-- cakkhuṃ . . . pe . . . phoṭṭhabbe aniccato . . . pe . . . domanassaṃ uppajjati; dibbena cakkhunā rūpaṃ passati, dibbāya sotadhātuyā saddaṃ suṇāti;
rūpāyatanaṃ cakkhuviññāṇassa . . . phoṭṭhābbāyatanaṃ kāyaviññāṇassa, cakkhāyatanaṃ cakkhuviññāṇassa . . .
kāyāyatanaṃ kāyaviññāṇassa atthipaccayena paccayo.
     3. Sappaṭigho dhammo sappaṭighassa ca . . .
     Sappaṭighaṃ ekaṃ mahābhūtaṃ dvinnaṃ mahābhūtānaṃ āpodhātuyā ca atthipaccayena paccayo . . . pe . . . (paṭisandhi yāva asaññasattā).
     4. Appaṭigho dhammo appaṭighassa . . .
     Sahajātaṃ, purejātaṃ, pacchājātaṃ āhāraṃ indriyaṃ. Sahajāto appaṭigho eko khandho tiṇṇannaṃ . . . (yāva asaññasattā). Purejātaṃ vatthuṃ itthindriyaṃ purisindriyaṃ jīvitindriyaṃ āpodhātuṃ kabaḷiṃkāraṃ āhāraṃ aniccato . . .
pe . . . domanassaṃ uppajjati; vatthu appaṭighānaṃ khandhānaṃ atthipaccayena paccayo. Pacchājātā appaṭighā khandhā purejātassa imassa appaṭighassa kāyassa atthipaccayena paccayo.

                     SAPPAṬIGHA-DUKAṂ niṭṭhitaṃ.


[page 121]
                               121
                          [XI. RŪPI-DUKAṂ.]
     1. Rūpiṃ dhammaṃ paṭicca rūpī dhammo uppajjati hetupaccayā.
     Ekaṃ mahābhūtaṃ paṭicca tayo mahābhūtā; dve . . .
pe . . . Mahābhūte paṭicca cittasamuṭṭhānaṃ rūpaṃ kaṭattā rūpaṃ upādā rūpaṃ.
     2. Rūpiṃ dhammaṃ paṭicca arūpī dhammo uppajjati hetupaccayā.
     Paṭisandhikkhaṇe vatthuṃ paṭicca arūpino khandhā.
     3. Rūpiṃ dhammaṃ paṭicca rūpī ca arūpī ca dhammā uppajjanti hetupaccayā.
     Paṭisandhikkhaṇe vatthuṃ paṭicca arūpino khandhā;
mahābhūte paṭicca kaṭattā rūpaṃ.
     4. Arūpiṃ dhammaṃ paṭicca arūpī dhammo . . .
     Arūpiṃ ekaṃ khandhaṃ paṭicca tayo khandhā; dve . . .
(paṭisandhi).
     5. Arūpiṃ dhammaṃ paṭicca rūpī dhammo . . .
     Arūpino khandhe paṭicca cittasamuṭṭhānaṃ rūpaṃ . . .
(paṭisandhi).

122                     Rūpidukaṃ.

     Arūpino khandhe ca mahābhūte ca paṭicca kaṭattā rūpaṃ . . . (saṃkhittaṃ).
          Hetuyā nava,                     vipāke nava,
          ārammaṇe tīṇi,                    āhāre nava,
          adhipatiyā pañca,                indriye nava,
          anantare tīṇi,                    jhāne nava,

          nissaye nava,                     atthiyā nava,

          āsevane ekaṃ,                     avigate nava.
          kamme nava,
                          Anulomaṃ niṭṭhitaṃ.
     1. Rūpiṃ dhammaṃ paṭicca rūpī dhammo uppajjati nahetupaccayā . . . (tīṇi).

dve . . . Ahetupaṭisandhikkhaṇe vicikicchāsahagate uddhaccasahagate khandhe paṭicca vicikicchāsahagato uddhaccasahagato moho.

pe . . . domanassaṃ uppajjati; dibbena cakkhunā rūpaṃ passati, dibbāya sotadhātuyā saddaṃ suṇāti. Rūpāyatanaṃ cakkhuviññāṇassa ārammaṇapaccayena paccayo . . .
phoṭṭhabbāyatanaṃ kāyaviññāṇassa ārammaṇapaccayena paccayo. Rūpino khandhā iddhividhañāṇassa . . . pe . . . anāgataṃsañāṇassa āvajjanāya ārammaṇapaccayena paccayo.

     Dānaṃ, sīlaṃ, uposathakammaṃ taṃ paccavekkhati, pubbe jhānā . . . Ariyā maggā . . . phalaṃ paccavekkhanti.
Nibbānaṃ gotrabhussa vodānassa maggassa phalassa āvajjanāya ārammaṇapaccayena paccayo. Ariyā pahīnakilese . . .
(saṃkhittaṃ) . . . vikkhambhitakilese. . . pubbe . . . Arūpino khandhe aniccato . . . pe . . . domanassaṃ uppajjati;
cetopariyañāṇena arūpicittasamaṃgissa cittaṃ jānāti, ākāsānañcāyatanaṃ viññāṇañcāyatanassa ākiñcaññāyatanaṃ nevasaññānāsaññāyatanassa arūpino khandhā iddhividhañāṇassa cetopariyañāṇassa pubbenivāsānussatiñāṇassa yathākammūpagañāṇassa anāgataṃsañāṇassa āvajjanāya ārammaṇapaccayena paccayo.

128                          Rūpidukaṃ.
     Ārammaṇādhipati:-- cakkhuṃ . . . pe . . . kabaḷiṃkāraṃ āhāraṃ garuṃ katvā assādeti abhinandati, taṃ garuṃ katvā rāgo uppajjati diṭṭhi uppajjati.
     4. Arūpī dhammo arūpissa dhammassa . . .
     Ārammaṇādhipati, sahajātādhipati. Ārammaṇādhipati:-- dānaṃ . . . (saṃkhittaṃ) . . . nibbānaṃ maggassa phalassa adhipatipaccayena paccayo. Arūpino khandhe garuṃ katvā assādeti . . . rāgo uppajjati, diṭṭhi uppajjati. Sahajātādhipāti:-- arūpī adhipati sampayuttakānaṃ khandhānaṃ adhipatipaccayena paccayo.

     6. Arūpī dhammo rūpissa . . . ca arūpissa . . .
     Sahajātādhipati:-- arūpī adhipati sampayuttakānaṃ khandhānaṃ cittasamuṭṭhānānañ ca rūpānaṃ adhipatipaccayena paccayo.
     4. Arūpī dhammo arūpissa dhammassa anantarapaccayena paccayo.
     Purimā purimā arūpino khandhā pacchimānaṃ pacchimānaṃ arūpīnaṃ khandhānaṃ phalasamāpattiyā anantarapaccayena paccayo . . . samanantarapaccayena paccayo . . . sahajātapaccayena paccayo . . . (satta, miha ghaṭanā natthi) . . . aññamaññapaccayena paccayo . . .
nissayapaccayena paccayo . . . (satta pañhā, miha ghaṭanā natthi).

[page 130]
130                               Rūpidukaṃ.
     5. Arūpī dhammo rūpissa dhammassa . . .

     6. Arūpī dhammo rūpissa ca arūpissa . . .
     Sahajātā, nānākhaṇikā. Sahajātā arūpī cetanā sampayuttakānaṃ khandhānaṃ cittasamuṭṭhānānañ ca rūpānaṃ kammapaccayena paccayo. Nānākhaṇikā arūpī cetanā vipākānaṃ khandhānaṃ kaṭattā ca rūpānaṃ kammapaccayena paccayo.
     4. Arūpī dhammo arūpissa dhammassa vipākapaccayena paccayo . . . (tīṇi).

     Kabaḷiṃkāro āhāro imassa kāyassa āhārapaccayena paccayo.
     4. Arūpī dhammo arūpissa dhammassa āhārapaccayena paccayo . . . (tīṇi).

     Rūpajīvitindriyaṃ kaṭattā rūpānaṃ indriyapaccayena paccayo.
     2. Rūpī dhammo arūpissa dhammassa . . .

     4. Arūpī dhammo arūpissa dhammassa indriyapaccayena paccayo . . . (tīṇi).

[page 131]
                          Atthivāro.                131
     Cakkhundriyañ ca cakkhuviññāṇañ ca cakkhuviññāṇasahagatānaṃ khandhānaṃ indriyapaccayena paccayo. Kāyindriyañ ca . . . pe . . .
     4. Arūpī dhammo arūpissa dhammassa jhānapaccayena paccayo . . . (tīṇi) . . . maggapaccayena paccayo . . .
(tīṇi) . . . sampayuttapaccayena paccayo . . . (ekaṃ).
     2. Rūpī dhammo arūpissa dhammassa vippayuttapaccayena paccayo.
     Sahajātaṃ, purejātaṃ. Sahajātaṃ:-- paṭisandhikkhaṇe vatthu arūpīnaṃ khandhānaṃ vippayuttapaccayena paccayo. Purejātaṃ cakkhāyatanaṃ cakkhuviññāṇassa . . .
kāyāyatanaṃ kāyaviññāṇassa, vatthu arūpīnaṃ khandhānaṃ vippayuttapaccayena paccayo.
     5. Arūpī dhammo rūpissa dhammassa . . .
     Sahajātaṃ, pacchājātaṃ. Sahajātā arūpino khandhā cittasamuṭṭhānānaṃ rūpānaṃ vippayuttapaccayena paccayo. Paṭisandhikkhaṇe arūpī khandhā kaṭattā rūpānaṃ vippayuttapaccayena paccayo. Pacchājātā arūpino khandhā purejātassa imassa kāyassa vippayuttapaccayena paccayo.
     1. Rūpī dhammo rūpissa dhammassa atthipaccayena paccayo.
     Sahājātaṃ āhāraṃ indriyaṃ. Sahajātaṃ ekaṃ mahābhūtaṃ . . . (yāva asaññasattā). Kabaḷiṃkāro āhāro imassa kāyassa atthiyapaccayena paccayo. Rūpajīvitindriyaṃ kaṭattā rūpānaṃ atthipaccayena paccayo.
     2. Rūpī dhammo arūpissa dhammassa . . .
     Sahajātaṃ, purejātaṃ. Sahajātaṃ:-- paṭisandhikkhaṇe vatthu arūpīnaṃ khandhānaṃ atthipaccayena paccayo.
Purejātaṃ:-- cakkhuṃ . . . pe . . . kabaḷiṃkāraṃ āhāraṃ aniccato . . . pe . . . domanassaṃ uppajjati; dibbena cakkhunā.. pe . . . dibbāya sotadhātuyā . . . pe . . .
rūpāyatanaṃ cakkhuviññāṇassa . . . phoṭṭhabbāyatanaṃ kāyaviññāṇassa, cakkhāyatanaṃ cakkhuviññāṇassa . . .


[page 132]
132                     Rūpidukaṃ.
kāyāyatanaṃ kāyaviññāṇassa, vatthu arūpīnaṃ khandhānaṃ atthipaccayena paccayo.
     4. Arūpī dhammo arūpissa dhammassa . . .
     Arūpī eko khandho tiṇṇannaṃ khandhānaṃ . . . pe . . .
dve . . . pe . . . Paṭisandhikkhaṇe . . . pe . . .
     5. Arūpī dhammo rūpissa dhammassa . . .
     Sahajātaṃ, pacchājātaṃ. Sahajātā arūpino khandhā cittasamuṭṭhānānaṃ rūpānaṃ atthipaccayena paccayo.
Paṭisandhikkhaṇe pacchājātā arūpino khandhā purejātassa imassa kāyassa atthipaccayena paccayo.
     6. Arūpī dhammo rūpissa ca arūpissa ca . . .

dve . . . pe . . . Paṭisandhikkhaṇe . . . pe . . .
     7. Rūpī ca arūpī ca dhammā rūpissa . . .

Pacchājātā arūpino khandhā ca kabaḷiṃkāro āhāro ca imassa kāyassa atthipaccayena paccayo. Pacchājātā arūpino khandhā ca rūpajīvitindriyañ ca kaṭattā rūpānaṃ atthipaccayena paccayo.
     8. Rūpī ca arūpī ca dhammā arūpissa . . .

Kāyaviññāṇasahagato arūpī eko khandho ca vatthu ca tiṇṇannaṃ khandhānaṃ atthipaccayena paccayo . . . pe . . . dve . . . pe . . . Paṭisandhikkhaṇe arūpī eko khandho ca vatthu ca tiṇṇannaṃ khandhānaṃ . . . pe . . . dve . . . pe . . . natthipaccayena paccayo . . .
vigata- . . . avigatapaccayena paccayo.

[page 140]
140                               Lokiyadukaṃ.
     1. Lokiyo dhammo lokiyassa dhammassa ārammaṇapaccayena paccayo.
     Dānaṃ sīlaṃ uposathakammaṃ katvā taṃ paccavekkhati, pubbe suciṇṇāni paccavekkhati. Jhānā . . . pe . . . Ariyā gotrabhuṃ paccavekkhanti, vodānaṃ paccavekkhanti, pahīnakilese paccavekkhanti, vikkhambhitakilese paccavekkhanti, pubbe samudāciṇṇe kilese jānanti.
Cakkhuṃ . . . pe . . . vatthuṃ . . . pe . . . lokiye khandhe aniccato . . . pe . . . domanassaṃ uppajjati;
dibbena cakkhunā rūpaṃ passati, dibbāya sotadhātuyā saddaṃ suṇāti, cetopariyañāṇena lokiyacittasamaṃgissa cittaṃ jānāti, ākāsānañcāyatanaṃ viññāṇañcāyatanassa, ākiñcaññāyatanaṃ nevasaññānāsaññāyatanassa, rūpāyatanaṃ cakkhuviññāṇassa . . . pe . . . phoṭṭhabbāyatanaṃ kāyaviññāṇassa, lokiyā khandhā iddhividhañāṇassa cetopariyañāṇassa pubbenivāsānussatiñāṇassa yathākammūpagañāṇassa anāgataṃsañāṇassa āvajjanāya ārammaṇapaccayena paccayo.
     4. Lokuttaro dhammo lokuttarassa dhammassa . . .
     Nibbānaṃ maggassa phalassa ārammaṇapaccayena paccayo.
     5. Lokuttaro dhammo lokiyassa . . .
     Ariyā maggā vuṭṭhahitvā maggaṃ paccavekkhanti, phalaṃ paccavekkhanti, nibbānaṃ paccavekkhanti, nibbānaṃ gotrabhussa vodānassa āvajjanāya ārammaṇapaccayena paccayo.
Ariyā cetopariyañāṇena lokuttaracittasamaṃgissa cittaṃ jānanti. Lokuttarā khandhā cetopariyañāṇassa pubbenivāsānussatiñāṇassa yathākammūpagañāṇassa anāgataṃsañāṇassa āvajjanāya ārammaṇapaccayena paccayo.
     1. Lokiyo dhammo lokiyassa dhammassa adhipatipaccayena paccayo.
     Ārammaṇādhipati, sahajātādhipati. Ārammaṇādhipati:
-- dānaṃ datvā sīlaṃ uposathakammaṃ . . . pubbe . . . jhānā


[page 141]
                               Anantaravāro.                     141
. . . pe . . . sekhā gotrabhuṃ garuṃ katvā . . . pe . . .
vodānaṃ garuṃ katvā paccavekkhanti. Cakkhuṃ . . . pe . . . vatthuṃ lokiye khandhe garuṃ katvā assādeti abhinandati, taṃ garuṃ katvā rāgo uppajjati diṭṭhi uppajjati. Sahajātādhipati:-- lokiyādhipati sampayuttakānaṃ khandhānaṃ cittasamuṭṭhānānañ ca rūpānaṃ adhipatipaccayena paccayo.
     4. Lokuttaro dhammo lokuttarassa . . .
     Ārammaṇādhipati, sahajātādhipati. Ārammaṇādhipati:
-- nibbānaṃ maggassa phalassa adhipatipaccayena paccayo.
Sahajātādhipati:-- lokuttarādhipati sampayuttakānaṃ khandhānaṃ adhipatipaccayena paccayo.
     5. Lokuttaro dhammo lokiyassa . . .
     Ārammaṇādhipati, sahajātādhipati. Ārammaṇādhipati:
-- ariyā maggā vuṭṭhahitvā maggaṃ garuṃ, phalaṃ, nibbānaṃ garuṃ katvā paccavekkhanti; nibbānaṃ gotrabhussa vodānassa adhipatipaccayena paccayo. Sahajātādhipati:-- lokuttarādhipati cittasamuṭṭhānānaṃ rūpānaṃ adhipatipaccayena paccayo.
     6. Lokuttaro dhammo lokuyassa ca . . .
     Sahajātādhipati:-- lokuttarādhipati sampayuttakānaṃ khandhānaṃ cittasamuṭṭhānānañ ca rūpānaṃ adhipatipaccayena paccayo.
     1. Lokiyo dhammo lokiyassa dhammassa anantarapaccayena paccayo.
     Purimā purimā lokiyā khandhā pacchimānaṃ pacchimānaṃ lokiyānaṃ khandhānaṃ . . . pe . . . anulomaṃ gotrabhussa anulomaṃ vodānassa anantarapaccayena paccayo.
     2. Lokiyo dhammo lokuttarassa . . .

upanissayapaccayena paccayo.

abhiññaṃ uppādeti, samāpattiṃ uppādeti; mānaṃ jappeti,

kāyikassa dukkhassa upanissayapaccayena paccayo. Kusalākusalaṃ kammaṃ vipākassa upanissayapaccayena paccayo.

pe . . . catutthassa maggassa parikammaṃ catutthassa maggassa upanissayapaccayena paccayo.

                               [XIV.
                          ĀSAVA-DUKAṂ.]
                              [Anulomaṃ.]
     1. Āsavaṃ dhammaṃ paṭicca āsavo dhammo uppajjati hetupaccayā.
     Kāmāsavaṃ paṭicca diṭṭhāsavo avijjāsavo. Diṭṭhāsavaṃ paṭicca kāmāsavo avijjāsavo. Avijjāsavaṃ paṭicca kāmāsavo diṭṭhāsavo. Bhavāsavaṃ paṭicca avijjāsavo. Diṭṭhāsavaṃ paṭicca avijjāsavo. (Ekekamhi cakkaṃ kātabbaṃ.)
     2. Āsavaṃ dhammaṃ paṭicca no-āsavo dhammo uppajjati hetupaccayā.
     Āsavaṃ paṭicca sampayuttakā khandhā cittasamuṭṭhānañ ca rūpaṃ.
     3. Āsavaṃ dhammaṃ paṭicca āsavo ca no-āsavo ca dhammā uppajjanti hetupaccayā.
     Kāmāsavaṃ paṭicca diṭṭhāsavo avijjāsavo sampayuttakā ca khandhā cittasamuṭṭhānañ ca rūpaṃ . . . [cakkaṃ bandhitabbaṃ).
     4. No-āsavaṃ dhammaṃ paṭicca no-āsavo . . .
     No-āsavaṃ ekaṃ khandhaṃ paṭicca tayo khandhā cittasamuṭṭhānaṃ rūpaṃ . . . pe . . . dve . . . pe . . .

154                     Āsavadukaṃ.

     4. No-āsavo dhammo no-āsavassa dhammassa purejātapaccayena paccayo.
     Ārammaṇapurejātaṃ, vatthupurejātaṃ. Ārammaṇapurejātaṃ:-- cakkhuṃ . . . pe . . . vatthuṃ . . . (evaṃ vitthāretabbaṃ) . . . phoṭṭhabbāyatanaṃ kāyaviññāṇassa purejātapaccayena paccayo. Vatthupurejātaṃ:-- cakkhāyatanaṃ cakkhuviññāṇassa . . . kāyāyatanaṃ kāyaviññāṇassa, vatthu no-āsavānaṃ khandhānaṃ purejātapaccayena paccayo.
     5. No-āsavo dhammo āsavassa dhammassa purejātapaccayena paccayo.
     Ārammaṇapurejātaṃ, vatthupurejātaṃ. Ārammaṇapurejātaṃ:-- cakkhuṃ . . . pe . . . vatthuṃ assādeti abhinandati,
taṃ ārabbha āsavā uppajjanti. Vatthupurejātaṃ:-- vatthu āsavānaṃ purejātapaccayena paccayo.
     6. No-āsavo dhammo āsavassa ca . . . paccayo.
     Ārammaṇapurejātaṃ . . . taṃ ārabbha āsavā ca sampayuttakā ca khandhā uppajjanti. Vatthupurejātaṃ:-- vatthu āsavānañ ca sampayuttakānañ ca khandhānaṃ purejātapaccayena paccayo.
     2. Āsavo dhammo no-āsavassa dhammassa pacchājātapaccayena paccayo.
     Pacchājātā āsavā purejātassa imassa kāyassa pacchājātapaccayena paccayo.
     4. No-āsavo dhammo no-āsavassa . . .
     Pacchājātā no-āsavā khandhā purejātassa imassa kāyassa pacchājātapaccayena paccayo.
     8. Āsavo ca no-āsavo ca dhammā no-āsavassa . . .
     Pacchājātā āsavā ca sampayuttakā ca khandhā purejātassa imassa kāyassa pacchājātapaccayena paccayo.
     1. Āsavo dhammo āsavassa dhammassa āsevanapaccayena paccayo . . . (nava).
     4. No-āsavo dhammo no-āsavassa dhammassa kammapaccayena paccayo.


[page 164]
164                     Āsavadukaṃ.
     Sahajātā, nānākhaṇikā. Sahajātā no-āsavā cetanā sampayuttakānaṃ khandhānaṃ cittasamuṭṭhānānañ ca rūpānaṃ kammapaccayena paccayo. Nānākhaṇikā:-- no-āsavā cetanā vipākānaṃ khandhānaṃ kaṭattā ca rūpānaṃ kammapaccayena paccayo.
     5. No-āsavo dhammo āsavassa . . .
     No-āsavā cetanā sampayuttakānaṃ āsavānaṃ kammapaccayena paccayo.
     6. No-āsavo dhammo āsavassa ca . . .
     No-āsavā cetanā sampayuttakānaṃ khandhānaṃ āsavānañ ca cittasamuṭṭhānānañ ca rūpānaṃ kammapaccayena paccayo.
     4. No-āsavo dhammo no-āsavassa dhammassa vipākapaccayena paccayo . . . (ekaṃ) . . . āhārapaccayena paccayo.
     No-āsavā āhārā sampayuttakānaṃ khandhānaṃ cittasamuṭṭhānānañ ca rūpānaṃ āhārapaccayena paccayo. Paṭisandhikkhaṇe kabaḷiṃkāro āhāro imassa kāyassa āhārapaccayena paccayo.
     5. No-āsavo dhammo . . . āsavassa . . .
     No āsavā āharā sampayuttakānaṃ āsavānaṃ āhārapacca yena paccayo.
     6. No-āsavo dhammo āsavassa ca no-āsavassa ca dhammassa āhārapaccayena paccayo.
     No-āsavā āhārā sampayuttakānaṃ khandhānaṃ āsavānañ ca cittasamuṭṭhānānañ ca rūpānaṃ āhārapaccayena paccayo.
     4. no-āsavo dhammo no-āsavassa dhammassa indriyapaccayena paccayo.
     No-āsavā indriyā sampayuttakānaṃ khandhānaṃ cittasamuṭṭhānānañ ca rūpānaṃ indriyapaccayena paccayo. Paṭisandhikkhaṇe cakkhundriyaṃ cakkhuviññāṇassa . . . kāyindriyaṃ kāyaviññāṇassa indriyapaccayena paccayo. Rūpajīvitindriyaṃ kaṭattā rūpānaṃ indriyapaccayena paccayo . . .
(tīṇi), jhāna-, . . . (tīṇi), magga-, . . . (nava), sampayuttapaccayena paccayo . . . (nava).

     4. Anāsavaṃ dhammaṃ paṭicca anāsavo dhammo uppajjati hetupaccayā.

     7. Sāsavañ ca anāsavañ ca dhammaṃ paṭicca sāsavo dhammo uppajjati hetupaccayā.
     Anāsave khandhe ca mahābhūte ca paṭicca cittasamuṭṭhānaṃ rūpaṃ (yathā cūlantaraduke lokiya-dukaṃ, evaṃ kātabbaṃ; ninnānākaraṇaṃ).

          āsevane cha,                     avigate nava.

     1. Asavasampayutto dhammo āsavasampayuttassa dhammassa hetupaccayena paccayo.

     Āsavasampayuttā hetū sampayuttakānaṃ khandhānaṃ mohassa . . .

     5. Āsavavippayutto . . . āsavasampayuttassa . . .
     Domanassa-, vicikicchā-, uddhacca-sahagato moho sampayuttakānaṃ khandhānaṃ hetupaccayena paccayo.
     6. Āsavavippayutto . . . āsavasampayuttassa ca . . .
     Domanassasahagato . . . pe . . . khandhānaṃ cittasamuṭṭhānānañ ca rūpānaṃ hetupaccayena paccayo.

182                Āsavasampayuttadukaṃ.
     9. Āsavasampayutto ca . . . dhammā āsavasampayuttassa ca dhammassa hetupaccayena paccayo.

     1. Āsavasampayutto dhammo āsavasampayuttassa dhammassa ārammaṇapaccayena paccayo.

     4. Āsavavippayutto . . . āsavavippayuttassa . . .
     Dānaṃ sīlaṃ uposathakammaṃ taṃ paccavekkhati, pubbe suciṇṇāni . . . jhānā . . . Ariyā maggā vuṭṭhahitvā maggaṃ, phalaṃ, nibbānaṃ . . . nibbānaṃ gotrabhussa vodānassa maggassa phalassa āvajjanāya ārammaṇapaccayena paccayo. Ariyā āsavavippayutte pahīnakilese paccavekkhanti,
vikkhāmbhitakilese paccavekkhanti, pubbe . . . pe . . .
cakkhuṃ, vatthuṃ āsavavippayutte khandhe aniccato dukkhato anattato vipassanti (idha assādanā natthi). Dibbena cakkhunā rūpaṃ passati, dibbāya sotadhātuyā saddaṃ suṇāti,
cetopariyañāṇena āsavavippayuttacittasamaṃgissa cittaṃ jānāti; ākāsānañcāyatanaṃ viññāṇañcāyatanassa, ākiñcaññāyatanaṃ nevasaññānāsaññāyatanassa, rūpāyatanaṃ cakkhuviññāṇassa, . . . phoṭṭhabbāyatanaṃ kāyaviññāṇassa, āsavavippayuttā khandhā iddhividhañāṇassa cetopariyañāṇassa pubbenivāsānussatiñāṇassa yathākammūpagañāṇassa anāgataṃsañāṇassa āvajjanāya mohassa ārammaṇapaccayena paccayo.

     Dānaṃ sīlaṃ uposathakammaṃ katvā taṃ assādeti abhinandati, taṃ ārabbha rāgo uppajjati diṭṭhi uppajjati vicikicchā,

                          Adhipativāro.                183
[... content straddling page break has been moved to the page above ...] uddhaccaṃ, domanassaṃ uppajjati; pubbe suciṇṇāni . . . jhānā vuṭṭhahitvā jhānaṃ . . . cakkhuṃ . . . pe . . .
vatthuṃ āsavavippayutte khandhe assādeti abhinandati; taṃ ārabbha rāgo, diṭṭhi . . . domanassaṃ uppajjati.
     6. Āsavavippayutto . . . āsavasampayuttassa ca . . .
     Cakkhuṃ . . . pe . . . vatthuṃ āsavavippayutte khandhe ārabbha domanassa-, vicikicchā-, uddhacca-sahagatā khandhā ca moho ca uppajjanti.
     7. Āsavasampayutto ca . . . āsavasampayuttassa . . .
     Domanassa-, vicikicchā-, uddhacca-sahagate khandhe ca mohañ ca ārabbha āsavasampayuttā khandhā uppajjanti.
     8. Āsavasampayutto ca . . . dhammā āsavavippayuttassa . . .
     Domanassa-, vicikicchā-, uddhacca-sahagate khandhe ca mohañ ca ārabbha āsavavippayuttā khandhā ca moho ca uppajjanti.
     9. Āsavasampayutto ca āsavavippayutto ca dhammā āsavasampayuttassa ca āsavavippayuttassa ca . . .
     Domanassa-, vicikicchā-, uddhacca-sahagate khandhe ca mohañ ca ārabbha domanassa-vicikicchā-uddhacca-sahagatā khandhā ca moho ca uppajjanti.
     1. Āsavasampayutto dhammo āsavasampayuttassa dhammassa adhipatipaccayena paccayo.
     Ārammaṇādhipati, sahajātādhipati. Ārammaṇādhipati:-- āsavasampayutte khandhe garuṃ katvā āsavasampayuttā khandhā uppajjanti. Sahajātādhipati:-- āsavasampayuttādhipati sampayuttakānaṃ khandhānaṃ adhipatipaccayena paccayo.
     2. Āsavasampayutto dhammo āsavavippayuttassa . . .
     Sahajātādhipati:-- āsavasampayuttādhipati cittasamuṭṭhānānaṃ rūpānaṃ adhipatipaccayena paccayo. Domanassasahagatādhipati mohassa cittasamuṭṭhānānañ ca rūpānaṃ adhipatipaccayena paccayo.


[page 184]
184                Āsavasampayuttadukaṃ.
     3. Āsavasampayutto dhammo āsavasampayuttassa ca āsavavippayuttassa ca . . .
     Sahajātā āsavasampayuttādhipati sampayuttakānaṃ khandhānaṃ cittasamuṭṭhānānañ ca rūpānaṃ adhipatipaccayena paccayo. Domanassasahagatādhipati sampayuttakānaṃ khandhānaṃ mohassa ca cittasamuṭṭhānānañ ca rūpānaṃ adhipatipaccayena paccayo.
     4. Āsavavippayutto dhammo āsavavippayuttassa . . .
     Ārammaṇādhipati, sahajātādhipati. Ārammaṇādhipati:-- dānaṃ sīlaṃ uposathakammaṃ . . . taṃ garuṃ katvā paccavekkhati, pubbe suciṇṇāni . . . jhānā vuṭṭhahitvā jhānaṃ . . . Ariyā maggā vuṭṭhahitvā maggaṃ phalaṃ garuṃ katvā paccavekkhanti, nibbānaṃ . . . Nibbānaṃ gotrabhussa vodānassa maggassa phalassa adhipatipaccayena paccayo.
Sahajātādhipati:-- āsavavippayuttādhipati sampayuttakānaṃ khandhānaṃ cittasamuṭṭhānānañ ca rūpānaṃ adhipatipaccayena paccayo.
     5. Āsavavippayutto dhammo āsavasampayuttassa . . .
     Ārammaṇādhipati:-- dānaṃ sīlaṃ uposathakammaṃ katvā taṃ garuṃ katvā assādeti abhinandati, taṃ garuṃ katvā rāgo uppajjati diṭṭhi uppajjati . . . pe . . . pubbe suciṇṇāni . . . jhānā . . . cakkhuṃ . . . vatthuṃ āsavavippayutte khandhe garuṃ katvā assādeti . . . pe . . . uppajjati.
     1. Āsavasampayutto dhammo āsavasampayuttassa dhammassa anantarapaccayena paccayo.
     Purimā purimā āsavasampayuttā khandhā pacchimānaṃ pacchimānaṃ āsavasampayuttakānaṃ khandhānaṃ anantarapaccayena paccayo.
     2. Āsavasampayutto dhammo āsavavippayuttassa . . .
     Purimā purimā domanassa-vicikicchā-uddhacca-sahagatā khandhā pacchimassa pacchimassa domanassa-vicikicchāuddhaccasahagatassa mohassa anantarapaccayena paccayo.

                          Anantaravāro.                185
[... content straddling page break has been moved to the page above ...]
Āsavasampayuttā khandhā vuṭṭhānassa anantarapaccayena paccayo.

Purimā purimā āsavavippayuttā khandhā pacchimānaṃ pacchimānaṃ āsavavippayuttānaṃ khandhānaṃ anantarapaccayena paccayo. Anulomaṃ gotrabhussa phalasamāpattiyā anantarapaccayena paccayo,

     6. Āsavavippayutto dhammo āsavasampayuttassa ca āsavavippayuttassa ca . . .

     1. Āsavasampayutto dhammo āsavasampayuttassa dhammassa āsevanapaccayena paccayo . . . (nava. Āvajjanā pi vuṭṭhānam pi natthi).


[page 189]
                          Āhāravāro.                189
     1. Āsavasampayutto dhammo āsavasampayuttassa dhammassa kammapaccayena paccayo.
     Āsavasampayuttā cetanā sampayuttakānaṃ khandhānaṃ kammapaccayena paccayo.
     2. Āsavasampayutto dhammo āsavavippayuttassa . . .
     Sahajātā, nānākhaṇikā. Sahajātā āsavasampayuttā cetanā cittasamuṭṭhānānaṃ rūpānaṃ kammapaccayena paccayo.
Nānākhaṇikā āsavasampayuttā cetanā vipākānaṃ khandhānaṃ kaṭattā ca rūpānaṃ kammapaccayena paccayo. Domanassa-, vicikicchā-, uddhacca-sahagatā cetanā mohassa cittasamuṭṭhānānañ ca rūpānaṃ kammapaccayena paccayo.
     3. Āsavasampayutto . . . āsavasampayuttassa ca . . .
     Āsavasampayuttā cetanā sampayuttakānaṃ khandhānaṃ cittasamuṭṭhānānañ ca rūpānaṃ kammapaccayena paccayo.
Domanassa-, vicikicchā-, uddhacca-sahagatā cetanā sampayuttakānaṃ khandhānaṃ mohassa ca cittasamuṭṭhānānañ ca rūpānaṃ kammapaccayena paccayo.
     4. Āsavavippayutto . . . āsavavippayuttassa . . .
     Sahajātā, nānākhaṇikā. Sahajātā āsavavippayuttā cetanā sampayuttakānaṃ khandhānaṃ cittasamuṭṭhānānañ ca rūpānaṃ kammapaccayena paccayo. Nānākhaṇikā āsavavippayuttā cetanā vipākānaṃ khandhānaṃ kaṭattā ca rūpānaṃ kammapaccayena paccayo.
     4. Āsavavippayutto dhammo āsavavippayuttassa dhammassa vipākapaccayena paccayo . . . (ekaṃ).
     1. Āsavasampayutto dhammo āsavasampayuttassa dhammassa āhārapaccayena paccayo.
     Āsavasampayuttā āhārā sampayuttakānaṃ khandhānaṃ āhārapaccayena paccayo.
     2. Āsavasampayutto . . . āsavavippayuttassa . . .
     Āsavasampayuttā āhārā cittasamuṭṭhānānaṃ rūpānaṃ āhārapaccayena paccayo. Domanassa-vicikicchā-uddhacca-sahagatā āhārā mohassa cittasamuṭṭhānānañ ca rūpānaṃ āhārapaccayena paccayo.

                          Atthivāro.                191
     Sahajātaṃ, pacchājātaṃ. Sahajātā domanassa-vicikicchāuddhacca-sahagatā khandhā ca moho ca cittasamuṭṭhānānaṃ rūpānaṃ vippayuttapaccayena paccayo. Pacchājātā domanassa-vicikicchā-uddhacca-sahagatā khandhā ca moho ca purejātassa imassa kāyassa vippayuttapaccayena paccayo.
     1. Āsavasampayutto dhammo āsavasampayuttassa dhammassa atthipaccayena paccayo . . . (ekaṃ).
     2. Āsavasampayutto . . . āsavavippayuttassa . . .

Domanassa-vicikicchā-, uddhacca-sahagatā khandhā mohassa ca cittasamuṭṭhānānañ ca rūpānaṃ atthipaccayena paccayo. Pacchājātā āsavasampayuttā khandhā purejātassa imassa kāyassa atthipaccayena paccayo.

(sahajātasadisaṃ).

192                Asavasampayuttadukaṃ.
     7. Āsavasampayutto ca . . . āsavasampayuttassa . . .
     Sahajātaṃ, purejātaṃ. Sahajāto āsavasampayutto eko khandho ca vatthu ca tiṇṇannaṃ khandhānaṃ atthipaccayena paccayo; dve . . . Domanassa-vicikicchā-uddhaccasahagato eko khandho ca moho ca tiṇṇannaṃ khandhānaṃ atthipaccayena paccayo; dve . . .
     8. Āsavasampayutto ca . . . āsavavippayuttassa . . .
     Sahajātaṃ, pacchājātaṃ āhāraṃ indriyaṃ. Sahajātā āsavasampayuttā khandhā ca mahābhūtā ca cittasamuṭṭhānānaṃ rūpānaṃ domanassa-vicikicchā-uddhacca-sahagatā khandhā ca moho ca cittasamuṭṭhānānaṃ rūpānaṃ atthipaccayena paccayo. Domanassa- vicikicchā-uddhaccasahagatā khandhā ca vatthu ca mohassa atthipaccayena paccayo. Pacchājātā āsavasampayuttā khandhā ca kabaḷiṃkāro āhāro ca imassa kāyassa atthipaccayena paccayo.
Pacchājātā āsavasampayuttā khandhā ca rūpajīvitindriyañ ca kaṭattā rūpānaṃ atthipaccayena paccayo.
     9. Āsavasampayutto ca . . . āsavasampayuttassa ca . . .
     Sahajātaṃ, purejātaṃ. Sahajāto domanassa-vicikicchāuddhacca-sahagato eko khandho ca moho ca tiṇṇannaṃ khandhānaṃ cittasamuṭṭhānānañ ca rūpānaṃ atthipaccayena paccayo; dve . . . pe . . .
          Hetuyā nava,                     purejāte tīṇi,
          ārammaṇe nava,                    pacchājāte tīṇi,
          adhipatiyā pañca,                āsevane nava,
          anantare nava,                    kamme cattāri,
          samanantare nava,                vipāke ekaṃ,

          nissaye nava,                     jhāne cattāri,
          upanissaye nava,                magge cattāri,

          sampayutte cha,                natthiyā nava,

          atthiyā nava,                     avigate nava.

                               205
                               [XX.
                          SAṂYOJANA-DUKAṂ]
     1. Saṃyojanaṃ dhammaṃ paṭicca saṃyojano dhammo uppajjati hetupaccayā.
     Kāmarāgasaṃyojanaṃ paṭicca diṭṭhisaṃyojanaṃ avijjāsaṃyojanaṃ. Kāmarāgasaṃyojanaṃ paṭicca sīlabbataparāmāsasaṃyojanaṃ avijjāsaṃyojanaṃ. Kāmarāgasaṃyojanaṃ paṭicca mānasaṃyojanaṃ avijjāsaṃyojanaṃ. Kāmarāgasaṃyojanaṃ paṭicca avijjāsaṃyojanaṃ. Paṭighasaṃyojanaṃ paṭicca issāsaṃyojanaṃ avijjāsaṃyojanaṃ. Paṭighasaṃyojanaṃ paṭicca macchariyasaṃyojanaṃ avijjāsaṃyojanaṃ.
Paṭighasaṃyojanaṃ paṭicca avijjāsaṃyojanaṃ. Mānasaṃyojanaṃ paṭicca bhavarāgasaṃyojanaṃ avijjāsaṃyojanaṃ.
Bhavarāgasaṃyojanaṃ paṭicca avijjāsaṃyojanaṃ. Vicikicchāsaṃyojanaṃ paṭicca avijjāsaṃyojanaṃ.
     2. Saṃyojanaṃ dhammaṃ paṭicca nosaṃyojano dhammo uppajjati hetupaccayā.
     Saṃyojane paṭicca sampayuttakā khandhā cittasamuṭṭhānañ ca rūpaṃ.
     3. Saṃyojanaṃ dhammaṃ paṭicca saṃyojano ca nosaṃyojano ca dhammā uppajjanti hetupaccayā.
     Kāmarāgasaṃyojanaṃ paṭicca diṭṭhisaṃyojanaṃ avijjāsaṃyojanaṃ sampayuttakā ca khandhā cittasamuṭṭhānañ ca rūpaṃ . . . (cakkaṃ bandhitabbaṃ) . . .


[page 206]
206                         Saṃyojanadukaṃ.
     4. Nosaṃyojanaṃ dhammaṃ paṭicca nosaṃyojano dhammo uppajjati hetupaccayā.
     Nosaṃyojanaṃ ekaṃ khandhaṃ paṭicca tayo khandhā cittasamuṭṭhānañ ca rūpaṃ; dve . . . Paṭisandhikkhaṇe khandhe paṭica vatthu, vatthuṃ paṭicca khandhā; ekaṃ mahābhūtaṃ . . . pe . . . mahābhūte paṭicca cittasamuṭṭhānaṃ rūpaṃ kaṭattā rūpaṃ upādā rūpaṃ.
     5. Nosaṃyojanaṃ dhammaṃ paṭicca saṃyojano dhammo uppajjati hetupaccayā.
     Nosaṃyojane khandhe paṭicca saṃyojanā.
     6. Nosaṃyojanaṃ dhammaṃ paṭicca saṃyojano ca nosaṃyojano ca dhammā uppajjanti hetupaccayā.
     Nosaṃyojanaṃ ekaṃ khandhaṃ paṭicca tayo khandhā saṃyojanā cittasamuṭṭhānañ ca rūpaṃ; dve . . .
     7. Saṃyojananañ ca nosaṃyojanañ ca dhammaṃ paṭicca saṃyojano dhammo uppajjati hetupaccayā.
     Kāmarāgasaṃyojanañ ca sampayuttake ca khandhe paṭicca diṭṭhisaṃyojanaṃ avijjāsaṃyojanaṃ . . . (cakkaṃ bandhitabbaṃ) . . .
     8. Saṃyojanañ ca nosaṃyojanañ ca dhammaṃ paṭicca nosaṃyojano dhammo uppajjati hetupaccayā.
     Nosaṃyojanaṃ ekaṃ khandhañ ca saṃyojane ca paṭicca tayo khandhā cittasamuṭṭhānañ ca rūpaṃ; dve . . .
     9. Saṃyojanañ ca nosaṃyojanañ ca dhammaṃ paṭicca saṃyojano ca nosaṃyojano ca dhammā uppajjanti hetupaccayā.
     Nosaṃyojanaṃ ekaṃ khandhañ ca kāmarāgasaṃyojanañ ca paṭicca tayo khandhā diṭṭhisaṃyojanaṃ avijjāsaṃyojanaṃ cittasamuṭṭhānañ ca rūpaṃ . . . (cakkaṃ bandhitabbaṃ.
Saṃkhittaṃ. Arammaṇapaccaye rūpaṃ natthi. Adhipatipaccayo hetusadiso. Vicikicchāsaṃyojanaṃ natthi).
     . . . anantarapaccayā . . . avigatapaccayā. . . .
          Hetuyā nava,                     sabbattha nava;
          ārammaṇe nava,                    vipāke-ekaṃ,
          adhipatiyā nava,                āhāre nava,
          anantare nava,                    avigate nava.

     1. Saṃyojanaṃ dhammaṃ paṭicca saṃyojano dhammo uppajjati nahetupaccayā.

     4. Nosaṃyojanaṃ dhammaṃ paṭicca nosaṃyojano dhammo uppajjati hetupaccayā.
     Ahetukaṃ nosaṃyojanaṃ ekaṃ khandhaṃ paṭicca tayo khandhā cittasamuṭṭhānañ ca rūpaṃ; dve . . . (yāva asaññasattā).

     Vicikicchāsahagati uddhaccasahagate khandhe paṭicca avijjāsaṃyojanaṃ.

          nārammaṇe tīṇi,                navipāke nava,

          na-aññamaññe tīṇi,                namagge ekaṃ,

          napacchājāte nava,                nonatthiyā tīṇi,
          nāsevane nava,                    novigate tīṇi.
     Hetupaccayā, nārammaṇe tīṇi, nādhipatiyā nava, . . .
(evaṃ sesañ ca gaṇetabbaṃ).

          vipāke ekaṃ,                     avigate cattāri.

Vatthuṃ paccayā saṃyojanā sampayuttakā khandhā.

Saṃyojanasampayutte khandhe ārabbha saṃyojanavippayuttā khandhā ca moho ca uppajjanti . . . (mūlaṃ kātabbaṃ). Saṃyojanasampayutte khandhe ārabbha uddhaccasahagatā khandhā ca moho ca uppajjanti.
     4. Saṃyojanavippayutto dhammo saṃyojanavippayuttassa . . .
     Dānaṃ datvā sīlaṃ uposathakammaṃ taṃ paccavekkhati,
pubbe suciṇṇāni paccavekkhati, jhānā vuṭṭhahitvā jhānaṃ paccavekkhati. Ariyā maggā vuṭṭhahitvā maggaṃ paccavekkhanti, phalaṃ nibbānaṃ paccavekkhanti. Nibbānaṃ gotrabhussa vodānassa maggassa phalassa āvajjanāya ārammaṇapaccayena paccayo. Ariyā saṃyojanavippayutte pahīnakilese paccavekkhanti, vikkhambhitakilese paccavekkhanti,
pubbe samudāciṇṇe kilesa jānanti, cakkhuṃ . . . pe . . .
vatthuṃ saṃyojanavippayutte khandhe ca mohañ ca aniccato . . . pe . . . vipassanti. Dibbena cakkhunā rūpaṃ passati,
dibbāya sotadhātuyā saddaṃ suṇāti, cetopariyāñāṇena saṃyojanavippayuttacittasamaṃgissa cittaṃ jānāti;

226           Saṃyojanasampayuttadukaṃ.

     Dānaṃ sīlaṃ uposathakammaṃ . . . pubbe suciṇṇāni . . .
jhānā vuṭṭhahitvā jhānaṃ . . . cakkhuṃ . . . pe . . . vatthuṃ saṃyojanavippayutte khandhe ca mohañ ca assādeti abhinandati, taṃ ārabbha rāgo . . . pe . . . domanassaṃ uppajjati.
     6. Saṃyojanavippayutto dhammo saṃyojanasampayuttassa ca . . .
     Cakkhuṃ . . . pe . . . vatthuṃ saṃyojanavippayutte khandhe ārabbha uddhaccasahagatā khandhā ca moho ca uppajjanti.
     7. Saṃyojanasampayutto ca saṃyojanavippayutto ca . . .
     Uddhaccasahagate khandhe ca mohañ ca ārabbha saṃyojanasampayuttā khandhā uppajjanti . . . (mūlaṃ kātabbaṃ).
Uddhaccasahagate . . . saṃyojanavippayuttā khandhā ca moho ca uppajjanti . . . (mūlaṃ kātabbaṃ). Uddhaccasahagate khandhe ca mohañ ca ārabbha uddhaccasahagatā khandhā ca moho ca uppajjanti.
     1. Saṃyojanasampayutto dhammo saṃyojanasampayuttassa dhammassa adhipatipaccayena paccayo.
     Ārammaṇādhipati, sahajātādhipati. Ārammaṇādhipati:-- rāgaṃ diṭṭhiṃ garuṃ katvā assādeti abhinandati, taṃ garuṃ katvā rāgo, diṭṭhi uppajjati. Sahajātādhipati:-- saṃyojanasampayuttādhipati sampayuttakānaṃ khandhānaṃ adhipatipaccayena paccayo.

                     Anantaravāro.                227
     2. Saṃyojanasampayutto dhammo saṃyojanavippayuttassa . . .
     Sahajātādhipati:-- saṃyojanasampayuttādhipati cittasamuṭṭhānānaṃ rūpānaṃ adhipatipaccayena paccayo.
     3. Saṃyojanasampayutto dhammo saṃyojanasampayuttassa ca . . .
     Sahajātādhipati:-- . . . khandhānaṃ cittasamuṭṭhānānañ ca rūpānaṃ adhipatipaccayena paccayo.
     4. Saṃyojanavippayutto dhammo . . .
     Ārammaṇādhipati, sahajātādhipati. Ārammaṇādhipati:
-- dānaṃ datvā sīlaṃ uposathakammaṃ taṃ garuṃ katvā paccavekkhati, pubbe suciṇṇāni . . . jhānā vuṭṭhahitvā . . .
Ariyā maggā . . . phalaṃ . . . nibbānaṃ gotrabhussa vodānassa maggassa phalassa abhipatipaccayena paccayo. Sahajātādhipati:-- saṃyojanavippayuttādhipati . . .
     5. Saṃyojanavippayutto dhammo . . .
     Ārammaṇādhipati:-- dānaṃ . . . katvā assādeti abhi nandati; taṃ garuṃ katvā rāgo uppajjati, diṭṭhi uppajjati;
pubbe suciṇṇāni . . . jhānā . . . cakkhuṃ . . . pe . . .
vatthuṃ saṃyojanavippayutte khandhe garuṃ katvā assādeti abhinandati . . . uppajjati.
     1. Saṃyojanasampayutto dhammo saṃyojanasampayuttassa dhammassa anantarapaccayena paccayo.
     Purimā purimā saṃyojanasampayuttā khandhā pacchimānaṃ pacchimānaṃ saṃyojanasampayuttānaṃ khandhānaṃ anantarapaccayena paccayo.
     2. Saṃyojanasampayutto dhammo . . .
     Purimā purimā uddhaccasahagatā khandhā pacchimassa pacchimassa uddhaccasahagatassa mohassa anantarapaccayena paccayo.
     Saṃyojanasampayuttā khandhā vuṭṭhānassa anantarapaccayena paccayo.

nissayapaccayena paccayo (nava) . . . upanissayapaccayena paccayo.

     Ārammaṇūpanissayo, anantarūpanissayo, pakatūpanissayo; . . . pe . . . Pakatūpanissayo:-- saṃyojanasampayuttā khandhā saṃyojanasampayuttānaṃ khandhānaṃ upanissayapaccayena paccayo.
     2. Saṃyojanasampayutto dhammo . . .

pe . . . samāpattiṃ uppādeti; saddhā . . . pe . . . senāsanaṃ maho ca saddhāya . . . pe . . . phalasamāpattiyā upanissayapaccayena paccayo.

230                Saṃyojanasampayuttadukaṃ.

     Anantarūpanissayo . . . moho ca uddhaccasahagatānaṃ khandhānaṃ mohassa ca upanissayapaccayena paccayo.
     4. Saṃyojanavippayutto dhammo saṃyojanavippayuttassa dhammassa purejātapaccayena paccayo.
     Ārammaṇapurejātaṃ, vatthupurejātaṃ. Ārammaṇapurejātaṃ:-- cakkhuṃ . . . pe . . . vatthuṃ aniccato . . . pe . . . dibbena cakkhunā rūpaṃ passati, dibbāya sotadhātuyā saddaṃ suṇāti; rūpāyatanaṃ cakkhuviññāṇassa . . . pe . . .
phoṭṭhabbāyatanaṃ kāyaviññāṇassa . . . Vatthupurejātaṃ:-- cakkhāyatanaṃ cakkhuviññāṇassa . . . pe . . . kāyāyatanaṃ kāyaviññāṇassa, vatthu saṃyojanavippayuttānaṃ khandhānaṃ mohassa ca purejātapaccayena paccayo.
     5. Saṃyojanavippayutto dhammo saṃyojanasampayuttassa . . .
     Ārammaṇapurejātaṃ . . . pe . . . vatthuṃ assādeti abhinandati, taṃ ārabbha rāgo . . . pe . . . domanassaṃ uppajjati. Vatthupurejātaṃ:-- vatthuṃ saṃyojanasampayuttānaṃ khandhānaṃ purejātapaccayena paccayo.
     6. Saṃyojanavippayutto dhammo . . .

     2. Saṃyojanasampayutto dhammo saṃyojanavippayuttassa dhammassa pacchājātapaccayena paccayo.

                     Kammavāro.                         231
     Pacchājātā saṃyojanasampayuttā khandhā purejātassa imassa kāyassa pacchājārapaccayena paccayo.
     4. Saṃyojanavippayutto dhammo . . .
     Pacchājārā saṃyojanavippayuttā khandhā ca moho ca purejātassa . . .
     8. Saṃyojanasampayutto ca saṃyojanavippayutto ca dhammā saṃyojanavippayuttassa . . .
     Pacchājātā uddhaccasahagatā khandhā ca moho ca purejātassa imassa kāyassa pacchājātapaccayena paccayo.
     1. Saṃyojanasampayutto dhammo saṃyojanasampayuttassa dhammassa āsevanapaccayena paccayo . . . (nava.
Āvajjanā pi vuṭṭhānam pi natthi) . . . kammapaccayena paccayo.
     Saṃyojanasampayuttā cetanā saṃyojanasampayuttānaṃ khandhānaṃ kammapaccayena paccayo.
     2. Saṃyojanasampayutto dhammo . . .
     Sahajātā, nānākhaṇikā. Sahajātā:-- saṃyojanasampayuttā cetanā cittasamuṭṭhānānaṃ rūpānaṃ kammapaccayena paccayo. Uddhaccasahagatā cetanā mohassa cittasamuṭṭhānañ ca rūpānaṃ kammapaccayena paccayo.
Nānākhaṇikā:-- saṃyojanasampayuttā cetanā vipākānaṃ khandhānaṃ kaṭattā ca rūpānaṃ kammapaccayena paccayo.
     3. Saṃyojanasampayutto dhammo saṃyojanasampayuttassa ca . . .
     Saṃyojanasampayutto cetanā sampayuttakānaṃ khandhānaṃ cittasamuṭṭhānānañ ca rūpānaṃ kammapaccayena paccayo. Uddhaccasahagatā cetanā sampayuttakānaṃ khandhānaṃ mohassa ca cittasamuṭṭhānānañ ca . . .
     4. Saṃyojanavippayutto dhammo . . .
     Sahajātā, nānākhaṇikā. Sahajātā saṃyojanavippayuttā cetanā . . . Paṭisandhikkhaṇe nānākhaṇikā saṃyojanavippayuttā cetanā vipākānaṃ khandhānaṃ kaṭattā ca rūpānaṃ kammapaccayena paccayo.

232           Saṃyojanasampayuttadukaṃ.
     4. Saṃyojanavippayutto dhammo saṃyojanavippayuttassa dhammassa vipākapaccayena paccayo . . . (ekaṃ).
     1. Saṃyojanasampayutto dhammo saṃyojanasampayuttassa dhammassa āhārapaccayena paccayo . . . (cattāri) . . .
indriya- . . . (cattāri) . . . jhāna- . . . (cattāri) . . . magga. . . (cattāri) . . . sampayuttapaccayena paccayo . . . (cha).
     2. Saṃyojanasampayutto dhammo saṃyojanavippayuttassa dhammassa vippayuttapaccayena paccayo.
     Sahajātaṃ, pacchājātaṃ . . . (saṃkhittaṃ).
     4. Saṃyojanavippayutto dhammo . . . vippayuttapaccayena paccayo.
     Sahajātaṃ, purejātaṃ, pacchājātaṃ . . . (saṃkhittaṃ).
     5. Saṃyojanavippayutto dhammo . . .
     Purejātaṃ vatthu saṃyojanasampayuttānaṃ khandhānaṃ vippayuttapaccayena paccayo.
     6. Saṃyojanavippayutto dhammo . . .
     Purejātaṃ vatthu uddhaccasahagatānaṃ khandhānaṃ mohassa ca vippayuttapaccayena paccayo.
     8. Saṃyojanasampayutto ca saṃyojanavippayutto ca dhammā saṃyojanavippayuttassa dhammassa vippayuttapaccayena paccayo.
     Sahajātaṃ, pacchājātaṃ . . . (saṃkhittaṃ).
     1. Saṃyojanasampayutto dhammo saṃyojanasampayuttassa dhammassa atthipaccayena paccayo . . . (ekaṃ,
paṭiccasadisaṃ).
     2. Saṃyojanasampayutto dhammo . . .
     Sahajātaṃ, pacchājātaṃ. Sahajātā saṃyojanasampayuttā khandhā cittasamuṭṭhānānaṃ rūpānaṃ atthipaccayena paccayo. Uddhaccasahagatā khandhā mohassa cittasamuṭṭhānānañ ca rūpānaṃ atthipaccayena paccayo. Pacchājātā saṃyojanasampayuttā khandhā purejātassa imassa kāyassa atthipaccayena paccayo.
     3. Saṃyojanasampayutto dhammo . . .


[page 233]
                     Atthivāro.                     233
     Purejātaṃ vatthu saṃyojanasampayuttānaṃ khandhānaṃ vippayuttapaccayena paccayo.
     Saṃyojanasampayutto eko khandho tiṇṇannaṃ khandhānaṃ cittasamuṭṭhānānañ ca rūpānaṃ atthipaccayena paccayo; dve . . . Uddhaccasahagato eko khandho tiṇṇannaṃ khandhānaṃ mohassa ca cittasamuṭṭhānānañ ca . . .
     4. Saṃyojanavippayutto dhammo . . .
     Sahajātaṃ. purejātaṃ. pacchājātaṃ āhāraṃ indriyaṃ . . .
(saṃkhittaṃ, vitthāretabbaṃ).
     5. Saṃyojanavippayutto dhammo . . .
     Sahajātaṃ. purejātaṃ. Sahajāto uddhaccasahagato moho sampayuttānaṃ khandhānaṃ atthipaccayena paccayo.
Purejātaṃ:-- cakkhuṃ . . . pe . . . vatthuṃ assādeti abhinandati, taṃ ārabbha rāgo . . . pe . . . domanassaṃ uppajjati. Vatthu saṃyojanasampayuttānaṃ khandhānaṃ atthipaccayena paccayo.
     6. Saṃyojanavippayutto dhammo . . .
     Sahajātaṃ . . . khandhānaṃ cittasamuṭṭhānānañ ca rūpānaṃ atthipaccayena paccayo. Purejātaṃ:-- cakkhuṃ . . . pe . . . vattuṃ ārabbha uddhaccasahagatā khandhā ca moho ca uppajjanti. Vatthu uddhaccasahagatānaṃ khandhānaṃ mohassa ca atthipaccayena paccayo.
     7. Saṃyojanasampayutto ca saṃyojanavippayutto ca . . .
     Sahajātaṃ, purejātaṃ. Sahajāto saṃyojanasampayutto eko khandho ca vatthu ca tiṇṇannaṃ khandhānaṃ atthipaccayena paccayo; dve . . . Uddhaccasahagato eko khandho ca moho ca tiṇṇannaṃ . . .
     8. Saṃyojanasampayutto ca . . .
     Sahajātaṃ. purejātaṃ. pacchājātaṃ āhāraṃ indriyaṃ.
Sahajātā saṃyojanasampayuttā khandhā ca mahābhūtā ca cittasamuṭṭhānānaṃ rūpānaṃ atthipaccayena paccayo.
Uddhaccasahagatā khandhā ca moho ca cittasamuṭṭhānānaṃ . . . Uddhaccasahagatā khandhā ca vatthu ca mohassa atthipaccayena paccayo. Pacchājātā:-- uddhaccasahagatā khandhā ca moho ca purejātassa imassa kāyassa atthipaccayena paccayo.


[page 234]
234                Saṃyojanasampayuttadukaṃ.
[... content straddling page break has been moved to the page above ...] Pacchājātā saṃyojanasampayuttā khandhā ca kabaḷiṃkāro āhāro ca imassa . . . Pacchājātā saṃyojanasampayuttā khandhā ca rūpajīvitindriyañ ca kaṭattā rūpānaṃ atthipaccayena paccayo.
     9. Saṃyojanasampayutto ca . . .
     Sahajātaṃ. purejātaṃ. Sahajāto uddhaccasahagato eko khandho ca moho ca tiṇṇannaṃ khandhānaṃ cittasamuṭṭhānānañ ca rūpānaṃ atthipaccayena paccayo; dve . . .
Sahajāto uddhaccasahagato eko khandho ca vatthu ca tiṇṇannaṃ khandhānaṃ mohassa ca atthipaccayena paccayo; dve . . . natthipaccayena paccayo . . . vigata- . . .
avigatapaccayena paccayo . . .
          Hetuyā cha.                     kamme cattāri,
          ārammaṇe nava,                    vipāke ekaṃ,
          adhipatiyā pañca,                āhāre cattāri,
          anantare nava,                    indriye cattāri,
          samanantare nava,                jhāni cattāri,
          sahajāte nava,                    magge cattāri,
          aññanaññe cha,                sampayutte cha,
          nissaye nava,                     vippayutte pañca,
          upanissaye nava,                atthiyā nava,
          purejāte tīṇi,                    natthiyā nava,
          pacchājāte tīṇi,                vigate nava,
          āsevane nava,                     avigate nava.
     1. Saṃyojanasampayutto dhammo . . . ārammaṇa- . . .
sahajāta . . . upanissayapaccayena paccayo.
     2. Saṃyojanasampayutto dhammo . . . ārammaṇa- . . .
pacchājāta- . . . kammapaccayena paccayo.

     1. Saṃyojanañ ceva saṃyojaniyañ ca dhammaṃ paṭicca saṃyojano ceva saṃyojaniyo ca dhammo uppajjati hetupaccayā.

     2. Saṃyojanañ ceva saṃyojaniyañ dhammaṃ paṭicca saṃyojaniyo ceva no ca saṃyojano dhammo uppajjati hetupaccayā.
     Saṃyojane paṭicca sampayuttakā khandhā cittasamuṭṭhānañ ca rūpaṃ.
     3. Saṃyojanañ ceva saṃyojaniyañ ca dhammaṃ paṭicca saṃyojano ceva saṃyojaniyo ca saṃyojaniyo ceva no ca saṃyojano ca dhammā uppajjanti hetupaccayā.
     Kāmarāgasaṃyojanaṃ paṭicca diṭṭhisaṃyojanaṃ avijjāsaṃyojanaṃ sampayuttakā ca khandhā cittasamuṭṭhānañ ca rūpaṃ . . . (cakkaṃ).

(paṭisandhi yāva mahābhūtā).

                         [XXVI.
                    GANTHA-DUKAṂ.]
     1. Ganthaṃ dhammaṃ paṭicca gantho dhammo uppajjati hetupaccayā.
     Sīlabbataparāmāsakāyaganthaṃ paṭicca abhijjhākāyagantho, abhijjhākāyaganthaṃ paṭicca sīlabbataparāmāsakāyagantho, idaṃsaccābhinivesakāyaganthaṃ paṭicca abhijjhākāyagantho, abhijjhākāyaganthaṃ paṭicca idaṃsaccabhinivesakāyagantho.
     2. Ganthaṃ dhammaṃ paṭicca nogantho dhammo uppajjati hetupaccayā.
     Ganthe paṭicca sampayuttakā khandhā cittasamuṭṭhānañ ca rūpaṃ.
     3. Ganthaṃ dhammaṃ paṭicca gantho ca nogantho ca dhammā uppajjanti hetupaccayā.
     Sīlabbataparāmāsakāyaganthaṃ paṭicca abhijjhākāyagantho sampayuttakā ca khandhā cittasamuṭṭhānañ ca rūpaṃ . . . (cakkaṃ).
     4. Noganthaṃ dhammaṃ paṭicca nogantho dhammo . . .
     Noganthaṃ ekaṃ khandhaṃ paṭicca tayo khandhā cittasamuṭṭhānañ ca rūpaṃ; dve . . . Paṭisandhikkhaṇe khandhe paṭicca vatthu, vatthuṃ paṭicca khandhā; ekaṃ mahābhūtaṃ . . . pe . . .
     5. Noganthaṃ dhammaṃ paṭicca gantho dhammo . . .
     Noganthe khandhe paṭicca ganthā.


[page 246]
246                     Ganthadukaṃ.
     6. Noganthaṃ dhammaṃ paṭicca gantho ca nogantho ca dhammā . . .
     Noganthaṃ ekaṃ khandhaṃ paṭicca tayo khandhā ganthā ca cittasamuṭṭhānañ ca rūpaṃ; dve . . .
     7. Ganthañ ca noganthañ ca dhammaṃ paṭicca gantho . . .
     Sīlabbataparāmāsakāyaganthañ ca sampayuttake ca khandhe paṭicca abhijjhākāyagantho . . . (cakkaṃ).
     8. Ganthañ ca noganthañ ca dhammaṃ paṭicca nogantho . . .
     Noganthaṃ ekaṃ khandhañ ca ganthe ca paṭicca tayo khandhā cittasamuṭṭhānañ ca rūpaṃ; dve . . .
     9. Ganthañ ca . . . paṭicca gantho ca nogantho ca dhammā uppajjanti hetupaccayā.
     Noganthaṃ ekaṃ khandhañ ca sīlabbataparāmāsakāyaganthañ ca paṭicca tayo khandhā abhijjhākāyagantho cittasamuṭṭhānañ ca rūpaṃ; dve . . . (cakkaṃ; saṃkhittaṃ) . . .
ārammaṇapaccayā . . . avigatapaccayā.
          Hetuyā nava,                     vipāke ekaṃ,
          ārammaṇe nava,                    āhāre nava,
          adhipatiyā nava,                avigate nava.
          sabbattha nava;
     4. Noganthaṃ dhammaṃ paṭicca nogantho dhammo uppajjati nahetupaccayā.
     Ahetukaṃ noganthaṃ ekaṃ khandhaṃ paṭicca tayo khandhā cittasamuṭṭhānañ ca rūpaṃ; dve . . . (ahetukapaṭisandhi yūva asaññasattā). Vicikicchāsahagato uddhaccasahagate khandhe paṭicca vicikicchāsahagato uddhaccasahagato moho.
     2. Ganthaṃ dhammaṃ paṭicca nogantho dhammo uppajjati nārammaṇapaccayā.
     Ganthe paṭicca cittasamuṭṭhānaṃ rūpaṃ.
     4. Noganthaṃ dhammaṃ paṭicca nogantho . . .

     8. Ganthañ ca noganthañ ca dhammaṃ paṭicca nogantho dhammo uppajjati nārammaṇapaccayā.

(tīṇi).

                         Hetuvāro.                          249
     9. Ganthañ ca noganthañ ca dhammaṃ paccayā gantho ca nogantho ca dhammā uppajjanti hetupaccayā.

Cakkhāyatanaṃ paccayā cakkhuviññāṇaṃ, . . . kāyāyatanaṃ paccayā kāyaviññāṇaṃ. Vatthuṃ paccayā ahetuka noganthā khandhā. Vicikicchāsahagate uddhaccasahagate khandhe ca vatthuñ ca paccayā vicikicchāsahagato uddhaccasahagato moho . . . (saṃkhittaṃ).
     Nahetuyā ekaṃ, nārammaṇe tīṇi, nādhipatiyā nava:-- evaṃ gaṇetabbaṃ.
     Hetupaccayā, nārammaṇe tīṇi, nādhipatiyā nava, novigate tīṇi.
     Nahetupaccayā, ārammaṇe ekaṃ, avigate ekaṃ.
     (Nissayavāro pi paccayavārasadiso. Saṃsaṭṭhavāro pi sampayuttavāro pi, nava pañhā kātabbā. Rūpaṃ natthi.)

     Ganthā hetū sampayuttakānaṃ khandhānaṃ hetupaccayena paccayo.

dibbena cakkhunā rūpaṃ passati, dibbāya sotadhātuyā saddaṃ suṇāti, cetopariyañāṇena noganthacittasamaṃgissa cittaṃ jānāti. Ākāsānañcāyatanaṃ viññāṇañcāyatanassa, ākiñcaññāyatanaṃ nevasaññānāsaññāyatanassa,
rūpāyatanaṃ cakkhuviññāṇassa . . . phoṭṭhabbāyatanaṃ kāyaviññāṇassa, noganthā khandhā iddhividhañāṇassa cetopariyañāṇassa pubbenivāsānussatiñāṇassa yathākammūpagañāṇassa anāgataṃsañāṇassa āvajjanāya ārammaṇapaccayena paccayo.

[... content straddling page break has been moved to the page above ...] Pacchājātā ganthā sampayuttakā ca khandhā purejātassa imassa kāyassa atthipaccayena paccayo. Pacchājātā ganthā ca kavaḷiṃkāro āhāro ca imassa . . . Pacchājātā ganthā ca rūpajīvitindriyañ ca kaṭattā rūpānaṃ atthipaccayena paccayo.
     9. Gantho ca . . . dhammā ganthassa ca . . .
     Sahajātaṃ, purejātaṃ. Sahajāto nogantho eko khandho ca sīlabbataparāmāsakāyagantho ca tiṇṇannaṃ khandhānaṃ abhijjhākāyaganthassa ca cittasamuṭṭhānānañ ca rūpānaṃ atthipaccayena paccayo . . . (cakkaṃ). Sahajāto sīlabbataparāmāsakāyagantho ca vatthu ca abhijjhākāyaganthassa ca sampayuttakānañ ca khandhānaṃ atthipaccayena paccayo . . . (cakkaṃ).
          Hetuyā nava,                     indriye tīṇi,
          ārammaṇe nava,                    jhāne tīṇi,
          sabbattha nava;                magge nava,
          upanissaye nava,                sampayutte nava,
          purejāte tīṇi,                    vippayutte pañca,
          pacchājāte tīṇi,                atthiyā nava,
          āsevane nava,                    natthiyā nava,
          kamme tīṇi,                     vigate nava,
          vipāke ekaṃ,                     avigate nava.
          āhāre tīṇi,
     1. Gantho dhammo ganthassa dhammassa ārammaṇa-,
sahajāta-, upanissayapaccayena paccayo.
     2. Gantho dhammo noganthassa dhammassa ārammaṇasahajāta-, upanissaya-, pacchājātapaccayena paccayo.
     3. Gantho dhammo ganthassa ca noganthassa ca dhammassa . . .
     4. Nogantho dhammo noganthassa dhammassa ārammaṇa-, sahajāta-, upanissaya-, purejāta-, pacchājāta-,
kamma-, āhāra-, indriyapaccayena paccayo.

sahajāta-, upanissaya-, purejātapaccayena paccayo.

     7. Gantho ca nogantho ca dhammā ganthassa . . .
     8. Gantho ca nogantho ca dhammā noganthassa . . .
     9. Gantho ca nogantho ca dhammā ganthassa ca noganthassa ca . . .
          Nahetuyā nava,                    sabbattha nava;
          nārammaṇe nava,                no-avigate nava.
          Hetupaccayā, nārammaṇe           namagge nava,
           nava (saṃkhittaṃ),           nasampayutte tīṇi,
          nasamanantare nava,               navippayutte nava,

          Nahetupaccayā, ārammaṇe           adhipatiyā nava,
           nava,
     (anulomapadāni paripuṇṇāni kātabbāni),
                          avigate nava.

                          [XXVIII.
                GANTHASAMPAYUTTA-DUKAṂ.]
     1. Ganthasampayuttaṃ dhammaṃ paṭicca ganthasampayutto dhammo uppajjati hetupaccayā.
     Ganthasampayuttaṃ ekaṃ khandhaṃ paṭicca tayo khandhā; dve . . .
     2. Ganthasampayuttaṃ . . . ganthavippayutto . . .
     Ganthasampayutte khandhe paṭicca cittasamuṭṭhānaṃ rūpaṃ. Diṭṭhigatavippayuttalobhasahagate khandhe paṭicca lobho cittasamuṭṭhānañ ca rūpaṃ. Domanassasahagate khandhe paṭicca paṭighaṃ cittasamuṭṭhānañ ca rūpaṃ.
     3. Ganthasampayuttaṃ . . . ganthasampayutto ca . . .
     Ganthasampayuttaṃ ekaṃ . . . khandhā cittasamuṭṭhānañ ca rūpaṃ; dve . . . Diṭṭhigatavippayuttalobhasahagataṃ ekaṃ khandhaṃ paṭicca tayo khandhā lobho ca cittasamuṭṭhānañ ca rūpaṃ; dve . . . Domanassasahagataṃ ekaṃ khandhaṃ paṭicca tayo khandhā paṭighañ ca cittasamuṭṭhānañ ca rūpaṃ; dve . . .
     4. Ganthavippayuttaṃ . . . ganthavippayutto . . .
     Ganthavippayuttaṃ ekaṃ khandhaṃ paṭicca tayo khandhā cittasamuṭṭhānañ ca rūpaṃ; dve . . . Diṭṭhigatavippayuttaṃ lobhaṃ paṭicca cittasamuṭṭhānaṃ rūpaṃ. Paṭighaṃ paṭicca cittasamuṭṭhānaṃ rūpaṃ. Paṭisandhikkhaṇe khandhe paṭicca . . . (saṃkhittaṃ).

                          Paṭiccavāro.                     261
     5. Ganthavippayuttaṃ dhammaṃ paṭicca . . .
     Diṭṭhiganthavippayuttaṃ lobhaṃ paṭicca sampayuttakā khandhā. Paṭighaṃ paṭicca sampayuttakā khandhā.
     6. Ganthavippayuttaṃ . . . ganthasampayutto ca . . .
     Diṭṭhigatavippayuttaṃ lobhaṃ paṭicca sampayuttakā khandhā cittasamuṭṭhānañ ca rūpaṃ. Paṭighaṃ paṭicca sampayuttakā khandhā cittasamuṭṭhānañ ca rūpaṃ.
     7. Ganthasampayuttañ ca ganthavippayuttañ ca dhammaṃ . . .
     Diṭṭhigatavippayuttalobhasahagataṃ ekaṃ khandhañ ca lobhañ ca paṭicca tayo khandhā; dve . . . Domanassasahagataṃ ekaṃ khandhañ ca paṭighañ ca paṭicca tayo khandhā; dve . . .
     8. Ganthasampayuttañ ca ganthavippayuttañ ca . . .
     Ganthasampayutte khandhe ca mahābhūte ca paṭicca cittasamuṭṭhānaṃ rūpaṃ. Diṭṭhigatavippayuttalobhasahagate khandhe ca lobhañ ca paṭicca cittasamuṭṭhānaṃ rūpaṃ.
Domanassasahagate khandhe ca paṭighañ ca paṭicca cittasamuṭṭhānaṃ rūpaṃ.
     9. Ganthasampayuttañ ca ganthavippayuttañ ca dhammaṃ paṭicca ganthasampayutto ca ganthavippayutto ca dhammā uppajjanti hetupaccayā.
     Diṭṭhigatavippayuttalobhasahagataṃ . . . khandhā cittasamuṭṭhānañ ca rūpaṃ. Domanassasahagataṃ . . . tayo khandhā cittasamuṭṭhānañ ca rūpaṃ; dve . . .
     1. Ganthasampayuttaṃ dhammaṃ paṭicca ganthasampayutto dhammo uppajjati ārammaṇapaccayā.

     6. Ganthavippayuttaṃ . . . ganthasampayutto ca . . .
     Vatthuṃ paccayā ganthasampayuttā khandhā. Mahābhūte paccayā cittasamuṭṭhānaṃ rūpaṃ. Diṭṭhigatavippayuttaṃ lobhaṃ paccayā sampayuttakā khandhā cittasamuṭṭhānañ ca rūpaṃ. Paṭighaṃ paccayā sampayuttakā khandhā cittasamuṭṭhānañ ca rūpaṃ. Vatthuṃ paccayā diṭṭhigatavippayuttalobhasahagatā khandhā ca lobho ca.
Vatthuṃ paccayā domanassasahagatā khandhā ca paṭighañ ca.

Domanassasahagate khandhe ca paṭighañ ca paccayā cittasamuṭṭhānaṃ rūpaṃ. Diṭṭhigatavippayuttalobhasahagate khandhe ca vatthuñ ca paccayā lobho.
Domanassasahagate khandhe ca vatthuñ ca paccayā paṭighaṃ.

     evaṃ gaṇetabbaṃ.

     1. Ganthasampayuttaṃ dhammaṃ saṃsaṭṭho ganthasampayutto dhammo uppajjati hetupaccayā.
     Ganthasampayuttaṃ ekaṃ khandhaṃ saṃsaṭṭhā tayo khandhā; dve . . .

dve . . .

          napacchājāte cha,                namagge ekaṃ,
          nāsevane cha,                     navippayutte cha.
          Hetupaccayā, nādhipatiyā          nāsevane cha,
           cha,                          nakamme cattāri,
          napurejāte cha,                navipāke cha,
          napacchājāte cha,                navippayutte cha;
          Nahetupaccayā, ārammaṇe           anantare ekaṃ,
           ekaṃ,                          avigate ekaṃ.
     1. Ganthasampayutto dhammo ganthasampayuttassa dhammassa hetupaccayena paccayo.
     Ganthasampayuttā hetū sampayuttakānaṃ khandhānaṃ hetupaccayena paccayo.
     2. Ganthasampayutto dhammo ganthavippayuttassa . . .
     Ganthasampayuttā hetū cittasamuṭṭhānānaṃ rūpānaṃ hetupaccayena paccayo.


[page 268]
268                          Ganthasampayuttadukaṃ.
[... content straddling page break has been moved to the page above ...] Diṭṭhigatavippayuttalobhasahagato hetu lobhassa cittasamuṭṭhānānañ ca rūpānaṃ hetupaccayena paccayo. Domanassasahagato hetu paṭighassa cittasamuṭṭhānānañ ca . . .
     3. Ganthasampayutto . . . ganthasampayuttassa ca . . .
     Ganthasampayuttā hetū sampayuttakānaṃ khandhānaṃ cittasamuṭṭhānānañ ca . . . Diṭṭhigatavippayuttalobhasahagato hetu sampayuttakānaṃ khandhānaṃ lobhassa ca cittasamuṭṭhānānañ ca . . . Domanassasahagato hetu sampayuttakānaṃ khandhānaṃ paṭighassa ca cittasamuṭṭhānānañ ca rūpānaṃ hetupaccayena paccayo.
     4. Ganthavippayutto dhammo ganthavippayuttassa . . .
     5Diṭṭhigatavippayutto lobho cittasamuṭṭhānānaṃ . . .
Paṭighaṃ cittasamuṭṭhānānaṃ rūpānaṃ hetupaccayena paccayo. (Paṭisandhi.)
     5. Ganthavippayutto dhammo ganthasampayuttassa . . .
     Diṭṭhigatavippayutto lobho sampayuttakānaṃ khandhānaṃ hetupaccayena paccayo. Paṭighaṃ sampayuttakānaṃ . . .
     6. Ganthavippayutto dhammo ganthasampayuttassa ca . . .
     Diṭṭhigatavippayutto lobho sampayuttakānaṃ khandhānaṃ cittasamuṭṭhānānañ ca rūpānaṃ hetu paccayena paccayo.
Paṭighaṃ sampayuttakānaṃ khandhānaṃ . . .
     7. Ganthasampayutto ca ganthavippayutto ca . . .
     Diṭṭhigatavippayuttalobhasahagato hetu ca lobho ca sampayuttakānaṃ khandhānaṃ hetupaccayena paccayo.
Domanassasahagato hetu ca paṭighañ ca sampayuttakānaṃ . . .
     8. Ganthasampayutto ca ganthavippayutto ca . . .
     Diṭṭhigatavippayuttalobhasahagato hetu ca lobho ca cittasamuṭṭhānānaṃ rūpānaṃ hetupaccayena paccayo.


[page 269]
                          Ārammaṇavāro.                     269
Domanassasahagato hetu ca paṭighañ ca cittasamuṭṭhānānaṃ . . .
     9. Ganthasampayutto ca ganthavippayutto ca . . .
     Diṭṭhigatavippayuttalobhasahagato hetu ca lobho ca sampayuttakānaṃ khandhānaṃ cittasamuṭṭhānānañ ca rūpānaṃ hetupaccayena paccayo. Domanassasahagato hetu ca paṭighañ ca sampayuttakānaṃ . . .
     1. Ganthasampayutto dhammo ganthasampayuttassa dhammassa ārammaṇapaccayena paccayo.
     Ganthasampayutte khandhe ārabbha ganthasampayuttā khandhā uppajjanti . . . (tīsu pi mūlā pucchitabbā).
Ganthasampayutte khandhe ārabbha ganthavippayuttā khandhā uppajjanti. Ganthasampayutte khandhe ārabbha diṭṭhigatavippayuttalobhasahagatā khandhā ca lobho ca uppajjanti. Domanassasahagatā khandhā ca paṭighañ ca uppajjanti.
     4. Ganthavippayutto dhammo ganthavippayuttassa . . .
     Dānaṃ datvā sīlaṃ uposathakammaṃ taṃ paccavekkhati,
pubbe suciṇṇāni paccavekkhati, jhānā vuṭṭhahitvā jhānaṃ paccavekkhati. Āriyā maggā vuṭṭhahitvā maggaṃ paccavekkhanti, phalaṃ paccavekkhanti, nibbānaṃ paccavekkhanti. Nibbānaṃ gotrabhussa vodānassa maggassa phalassa āvajjanāya ārammaṇapaccayena paccayo. Ariyā ganthavippayutte pahīnakilese paccavekkhanti, vikkhambhitakilese paccavekkhanti, pubbe samudāciṇṇe kilese jānanti, cakkhuṃ . . . pe . . . vatthuṃ, ganthavippayutte khandhe ca lobhañ ca paṭighañ ca aniccato vipassanti . . . pe . . . assādeti abhinandati, taṃ ārabbha ganthavippayutto rāgo uppajjati,
. . . pe . . . vicikicchā uddhaccaṃ domanassaṃ uppajjati;
dibbena cakkhunā rūpaṃ passati, dibbāya sotadhātuyā saddaṃ suṇāti, cetopariyañāṇena ganthavippayuttacittasamaṃgissa cittaṃ jānāti. Ākāsānañcāyatanaṃ viññāṇañcāyatanassa, ākiñcaññāyatanaṃ nevasaññānāsaññāyatanassa,
rūpāyatanaṃ cakkhuviññāṇassa . . . phoṭṭhabbāyatanaṃ kāyaviññāṇassa ārammāṇapaccayena paccayo. Ganthavippayuttā khandhā iddhividhañāṇassa cetopariyañāṇassa pubbenivāsānussatiñāṇassa yathākammūpagañāṇassa anāgataṃsañāṇassa āvajjanāya ārammaṇapaccayena paccayo.

     6. Ganthavippayutto dhammo ganthasampayuttassa ca . . .
     Cakkhuṃ. . . . pe . . . vatthuṃ ganthavippayutte khandhe ca lobhañ ca paṭighañ ca ārabbha diṭṭhigatavippayuttalobhasahagatā khandhā ca lobho ca domanassasahagatā khandhā ca paṭighañ ca uppajjanti.
     7. Ganthasampayutto ca ganthavippayutto ca . . .
     Diṭṭhigatavippayuttalobhasahagate khandhe ca lobhañ ca domanassasahagate khandhe ca paṭighañ ca ārabbha ganthasampayuttā khandhā uppajjanti . . . (mūlaṃ pucchitabbaṃ). Diṭṭhigatavippayutta- . . . ārabbha ganthavippayuttā khandhā uppajjanti . . . (mūlaṃ pucchitabbaṃ).
Diṭṭhigatavippayutta- . . . ārabbha diṭṭhigatavippayuttalobhasahagatā khandhā ca lobho ca domanassasahagatā khandhā ca paṭighañ ca uppajjanti.
     1. Ganthasampayutto dhammo ganthasampayuttassa dhammassa adhipatipaccayena paccayo.
     Ārammaṇādhipati, sahajātādhipati. Ārammaṇādhipati:-- ganthasampayutte khandhe garuṃ katvā ganthasampayuttā khandhā uppajjanti. Sahajātādhipati:-- ganthasampayuttādhipati sampayuttakānaṃ khandhānaṃ adhipatipaccayena paccayo.
     2. Ganthasampayutto dhammo ganthavippayuttassa . . .
     Ārammaṇādhipati . . . garuṃ katvā diṭṭhigatavippayutto lobho uppajjati. Sahajātādhipati:-- ganthasampayuttādhipati cittasamuṭṭhānānaṃ rūpānaṃ adhipatipaccayena paccayo. Diṭṭhigatavippayuttalobhasahagatādhipati lobhassa ca cittasamuṭṭhānānañ ca . . . Domanassasahagatādhipati paṭighassa cittasamuṭṭhānānañ ca rūpānaṃ adhipatipaccayena paccayo.

                          Adhipativāro.                     271
[... content straddling page break has been moved to the page above ...]
     3. Ganthasampayutto . . . ganthasampayuttassa ca . . .
     Ārammaṇādhipati . . . garuṃ katvā diṭṭhigatavippayuttalobhasahagatā khandhā ca lobho ca uppajjantiSahajātādhipati:-- diṭṭhigatavippayuttalobhasahagatādhipati sampayuttakānaṃ khandhānaṃ lobhassa ca cittasamuṭṭhānānañ ca rūpānaṃ adhipatipaccayena paccayo.
Domanassasahagatādhipati sampayuttakānaṃ khandhānaṃ paṭighassa ca cittasamuṭṭhānānañ . . .
     4. Ganthavippayutto dhammo ganthavippayuttassa . . .
     Ārammaṇādhipati, sahajātādhipati. Ārammaṇādhipati:-- dānaṃ sīlaṃ uposathakammaṃ taṃ garuṃ katvā paccavekkhati, pubbe suciṇṇāni garuṃ katvā paccavekkhati, jhānā vuṭṭhahitvā jhānaṃ garuṃ katvā paccavekkhanti. Ariyā maggā vuṭṭhahitvā maggaṃ garuṃ katvā paccavekkhanti,
phalaṃ, nibbānaṃ garuṃ katvā paccavekkhanti. Nibbānaṃ gotrabhussa vodānassa maggassa phalassa adhipatipaccayena paccayo. Cakkhuṃ . . . pe . . . vatthuṃ, ganthavippayutte khandhe ca lobhañ ca garuṃ katvā assadeti abhinandati, taṃ garuṃ katvā ganthavippayutto rāgo diṭṭhi uppajjati.
Sahajātādhipati:-- ganthavippayuttādhipati sampayuttakānaṃ khandhānaṃ cittasamuṭṭhānānañ ca rūpānaṃ adhipatipaccayena paccayo.
     5. Ganthavippayutto dhammo ganthasampayuttassa dhammassa . . .
     Ārammaṇādhipati:-- dānaṃ . . . vuṭṭhāhitvā jhānaṃ . . . Cakkhuṃ . . . pe . . . vatthuṃ . . . garuṃ katvā ganthasampayutto rāgo, diṭṭhi uppajjati.
     6. Ganthavippayutto . . . ganthasampayuttassa ca . . .
     Ārammaṇādhipati:-- cakkhuṃ . . . pe . . . garuṃ katvā diṭṭhigatavippayuttalobhasahagatā khandhā ca lobho ca uppajjanti.
     7. Ganthasampayutto ca ganthavippayutto ca . . .
     Ārammaṇādhipati:-- diṭṭhigatavippayuttalobhasahagate khandhe ca lobhañ ca garuṃ katvā ganthasampayuttā khandhā uppajjanti .

272                          Ganthasampayuttadukaṃ.
[... content straddling page break has been moved to the page above ...] . . (mūlaṃ pucchitabbaṃ). Diṭṭhigata. . . katvā diṭṭhigatavippayutto lobho uppajjati . . .
(mūlaṃ pucchitabbaṃ). Diṭṭhigata- . . . katvā diṭṭhigatavippayuttalobhasahagatā khandhā ca lobho ca uppajjanti.
     1. Ganthasampayutto dhammo ganthasampayuttassa dhammassa anantarapaccayena paccayo.
     (a) Purimā purimā ganthasampayuttā khandhā pacchimānaṃ pacchimānaṃ ganthasampayuttānaṃ khandhānaṃ anantarapaccayena paccayo . . . (mūlaṃ pucchitabbaṃ).
     (b) Purimā purimā diṭṭhigatavippayuttalobhasahagatā khandhā pacchimassa pacchimassa diṭṭhigatavippayuttassa lobhassa anantarapaccayena paccayo. (c) Purimā purimā domanassasahagatā khandhā pacchimassa pacchimassa paṭighassa, ganthasampayuttā khandhā vuṭṭhānassa anantarapaccayena paccayo . . . (mūlaṃ pucchitabbaṃ).
(d) Purimā purimā diṭṭhigatavippayuttalobhasahagatā khandhā pacchimānaṃ pacchimānaṃ diṭṭhigatavippayuttalobhasahagatānaṃ khandhānaṃ lobhassa ca anantarapaccayena paccayo. (e) Purimā purimā domanassasahagatā khandhā pacchimānaṃ pacchimānaṃ domanassasahagatānaṃ khandhānaṃ paṭighassa ca anantarapaccayena paccayo.
     4. Ganthavippayutto . . . ganthavippayuttassa . . .
     Purimo purimo diṭṭhigatavippayutto lobho pacchimassa pacchimassa diṭṭhigatavippayuttassa lobhassa anantarapaccayena paccayo. Purimaṃ purimaṃ domanassa sahagataṃ paṭighaṃ pacchimassa pacchimassa paṭighassa anantarapaccayena paccayo. Purimā purimā diṭṭhigatavippayuttā khandhā pacchimānaṃ pacchimānaṃ ganthavippayuttānaṃ khandhānaṃ anantarapaccayena paccayo. Anulomaṃ gotrabhussa phalasamāpattiyā anantarapaccayena paccayo.
     5. Ganthavippayutto . . . ganthasampayuttassa dhammassa . . .


[page 273]
                     Anantaravāro.                          273
     (a) Purimo . . . pacchimānaṃ pacchimānaṃ diṭṭhigatevippayuttānaṃ khandhānaṃ anantarapaccayena paccayo.
     (b) Purimaṃ purimaṃ paṭighaṃ pacchimānaṃ pacchimānaṃ domanassasahagatānaṃ khandhānaṃ . . . Āvajjanā ganthasampayuttānaṃ khandhānaṃ anantarapaccayena paccayo.
     6. Ganthavippayutto . . . ganthasampayuttassa ca . . .
     Purimo . . . khandhānaṃ lobhassa ca anantarapaccayena paccayo. Purimaṃ . . . khandhānaṃ paṭighassa ca anantarapaccayena paccayo. Āvajjanā diṭṭhigatavippayuttalobhasahagatānaṃ khandhānaṃ lobhassa ca domanassasahagatānaṃ khandhānaṃ paṭighassa ca anantarapaccayena paccayo.
     7. Ganthasampayutto ca ganthavippayutto ca . . .
     (a) Purimā . . . khandhā lobho ca pacchimānaṃ . . .
khandhānaṃ anantarapaccayena paccayo. (b) Purimā . . .
khandhā ca paṭighañ ca pacchimānaṃ . . . khandhānaṃ anantarapaccayena paccayo . . . (mūlaṃ pucchitabbaṃ).
(c) Purimā . . . khandhā ca lobho ca pacchimassa . . .
(d) Purimā . . . paṭighañ ca pacchimassa pacchimassa paṭighassa anantarapaccayena paccayo. (e) Diṭṭhigatavippayuttalobhasahagatā khandhā ca lobho ca domanassasahagatā khandhā ca paṭighañ ca vuṭṭhānassa anantarapaccayena paccayo . . . (mūlaṃ pucchitabbaṃ). (f) Purimā . . . lobho ca pacchimānaṃ . . . (g) Purimā . . .
khandhānaṃ paṭighassa ca anantarapaccayena paccayo.
     1. Ganthasampayutto dhammo ganthasampayuttassa dhammassa samanantara- . . . sahajāta- . . . aññamañña- . . . nissaya- . . . upanissayapaccayena paccayo.
     Ārammaṇūpanissayo, anantarūpanissayo, pakatūpanissayo . . . pe . . . Pakatūpanissayo:-- ganthasampayuttā khandhā ganthasampayuttānaṃ khandhānaṃ upanissayapaccayena paccayo .

274                          Ganthasampayuttadukaṃ.
[... content straddling page break has been moved to the page above ...] . . (mūlaṃ pucchitabbaṃ) Ganthasampayuttā khandhā ganthavippayuttānaṃ . . . (mūlaṃ pucchitabbaṃ). Ganthasampayuttā khandhā diṭṭhigatavippa yuttalobhasahagatānaṃ khandhānaṃ lobhassa ca upanissayapaccayena paccayo. Domanassasahagatānaṃ khandhā naṃ paṭighassa ca upanissayapaccayena paccayo.
     4. Ganthavippayutto . . . ganthavippayuttassa . . .
     Ārammaṇūpanissayo . . . pe . . . Pakatūpanissayo:-- saddhaṃ upanissāya dānaṃ deti . . . pe . . . samāpattiṃ uppādeti, mānaṃ jappeti . . . Sīlaṃ . . . pe . . . paññaṃ, rāgaṃ dosaṃ, mohaṃ, mānaṃ, patthanaṃ, kāyikaṃ sukhaṃ kāyikaṃ dukkhaṃ . . . utuṃ bhojanaṃ senāsanaṃ upanissāya dānaṃ deti,
. . . pe . . . samāpattiṃ uppādeti . . . pāṇaṃ hanati . . . pe . . .
saṃghaṃ bhindati, saddhā . . . pe . . . paññā rāgo . . .
pe . . . patthanā senāsanaṃ . . . saddhāya . . . paññāya rāgassa dosassa mohassa mānassa patthanāya upanissayapaccayena paccayo.

Sīlaṃ . . . pe . . . pāññaṃ rāgaṃ . . . pe . . . mānaṃ patthanaṃ senāsanaṃ upanissāya pāṇaṃ hanati . . . pe . . . saṃghaṃ bhindati. Saddhā . . . pe . . . senāsanaṃ rāgassa dosassa mohassa mānassa diṭṭhiyā patthanāya upanissayapaccayena paccayo.
     6. Ganthavippayutto dhammo ganthasampayuttassa ca . . . (tīṇi).
     Saddhaṃ upanissāya mānaṃ jappeti, diṭṭhiṃ gaṇhāti,
sīlaṃ . . . pe . . . paññaṃ rāgaṃ dosaṃ mohaṃ mānaṃ patthanaṃ kāyikaṃ sukhaṃ, senāsanaṃ upanissāya pāṇaṃ hanati .
