                          Purejātavāro.                     275
[... content straddling page break has been moved to the page above ...] . . pe . . . saṃghaṃ bhindati, saddhā . . . pe . . . paññā rāgo doso moho māno patthanā senāsanaṃ diṭṭhigatavippayuttalobhasahagatānaṃ khandhānaṃ lobhassa ca domanassasahagatānaṃ khandhānaṃ paṭighassa ca upanissayapaccayena paccayo.
     7. Ganthasampayutto ca ganthavippayutto ca . . .
     Ārammaṇūpanissayo . . . pe . . . Pakatūpanissayo:-- diṭṭhigatavippayuttalobhasahagatā khandhā ca lobho ca domanassasahagatā lobhañ ca khandhā ca paṭighañ ca ganthasampayuttānaṃ khandhānaṃ upanissayapaccayena paccayo . . . (mūlaṃ pucchitabbaṃ). Diṭṭhigatavippayuttalobhasahagatā khandhā ca lobho ca domanassasahagatā khandhā ca paṭighañ ca ganthavippayuttānaṃ khandhānaṃ diṭṭhigatavippayuttassa lobhassa ca paṭighassa ca upanissayapaccayena paccayo . . . (mūlaṃ pucchitabbaṃ). Diṭṭhigatavippayuttalobhasahagatā khandhā ca lobho ca domanassasahagatā khandhā ca paṭighañ ca diṭṭhigatavippayuttalobhasahagatānaṃ khandhānaṃ lobhassa ca domanassasahagatānaṃ khandhānaṃ paṭighassa ca upanissayapaccayena paccayo.
     4. Ganthavippayutto dhammo ganthavippayuttassa dhammassa purejātapaccayena paccayo.
     Ārammaṇapurejātaṃ, vatthupurejātaṃ. Ārammaṇapurejātaṃ:-- cakkhuṃ . . . pe . . . vatthuṃ aniccato vipassati,
assādeti abhinandati, taṃ ārabbha ganthavippayutto rāgo uppajjati diṭṭhi vicikicchā uddhaccaṃ domanassaṃ uppajjati:
dibbena cakkhunā rūpaṃ passati, dibbāya sotadhātuyā saddaṃ suṇāti. Rūpāyatanaṃ cakkhuviññāṇassa . . . phoṭṭhabbāyatanaṃ kāyaviññāṇassa . . . Vatthupurejātaṃ:-- cakkhāyatanaṃ cakkhuviññāṇassa . . . kāyāyatanaṃ kāyaviññāṇassa,
vatthu ganthavippayuttānaṃ khandhānaṃ diṭṭhigatavippayuttassa lobhassa ca paṭighassa ca purejātapaccayena paccayo.
     5. Ganthavippayutto . . . ganthasampayuttassa . . .

276                     Ganthasampayuttadukaṃ.
     Ārammaṇapurejātaṃ . . . pe . . . vatthuṃ assādeti abhinandati, taṃ ārabbha ganthasampayutto rāgo uppajjati diṭṭhi domanassaṃ uppajjati. Vatthupurejātaṃ:-- vatthu ganthasampayuttānaṃ khandhānaṃ purejātapaccayena paccayo.
     6. Ganthavippayutto . . . ganthasampayuttassa ca . . .
     Ārammaṇapurejātaṃ . . . pe . . . vatthuṃ ārabbha diṭṭhigatavippayuttalobhasahagatā khandhā ca lobho ca domanassasahagatā khandhā ca paṭighañ ca uppajjanti.
Vatthupurejātaṃ:-- vatthu diṭṭhigatavippayuttalobhasahagatānaṃ khandhānaṃ lobhassa ca domanassasahagatānaṃ khandhānaṃ paṭighassa ca purejātapaccayena paccayo.
     2. Ganthasampayutto dhammo ganthavippayuttassa dhammassa pacchājātapaccayena paccayo . . . (ekaṃ).
     4. Ganthavippayutto dhammo ganthavippayuttassa . . .
(ekaṃ).
     8. Ganthasampayutto ca . . . ganthavippayuttassa dhammassa . . .
     Pacchājātā diṭṭhigatavippayuttalobhasahagatā khandhā ca lobho ca domanassasahagatā khandhā ca paṭighañ ca purejātassa imassa kāyassa pacchājātapaccayena paccayo.
     1. Ganthasampayutto dhammo . . . āsevanapaccayena paccayo . . . (anantarasadisaṃ. Āvajjanā pi vuṭṭhānam pi natthi) . . . kammapaccayena paccayo.
     Ganthasampayuttā cetanā sampayuttakānaṃ khandhānaṃ kammapaccayena paccayo.
     2. Ganthasampayutto . . . ganthavippayuttassa . . .
     Sahajātā, nānākhaṇikā. Sahajātā ganthasampayuttā cetanā cittasamuṭṭhānānaṃ rūpānaṃ kammapaccayena paccayo. Diṭṭhigatavippayuttalobhasahagatā cetanā lobhassa cittasamuṭṭhānānañ ca . . . Domanassasahagatā cetanā paṭighassa cittasamuṭṭhānānañ ca . . . Nānākhaṇikā ganthasampayuttā cetanā vipākānaṃ khandhānaṃ kaṭattā ca rūpānaṃ kammapaccayena paccayo.


[page 277]
                          Vippayuttavāro.                    277
[... content straddling page break has been moved to the page above ...]
     3. Ganthasampayutto . . . ganthasampayuttassa ca . . .

kammapaccayena paccayo.
     4. Ganthavippayutto dhammo . . . vipākapaccayena paccayo . . . (ekaṃ).
     1. Ganthasampayutto dhammo ganthasampayuttassa dhammassa āhārapaccayena paccayo . . . (cattāri) . . .
indriya- . . . (cattāri) . . . jhāna- . . . (cattāri) . . .
magga- . . . (cattāri) . . . sampayuttapaccayena paccayo . . . (cha).
     2. Ganthasampayutto dhammo ganthavippayuttassa dhammassa vippayuttapaccayena paccayo.
     Sahajātaṃ, pacchājātaṃ . . . (saṃkhittaṃ,vibhajitabbaṃ).
     4. Ganthavippayutto . . . ganthavippayuttassa . . .
     Sahajātaṃ, purejātaṃ, pacchājātaṃ . . . (saṃkhittaṃ).
     5. Ganthavippayutto . . . ganthasampayuttassa . . .
     Purejātaṃ vatthu ganthasampayuttaṃ khandhānaṃ vippayuttapaccayena paccayo.
     6. Ganthavippayutto dhammo ganthasampayuttassa ca . . .
     Purejātaṃ vatthu diṭṭhigatavippayuttalobhasahagatānaṃ khandhānaṃ lobhassa ca domanassasahagatānaṃ khandhānaṃ paṭighassa ca vippayuttapaccayena paccayo.


[page 278]
278                          Ganthasampayuttadukaṃ.
     8. Ganthasampayutto ca . . . ganthavippayuttassa dhammassa . . .
     Sahajātaṃ, pacchājātaṃ. Sahajātā diṭṭhigatavippayuttalobhasahagatā khandhā ca lobho ca cittasamuṭṭhānānaṃ rūpānaṃ vippayuttapaccayena paccayo. Domanassasahagatā khandhā ca paṭighañ ca citta- . . . Pacchājātā diṭṭhigatavippayuttalobhasahagatā khandhā ca lobho ca domanassasahagatā khandhā ca paṭighañ ca purejātassa imassa kāyassa vippayuttapaccayena paccayo.
     1. Ganthasampayutto dhammo . . . atthipaccayena paccayo . . . (ekaṃ, paṭiccasadisaṃ).
     2. Ganthasampayutto . . . ganthavippayuttassa . . .
     Sahajātaṃ, pacchājātaṃ . . . (saṃkhittaṃ, vibhajitabbaṃ).
     3. Ganthasampayutto . . . ganthasampayuttassa ca . . .
(ekaṃ, paṭiccasadisaṃ).
     4. Ganthavippayutto . . . ganthavippayuttassa . . .
     Sahajātaṃ, purejātan, pacchājātaṃ āhāraṃ indriyaṃ . . .
(saṃkhittaṃ, vibhajitabbaṃ).
     5. Ganthavippayutto . . . ganthasampayuttassa . . .
     Sahajātaṃ, purejātaṃ. Sahajāto diṭṭhigatavippayutto lobho sampayuttakānaṃ khandhānaṃ atthipaccayena paccayo. Domanassasahagataṃ paṭighaṃ sampayuttakānaṃ khandhānaṃ atthipaccayena paccayo. Purejātaṃ:-- cakkhuṃ . . . pe . . . vatthuṃ assādeti abhinandati, taṃ ārabbha ganthasampayutto rāgo . . . pe . . . diṭṭhi domanassaṃ uppajjati; vatthu ganthasampayuttakānaṃ khandhānaṃ atthipaccayena paccayo.
     6. Ganthavippayutto . . . ganthasampayuttassa ca . . .
     Sahajātaṃ, purejātaṃ. Sahajāto diṭṭhigatavippayutto lobho sampayuttakānaṃ khandhānaṃ cittasamuṭṭhānānañ ca rūpānaṃ atthipaccayena paccayo. Paṭighaṃ sampayuttakānaṃ . . . Purejātaṃ:-- cakkhuṃ . . . pe . . . vatthuṃ ārabbha diṭṭhigatavippayuttalobhasahagatā khandhā ca lobho ca domanassasahagatā khandhā ca paṭighañ ca uppajjanti;


[page 279]
                          Atthivāro.                         279
[... content straddling page break has been moved to the page above ...] vatthu diṭṭhigatavippayuttalobhasahagatānaṃ khandhānaṃ lobhassa ca domanassasahagatānaṃ khandhānaṃ paṭighassa ca atthipaccayena paccayo.
     7. Ganthasampayutto ca . . . dhammā ganthasampayuttassa . . .
     Sahajātaṃ, purejātaṃ. Sahajāto ganthasampayutto eko khandho ca vatthu ca tiṇṇannaṃ khandhānaṃ atthipaccayena paccayo; dve . . . Sahajāto diṭṭhigatavippayuttalobhasahagato eko khandho ca lobho ca tiṇṇannaṃ . . .
paccayo; dve . . . Domanassasahagato eko khandho ca paṭighañ ca tiṇṇannaṃ . . . dve . . .
     8. Ganthasampayutto ca . . . dhammā ganthavippayuttassa . . .
     Sahajātaṃ, purejātaṃ, paccahājātaṃ āhāraṃ indriyaṃ.
Sahajātā ganthasampayuttā khandhā ca mahābhūtā ca cittasamuṭṭhānānaṃ rūpānaṃ atthipaccayena paccayo.
Sahajātā diṭṭhigatavippayuttalobhasahagatā khandhā ca lobho ca citta- . . . Sahajātā domanassasahagatā khandhā ca paṭighañ ca citta- . . . Diṭṭhigatavippayuttalobhasahagatā khandhā ca vatthu ca lobhassa atthipaccayena paccayo. Domanassasahagatā khandhā ca vatthu ca paṭighassa atthipaccayena paccayo. Pacchājātā diṭṭhigatavippayuttalobhasahagatā khandhā ca lobho ca domanassasahagatā khandhā ca paṭighañ ca purejātassa imassa kāyassa atthipaccayena paccayo. Pacchājātā ganthasampayuttā khandhā ca kabaḷiṃkāro āhāro ca imassa . . .
Pacchājātā ganthasampayuttā khandhā ca rūpajīvitindriyañ ca kaṭattā rūpānaṃ atthipaccayena paccayo.
     9. Ganthasampayutto ca ganthavippayutto ca . . .
     Sahajātaṃ, purejātaṃ. Sahajāto diṭṭhigatavippayuttalobhasahagato eko khandho ca lobho ca tiṇṇannaṃ khandhānaṃ cittasamuṭṭhānānañ ca rūpānaṃ atthipaccayena paccayo;


[page 280]
280                     Ganthasampayuttadukaṃ.
[... content straddling page break has been moved to the page above ...] dve . . . Sahajāto domanassasahagato eko khandho ca paṭighañ ca tiṇṇannaṃ khandhānaṃ cittasamuṭṭhānānañ ca rūpānaṃ atthipaccayena paccayo; dve . . . Sahajāto diṭṭhigatavippayuttalobhasahagato eko khandho ca vatthu ca tiṇṇannaṃ khandhānaṃ lobhassa ca atthipaccayena paccayo; dve . . . Sahajāto domanassasahagato eko khandho ca vatthu ca tiṇṇannaṃ khandhānaṃ paṭighassa ca atthipaccayena paccayo; dve . . .
          Hetuyā nava,                     purejāte tīṇi,
          ārammaṇe nava,                    pacchājāte tīṇi,
          adhipatiyā nava,                āsevane nava,
          anantare nava,                    kamme cattāri,
          samanantare nava,                vipāke ekaṃ,
          sahajāte nava,                āhāre cattāri,
          aññamaññe cha,                    indriye cattāri,
          nissaye nava,                     jhāne cattāri,
          upanissaye nava,                magge cattāri,
          sampayutte cha,                natthiyā nava,
          vippayutte pañca,                vigate nava,
          atthiyā nava,                     avigate nava.
     1. Ganthasampayutto . . . ganthasampayuttassa . . .

     4. Ganthavippayutto . . . ganthavippayuttassa . . .
purejāta-, pacchājāta-, kamma-,āhāra-, indriyapaccayena paccayo.
     5. Ganthavippayutto dhammo ganthasampayuttassa . . .
purejātapaccayena paccayo.

     7. Ganthasampayutto ca . . . dhammā ganthasampayuttassa . . .
     8. Ganthasampayutto ca . . . dhammā ganthavippayuttassa . . . pacchājāta paccayena paccayo.
     9. Ganthasampayutto ca . . . dhammā ganthasampayuttassa ca ganthavippayuttassa ca dhammassa . . .
          Nahetuyā nava,                    sabbattha nava;
          nārammaṇe nava,                no-avigate nava.
          Hetupaccayā, nārammaṇe nava,      (saṅkhittaṃ) . . .,
          nādhipatiyā nava . . .           namagge nava,

[page 282]
                               282
                          [XXIX.
                GANTHO-CEVA-GANTHANIYA-DUKAṂ.]
     1. Ganthañ ceva ganthaniyañ ca dhammaṃ paṭicca gantho ceva ganthaniyo ca dhammo uppajjati hetupaccayā.
     Sīlabbataparāmāsakāyaganthaṃ paṭicca abhijjhākāyagantho; abhijjhākāyaganthaṃ paṭicca sīlabbataparāmāsakāyagantho; idaṃsaccābhinivesakāyaganthaṃ paṭicca abhijjhākāyagantho; abhijjhākāyaganthaṃ paṭicca idaṃsaccābhinivesakāyagantho.
     2. Ganthañ ceva ganthaniyañ ca dhammaṃ paṭicca ganthaniyo ceva no ca gantho dhammo uppajjati hetupaccayā.
     Ganthe paṭicca sampayuttakā khandhā cittasamuṭṭhānañ ca rūpaṃ.
     3. Ganthañ ceva ganthaniyañ ca dhammaṃ paṭicca gantho ceva ganthaniyo ca ganthaniyo ceva no ca gantho ca dhammā uppajjanti hetupaccayā . . . (paṭiccavāro pi sahajātavāro pi paccayavāro pi nissayavāro pi saṃsaṭṭhavāro pi sampayuttavāro pi ganthadukasadisā. Ninnānākaraṇā).
     1. Gantho ceva ganthaniyo dhammo ganthassa ceva ganthaniyassa ca dhammassa hetupaccayena paccayo.
     Ganthā hetū sampayuttakānaṃ ganthānaṃ hetupaccayena paccayo . . . (evaṃ nava pañhā vitthāretabbā).
     1. Gantho ceva ganthaniyo ca dhammo ganthassa ceva ganthaniyassa dhammassa ārammaṇapaccayena paccayo.
     Ganthe ārabbha ganthā uppajjanti . . . (mūlaṃ pucchitabbaṃ).


[page 283]
                          Ārammaṇavāro.                     283
[... content straddling page break has been moved to the page above ...] Ganthe ārabbha ganthaniyā ceva no ca ganthā khandhā uppajjanti (mūlaṃ pucchitabbaṃ). Ganthe ārabbha ganthā ca sampayuttakā ca khandhā uppajjanti.
     4. Ganthaniyo ceva no ca gantho dhammo ganthaniyassa ceva no ca ganthassa ca dhammassa ārammaṇapaccayena paccayo.
     Dānaṃ sīlaṃ uposathakammaṃ taṃ paccavekkhati, pubbe suciṇṇāni, jhānaṃ paccavekkhati. Ariyā gotrabhuṃ paccavekkhanti, vodānaṃ paccavekkhanti, pahīnakilese vikkhambhitakilese paccavekkhanti, pubbe samudāciṇṇe kilese jānanti. Cakkhuṃ . . . pe . . . vatthuṃ ganthaniye ceva no ca ganthe khandhe aniccato . . . pe . . . domanassaṃ uppajjati, dibbena cakkhunā rūpaṃ passati, dibbāya sotadhātuyā saddaṃ suṇāti . . . (sabbaṃ vitthāretabbaṃ) . . . āvajjanāya ārammaṇapaccayena paccayo.
     5. Ganthaniyo ceva no ca gantho dhammo ganthassa ceva ganthaniyassa dhammassa ārammaṇapaccayena paccayo.
     Dānaṃ sīlaṃ uposathakammaṃ katvā taṃ assādeti abhinandati, taṃ ārabbha rāgo uppajjati, diṭṭhi, vicikicchā,
uddhaccaṃ, domanassaṃ uppajjati; pubbe suciṇṇāni . . . jhānā vuṭṭhahitvā jhānaṃ . . . Cakkhuṃ . . . pe . . . vatthuṃ ganthaniye ceva no ca ganthe khandhe assādeti abhinandati,
taṃ ārabbha rāgo uppajjati, diṭṭhi . . . pe . . . domanassaṃ uppajjati.
     6. Ganthaniyo ceva no ca . . . ganthassa ceva ganthaniyessa ca ganthaniyassa ceva no ca . . .
     Dānaṃ sīlaṃ . . . jhānaṃ . . . Cakkhuṃ . . . vatthuṃ . . . khandhe assādeti abhinandati, taṃ ārabbha ganthā ca sampayuttakā ca khandhā uppajjanti . . . (evaṃ itare pi tīṇi vitthāretabbā. Ārabbha kātabbā. Imamhi duke lokuttaraṃ natthi, ganthadukasadisaṃ. Ninnānākaraṇaṃ. Ganthaniyaṃ ti niyāmetabbaṃ. Magge nava pañhā kātabbā).
           GANTHO-CEVA-GANTHANIYA-DUKAṂ niṭṭhitaṃ.

                          [XXX.
                GANTHO-CEVA-GANTHASAMPAYUTTA-DUKAṂ.]
     1. Ganthañ ceva ganthasampayuttaṃ dhammaṃ paṭicca gantho ceva ganthasampayutto ca dhammo uppajjati hetupaccayā.
     Sīlabbataparāmāsakāyaganthaṃ paṭicca abhijjhākāyagantho; abhijjhākāyaganthaṃ paṭicca sīlabbataparāmāsakāyagantho; idaṃsaccābhinivesakāyaganthaṃ paṭicca abhijjhākāyagantho; abhijjhākāyaganthaṃ paṭicca idaṃsaccābhinivesakāyagantho.
     2. Ganthañ ceva ganthasampayuttaṃ dhammaṃ paṭicca ganthasampayutto ceva no ca gantho dhammo . . .
     Ganthe paṭicca sampayuttakā khandhā.
     3. Ganthañ ceva . . . paṭicca gantho ceva . . . ganthasampayutto ceva no ca gantho ca dhammā . . .
     Sīlabbataparāmāsakāyaganthaṃ paṭicca abhijjhākāyagantho sampayuttakā ca khandhā . . . (cakkaṃ).
     4. Ganthasampayuttañ ceva no ca ganthaṃ dhammaṃ . . . ganthasampayutte ceva no ca . . .
     Ganthasampayuttañ ceva no ca ganthaṃ ekaṃ khandhaṃ paṭicca tayo khandhā; dve . . .
     5. Ganthasampayuttañ ceva no ca ganthaṃ dhammaṃ . . . gantho ceva . . .
     Ganthasampayutte ceva no ca ganthe khandhe paṭicca ganthā.
     6. Ganthasampayuttañ ceva no ca ganthaṃ . . . gantho ceva . . . no ca gantho ca dhammā . . . (cakkaṃ).


[page 285]
                          Hetuvāro.                          285
     7. Ganthañ ceva ganthasampayuttañ ca . . . ganthasampayutto dhammo uppajjati hetupaccayā . . . pe . . .
     8. Ganthañ ceva . . . no ca gantho . . .
     Ganthasampayuttañ ceva no ca ganthaṃ ekaṃ khandhañ ca ganthe ca paṭicca tayo khandhā; dve . . .
     9. Ganthañ ceva . . . no ca gantho ca dhammā uppajjanti hetupaccayā.
     Ganthasampayuttañ ceva no ca ganthaṃ ekaṃ khandhañ ca sīlabbataparāmāsakāyaganthañ ca paṭicca tayo khandha abhijjhākāyagantho ca; dve . . . (cakkaṃ bandhitabbaṃ saṃkhittaṃ).
          Hetuyā nava,                     kamme nava,
          ārammaṇe nava,                    āhāre nava,
          sabbattha nava;                avigate nava,
     1. Ganthañ ceva ganthasampayuttaṃ dhammaṃ paṭicca gantho ceva ganthasampayutto dhammo uppajjati nādhipatipaccayā . . . (saṃkhittaṃ. Idha nahetupaccayo natthi).
          Nādhipatiyā nava,                nakamme tīṇi,
          napurejāte nava,                navipāke nava,
          napacchājāte nava,                navippayutte nava.
          nāsevane nava,
     (Itare pi dve gaṇanā pi sahajātavāro pi paccayavāro pi nissayavāro pi saṃsaṭṭhavāro pi sampayuttavāro pi paṭiccavārasadisā3.)
     1. Gantho ceva ganthasampayutto dhammo ganthassa ceva ganthasampayuttassa ca dhammassa hetupaccayena paccayo.
     Gantho ceva ganthasampayuttā ca hetū sampayuttakānaṃ khandhānaṃ hetupaccayena paccayo.
     2. Gantho ceva . . . no ca ganthassa dhammassa . . .
     Ganthā ceva . . .


[page 286]
286                Gantho-ceva-ganthasampayuttadukaṃ.
     3. Gantho ceva . . . no ca ganthassa . . .
     Ganthā ceva ganthasampayuttā ca hetū ganthānaṃ sampayuttakānañ ca . . .
     4. Ganthasampayutto ceva no ca gantho . . .
     Ganthasampayuttā ceva no ca ganthā hetū . . .
     5. Ganthasampayutto ceva no ca gantho . . .
     Ganthasampayuttā . . .
     6. Ganthasampayutto ceva no ca gantho . . .
     Ganthasampayuttā ceva no ca ganthā hetū ganthanaṃ sampayuttakānañ ca khandhānaṃ hetupaccayena paccayo.
     7. Gantho ceva ganthasampayutto ca . . .
     Ganthā ceva ganthasampayuttā ca ganthasampayuttā ceva no ca ganthā ca hetū ganthānaṃ sampayuttakānañ ca khandhānaṃ hetupaccayena paccayo.
     1. Gantho ceva ganthasampayutto dhammo ganthassa ceva ganthasampayuttassa dhammassa ārammaṇapaccayena paccayo.
     Ganthe ārabbha ganthā uppajjanti . . . (mūlaṃ kātabbaṃ).
Ganthe ārabbha ganthasampayuttā ceva no ca ganthā khandhā uppajjanti . . .; (mūlaṃ kātabbaṃ). Ganthe ārabbha ganthā ca ganthasampayuttā ca khandhā uppajjanti.
     4. Ganthasampayutto ceva no ca gantho dhammo . . .
     Ganthasampayutte ceva no ca ganthe khandhe ārabbha ganthasampayuttā ceva no ca ganthā khandhā uppajjanti . . . (mūlaṃ kātabbaṃ). Ganthasampayutte . . . ārabbha ganthā uppajjanti (mūlaṃ kātabbaṃ). Ganthasampayutte . . . ganthā ca ganthasampayuttakā ca khandhā uppajjanti. (Evaṃ itare pi tīṇi pañhā kātabbā, ārammaṇasadisā yeva, adhipatiyā pi anantare pi upanissaye pi vibhaṃgo natthi.)


[page 287]
                               Mātikā.                          287
          Hetuyā nava,                     kamme tīṇi,
          ārammaṇe nava,                    āhāre tīṇi,
          adhipatiyā nava,                indriye tīṇi,
          anantare nava,                    jhāne tīṇi,
          samanantare nava,                magge nava,
          sahajāte nava,                    sampayutte nava,
          aññamaññe nava,                atthiyā nava,
          nissaye nava,                     natthiyā nava,
          upanissaye nava,                vigate nava,
          āsevane nava,                    avigate nava.
     Arūpā yeva paccayā ekekassa tīṇi tīṇi kātabbā. Ārammaṇañ ca sahajātañ ca upanissayañ ca navasu pi parivattetabbaṃ. Evaṃ pañhāvāre pi sabbaṃ kātabbaṃ.
           GANTHO-CEVA-GANTHASAMPAYUTTA-DUKAṂ niṭṭhitaṃ.

                          288
                          [XXXI.
                GANTHAVIPPAYUTTA-GANTHANIYA-DUKAṂ.]
     1. Ganthavippayuttaganthaniyaṃ dhammaṃ paṭicca ganthavippayuttaganthaniyo dhammo uppajjati hetupaccayā.
     Ganthavippayuttaganthaniyaṃ ekaṃ khandhaṃ paṭicca tayo khandhā cittasamuṭṭhānañ ca rūpaṃ; dve . . . Paṭisandhikkhaṇe ekaṃ mahabhūtaṃ . . . pe . . . (yathā cūḷantaraduke lokiyadukaṃ, evaṃ viṭṭhāretabbaṃ. Ninnānākarāṇaṃ).
           GANTHAVIPPAYUTTA-GANTHANIYA-DUKAṂ niṭṭhitaṃ.
                          [XXXII.
                          OGHA-DUKAṂ.]
     Oghaṃ dhammaṃ paṭicca ogho dhammo uppajjati hetupaccayā . . . (dve pi gocchakā āsavagocchakasadisā. Ninnānākaraṇā).


[page 289]
                               289
                               XXXIII.
                          NĪVARAṆA-DUKAṂ.]
     1. Nīvaraṇaṃ dhammaṃ paṭicca nīvaraṇo dhammo uppajjati hetupaccayā.
     Kāmacchandanīvaraṇaṃ paṭicca thīnamiddhanīvaraṇaṃ avijjānīvaraṇaṃ; kāmacchandanīvaraṇaṃ paṭicca uddhaccanīvaraṇaṃ avijjānīvaraṇaṃ; kāmacchandanīvaraṇaṃ paṭicca avijjānīvaraṇaṃ. Ariyā nonīvaraṇe pahīnakilese vikkhambhitakilese pubbe samudāciṇṇe . . . Cakkhuṃ, vatthuṃ, nonīvaraṇe khandhe aniccato . . . pe . . . domanassaṃ uppajjati;

ākiñcaññāyatanaṃ nevasaññānāsaññāyatanassa, rūpāyatanaṃ cakkhuviññāṇassa . . . phoṭṭhabbāyatanaṃ kāyaviññāṇassa, nonīvaraṇā khandhā iddhividhañaṇassa cetopariyañāṇassa pubbenivāsānussatiñāṇassa yathākammūpagañāṇassa anāgataṃsañāṇassa āvajjanāya ārammaṇapaccayena paccayo.

Cakkhuṃ, vatthuṃ, nonīvaraṇe khandhe garuṃ katvā assādeti abhinandati, taṃ garuṃ katvā rāgo, diṭṭhi uppajjati . . . pe . . . Sahajātādhipati:-- nonīvaraṇādhipati sampayuttakānaṃ khandhānaṃ cittasamuṭṭhānānañ ca rūpānaṃ adhipatipaccayena paccayo.

cakkhuṃ, vatthuṃ . . . uppajjati; . . . pe . . . Sahajātādhipati:-- nonīvaraṇādhipati sampayuttakānaṃ nīvaraṇānaṃ adhipatipaccayena paccayo.
     6. Nonīvaraṇo dhammo nīvaraṇassa ca . . .
     Ārammaṇādhipati . . . katvā assādeti abhinandati, taṃ garuṃ katvā nīvaraṇā ca sampayuttakā ca khandhā uppajjanti. Sahajātādhipati:-- . . . khandhānaṃ nīvaraṇānañ ca cittasamuṭṭhānānañ ca rūpānaṃ adhipatipaccayena paccayo.
     7. Nīvaraṇo ca nonīvaraṇo ca dhammā nīvaraṇassa dhammassa adhipatipaccayena paccayo.
     Ārammaṇādhipati . . . (tīṇi, ārammaṇādhipati yeva).
     1. Nīvaraṇo dhammo nīvaraṇassa dhammassa anantarapaccayena paccayo.
     (a) Purimā purimā nīvaraṇā pacchimānaṃ pacchimānaṃ nīvaraṇānaṃ anantarapaccayena paccayo . . . (mūlaṃ pucchitabbaṃ). (b) Purimā . . . pacchimānaṃ nonīvaraṇānaṃ khandhānaṃ . . . Nīvaraṇā vuṭṭhānassa anantarapaccayena paccayo . . . (mūlaṃ pucchitabbaṃ). (c) Purimā . . .
nīvaraṇānaṃ sampayuttakānañ ca khandhānaṃ anantarapaccayena paccayo.
     4. Nonīvaraṇo dhammo nonīvaraṇassa dhammassa . . .
     Purimā purimā nonīvaraṇā khandhā pacchimāṇaṃ . . .
Nirodhā vuṭṭhahantassa navasaññānāsaññāyatanaṃ phalasamāpattiyā anantarapaccayena paccayo .

Āvajjanā nīvaraṇānaṃ sampayuttakānañ ca khandhānaṃ anantarapaccayena paccayo.
     7. Nīvaraṇo ca nonīvaraṇo ca . . . nīvaraṇassa . . .
     Purimā purimā nīvaraṇā ca sampayuttakā ca khandhā pacchimānaṃ pacchimānaṃ nīvaraṇānaṃ anantarapaccayena paccayo . . . (mūlāni pucchitabbāni). Purimā . . . nonīvaraṇānaṃ khandhānaṃ . . . Nīvaraṇā ca sampayuttakā ca khandhā vuṭṭhānassa anantarapaccayena paccayo.
Purimā purimā nīvaraṇā ca sampayuttakā ca khandhā pacchimānaṃ pacchimānaṃ nīvaraṇānañ ca sampayuttakānañ ca khandhānaṃ anantarapaccayena paccayo.
     1. Nīvaraṇo dhammo nīvaraṇassa dhammassa samanantara . . . sahajāta- . . . aññamañña- . . . nissaya- . . .
upanissayapaccayena paccayo.
     Ārammaṇūpanissayo, anantarūpanissayo, pakatūpanissayo; . . . pe . . . (nīvaraṇāni tīṇi).
     4. Nonīvaraṇo dhammo nonīvaraṇassa dhammassa . . .
     Ārammaṇūpanissayo . . . pe . . . Pakatūpanissayo:-- saddhaṃ upanissāya dānaṃ deti, sīlaṃ uposathakammaṃ jhānaṃ uppādeti, vipassanaṃ maggaṃ abhiññaṃ samāpattiṃ uppādeti, mānaṃ jappeti gaṇhāti, sīlaṃ . . . pe . . .
paññaṃ rāgaṃ dosaṃ mohaṃ mānaṃ diṭṭhiṃ patthanaṃ,
kāyikaṃ sukhaṃ kāyikaṃ dukkhaṃ. Senāsanaṃ upanissāya dānaṃ deti . . . pe . . . saṃghaṃ bhindati, saddhā . . . pe . . .
senāsanaṃ saddhāya . . . pe . . . paññāya rāgassa . . . pe . . .
patthanāya kāyikassa sukhassa kāyikassa dukkhassa maggassa phalassa samāpattiyā upanissayapaccayena paccayo.

     Sahajātaṃ, purejātaṃ, pacchājātaṃ āhāraṃ indriyaṃ.
Sahajāto nonīvaraṇo eko khandho ca nīvaraṇā ca tiṇṇannaṃ khandhānaṃ cittasamuṭṭhānānañ ca rūpānaṃ atthipaccayena paccayo; dve . . . khāndhā kabaḷiṃkāro āhāro ca imassa . . . Pacchājātā . . . khandhā rūpajīvitindriyañ ca kaṭattā rūpānaṃ atthipaccayena paccayo.

avijjānīvaraṇassa sampayuttakānañ ca khandhānaṃ atthipaccayena paccayo . . . (cakkaṃ).

     (a) Nīvaraṇasampayuttā hetū sampayuttakānaṃ khandhānaṃ hetupaccayena paccayo . . . (mūlāni pucchitabbāni).

     (c) Nīvaraṇasampayuttā . . . khandhānaṃ cittasamuṭṭhānānañ ca . . .
     4. Nīvaraṇavippayutto . . . nīvaraṇavippayuttassa . . .
     Nīvaraṇavippayuttā hetū . . . (paṭisandhi).
     1. Nīvaraṇasampayutto . . . ārammaṇapaccayena paccayo.
     Rāgaṃ assādeti abhinandati, taṃ ārabbha rāgo diṭṭhi vicikicchā uddhaccaṃ domanassaṃ uppajjati. Diṭṭhiṃ assādeti abhinandati, taṃ ārabbha rāgo diṭṭhi . . . uppajjati.
Vicikicchaṃ ārabbha vicikicchā diṭṭhi uddhaccaṃ domanassaṃ . . . Uddhaccaṃ ārabbha uddhaccaṃ uppajjati,
diṭṭhi, vicikicchā . . . Domanassaṃ ārabbha domanassaṃ uppajjati, diṭṭhi vicikicchā uddhaccaṃ uppajjati.
     2. Nīvaraṇasampayutto . . . nīvaraṇavippayuttassa . . .
     Ariyā nīvaraṇasampayutte pahīnakilese paccavekkhanti,
vikkhambhitakilese paccavekkhanti, pubbe samudāciṇṇe kilese jānanti. Nīvaraṇasampayutte khandhe aniccato dukkhato anattato vipassati, cetopariyañāṇena nīvaraṇasampayuttacittasamaṃgissa cittaṃ jānāti. Nīvaraṇasampayuttā khandhā iddhividhiñāṇassa cetopariyañāṇassa pubbenivāsānussatiñāṇassa yathākammūpagañāṇassa anāgataṃsañāṇassa āvajjanāya ārammaṇapaccayena paccayo.
     4. Nīvaraṇavippayutto dhammo . . .
     Dānaṃ sīlaṃ uposathakammaṃ taṃ paccavekkhati, pubbe suciṇṇāni . . . jhānā vuṭṭhahitvā jhānaṃ . . . Ariyā maggā vuṭṭhahitvā maggaṃ . . . phalaṃ nibbānaṃ paccavekkhanti.
Nibbānaṃ gotrabhussa vodānassa maggassa phalassa āvajjanāya ārammaṇapaccayena paccayo. Cakkhuṃ . . . vatthuṃ


[page 310]
310                     Nīvaraṇasampayuttadukaṃ.
. . . nīvaraṇavippayutte khandhe aniccato dukkhato anattato vipassati, dibbena cakkhunā rūpaṃ passati . . .
(yāva āvajjanāya).
     5. Nīvaraṇavippayutto . . . nīvaraṇasampayuttassa . . .
     Dānaṃ sīlaṃ uposathakammaṃ . . . pubbe . . . jhānā . . . cakkhuṃ . . . vatthuṃ . . . nīvaraṇavippayutte khandhe assādeti abhinandati, taṃ ārabbha rāgo diṭṭhi vicikicchā uddhaccaṃ domanassaṃ uppajjati.
     1. Nīvaraṇasampayutto . . . adhipatipaccayena paccayo.
     Ārammaṇādhipati, sahajātādhipati. Ārammaṇādhipati:
-- rāgaṃ garuṃ katvā assādeti abhinandati, taṃ garuṃ katvā rāgo uppajjati diṭṭhi uppajjati. Sahajātādhipati:-- nīvaraṇasampayuttādhipati sampayuttakānaṃ khandhānaṃ adhipatipaccayena paccayo.
     2. Nīvaraṇasampayutto dhammo . . .
     Sahajātādhipati:-- (a) nīvaraṇasampayuttādhipati cittasamuṭṭhānānaṃ rūpānaṃ adhipatipaccayena paccayo . . .
(mūlaṃ pucchitabbaṃ). (b) Nīvaraṇasampayuttādhipati . . . cittasamuṭṭhānānañ ca rūpānaṃ . . .
     4. Nīvaraṇavippayutto dhammo . . .
     Ārammaṇādhipati, sahajātādhipati. Ārammaṇādhipati:
-- dānaṃ sīlaṃ uposathakammaṃ taṃ garuṃ katvā paccavekkhati, pubbe suciṇṇāni jhānā vuṭṭhahitvā jhānaṃ . . .
Ariyā maggā vuṭṭhahitvā maggaṃ garuṃ katvā phalaṃ . . .
Nibbānaṃ gotrabhussa vodānassa maggassa phalassa adhipatipaccayena paccayo. Sahajātādhipati:-- nīvaraṇavippayuttādhipati sampayuttakānaṃ . . .
     5. Nīvaraṇavippayutto dhammo . . .
     Ārammaṇādhipati:-- dānaṃ . . . pe . . . pubbe . . .
jhānaṃ . . . cakkhuṃ . . . vatthuṃ . . . nīvaraṇavippayutte khandhe garuṃ katvā assādeti abhinandati, taṃ garuṃ katvā rāgo diṭṭhi uppajjati; . . . pe . . .
     1. Nīvaraṇasampayutto . . . anantara- . . . paccayo.
     Purimā purimā nīvaraṇasampayuttā khandhā pacchimānaṃ pacchimānaṃ nīvaraṇasampayuttānaṃ khandhānaṃ anantarapaccayena paccayo .

                          Upanissayavāro.                    311
[... content straddling page break has been moved to the page above ...] . . (mūlaṃ pucchitabbaṃ).
Nivaraṇasampayuttā khandhā vuṭṭhānassa anantarapaccayena paccayo. (Idha purimā purimā natthi.) Purimā purimā nīvaraṇavippayuttā khandhā . . . nīvaraṇavippayuttānaṃ . . . Anulomaṃ phalasamāpattiyā anantarapaccayena paccayo.
     5. Nīvaraṇavippayutto . . . nīvaraṇasampayuttassa . . .
     Āvajjanā nīvaraṇasampayuttānaṃ khandhānaṃ anantarapaccayena paccayo.
     1. Nīvaraṇasampayutto . . . samanantara- . . . sahajāta . . . aññamañña- . . . nissaya- . . . upanissayapaccayena paccayo.
     Ārammaṇūpanissayo, anantarūpanissayo, pakatūpanissayo . . . pe . . . Pakatūpanissayo:-- rāgaṃ upanissāya pāṇaṃ hanati, . . . pe . . . saṃghaṃ bhindati; dosaṃ,
mohaṃ, mānaṃ, diṭṭhiṃ . . . patthanaṃ upanissāya pāṇaṃ hanati . . . pe . . . saṃghaṃ bhindati; rāgo . . . pe . . .
patthanā rāgassa . . . pe . . . patthanāya upanissayapaccayena paccayo.
     2. Nīvaraṇasampayutto . . . nivaraṇavippayuttassa . . .
     Ārammaṇūpanissayo . . . pe . . . Pakatūpanissayo:-- rāgaṃ upanissāya dānaṃ deti, sīlaṃ uposathakammaṃ . . . jhānaṃ vipassanaṃ maggaṃ abhiññaṃ samāpattiṃ uppādeti; dosaṃ,
patthanaṃ upanissāya dānaṃ deti . . . pe . . . samāpattiṃ uppādeti, rāgo . . . pe . . . patthanā saddhāya . . . pe . . . paññāya kāyikassa sukhassa kāyikassa dukkhassa maggassa phalasamāpattiyā upanissayapaccayena paccayo.
     4. Nīvaraṇavippayutto . . . nīvaraṇavippayuttassa . . .
     Ārammaṇūpanissayo . . . pe . . . Pakātūpanissayo:-- saddhaṃ upanissāya dānaṃ deti, sīlaṃ . . . pe . . . maggaṃ abhiññaṃ samāpattiṃ uppādeti; sīlaṃ . . . pe . . . paññaṃ . . . pe . . . senāsanaṃ upanissāya dānaṃ deti; . . . pe . . . samāpattiṃ uppādeti; saddhā . . . pe . . . senāsanaṃ saddhāya .

312                     Nīvaraṇasampayuttadukaṃ.
[... content straddling page break has been moved to the page above ...] . . pe . . . paññāya maggassa phalasamāpattiyā upanissayapaccayena paccayo.
     5. Nīvaraṇavippayutto . . . nīvaraṇasampayuttassa . . .
     Ārammaṇūpanissayo . . . pe . . . Pakatūpanissayo:-- saddhaṃ upanissāya mānaṃ jappeti, diṭṭhiṃ gaṇhāti; sīlaṃ . . . pe . . . paññaṃ kāyikaṃ . . . pe . . . senāsanaṃ upanissāya pāṇaṃ hanati . . . pe . . . saṃghaṃ bhindati;
saddhā . . . pe . . . senāsanaṃ rāgassa dosassa mohassa mānassa diṭṭhiyā patthanāya upanissayapaccayena paccayo.
     4. Nīvaraṇavippayutto . . . purejātapaccayena paccayo.
     Ārammaṇapurejātaṃ, vatthupurejātaṃ. Ārammaṇapurejātaṃ:-- cakkhuṃ . . . pe . . . vatthuṃ aniccato dukkhato anattato vipassati, dibbena cakkhunā rūpaṃ passati, dibbāya sotadhātuyā saddaṃ suṇāti; rūpāyatanaṃ cakkhuviññāṇassa . . . phoṭṭhabbāyatanaṃ kāyaviññāṇassa . . . Vatthupurejātaṃ:-- cakkhāyatanaṃ cakkhuviññāṇassa . . . kāyāyatanaṃ kāyaviññāṇassa, vatthu nīvaraṇavippayuttānaṃ khandhānaṃ purejātapaccayena paccayo.
     5. Nīvaraṇavippayutto . . . nīvaraṇasampayuttassa . . .
     Ārammaṇapurejātaṃ . . . . . . pe . . . vatthuṃ assādeti abhinandati, taṃ ārabbha rāgo doso moho . . . Vatthupurejātaṃ:-- vatthu nīvaraṇasampayuttānaṃ khandhānaṃ purejātapaccayena paccayo.
     2. Nivaraṇasampayutto . . . nīvaraṇavippayuttassa . . . pacchājātapaccayena paccayo . . . (dve).
     1. Nīvaraṇasampayutto . . . nīvaraṇasampayuttassa . . . āsevana- . . . (dve) . . . kammapaccayena paccayo.
     Nīvaraṇasampayuttā cetanā sampayuttakānaṃ . . .
(mūlāni kātabbāni).
     Sahajāta, nānākhaṇikā. Sahajātā nīvaraṇasampayuttā cetanā cittasamuṭṭhānānaṃ . . . Nānākhaṇikā nīvaraṇasampayuttā cetanā vipākānaṃ khandhānaṃ kaṭattā ca rūpānaṃ kammapaccayena paccayo.

vippayuttapaccayena paccayo.

     Sahajātaṃ, purejātaṃ, pacchājātaṃ . . . (saṃkhittaṃ).
     5. Nīvaraṇavippayutto . . . nīvaraṇasampayuttassa . . .
     Purejātaṃ vatthuṃ nīvaraṇasampayuttānaṃ khandhānaṃ vippayuttapaccayena paccayo.
     1. Nīvaraṇasampayutto . . . atthipaccayena paccayo.
     Nīvaraṇasampayutto eko khandho tiṇṇannaṃ khandhānaṃ atthipaccayena paccayo.
     2. Nīvaraṇasampayutto . . . nīvaraṇavippayuttassa . . .
     Sahajātaṃ, pacchājātaṃ. Sahajātā nīvaraṇasampayuttā khandhā cittasamuṭṭhānānaṃ rūpānaṃ atthipaccayena paccayo. Pacchājātā nīvaraṇasampayuttā khandhā purejātassa imassa kāyassa atthipaccayena paccayo.
     3. Nīvaraṇasampayutto . . . nīvaraṇasampayuttassa ca . . .
     Nīvaraṇasampayutto eko khandho tiṇṇannaṃ khandhānaṃ ciṭṭasamuṭṭhānānañ ca; dve . . . dvinnaṃ . . .
     4. Nīvaraṇavippayutto . . . nīvaraṇavippayuttassa . . .
     Sahajātaṃ, purejātaṃ, pacchājātaṃ āhāraṃ indriyaṃ . . .
(saṃkhittaṃ).

314                     Nīvaraṇasampayuttadukaṃ.
     5. Nīvaraṇavippayutto . . . nīvaraṇasampayuttassa . . .
     Purejātaṃ:-- cakkhuṃ . . . vatthuṃ assādeti abhinandati, taṃ ārabbha rāgo diṭṭhi vicikicchā uddhaccaṃ domanassaṃ uppajjati. Vatthu nīvaraṇasampayuttānaṃ khandhānaṃ atthipaccayena paccayo.
     7. Nīvaraṇasampayutto ca . . . nīvaraṇasampayuttassa . . .
     Sahajātaṃ, purejātaṃ. Sahajāto nīvaraṇasampayutto eko khandho ca vatthu ca tiṇṇannaṃ khandhānaṃ atthipaccayena paccayo; dve . . . dvinnaṃ . . .
     8. Nīvaraṇasampayutto ca . . . nīvaraṇavippayuttassa . . .
     Sahajātaṃ, pacchājātaṃ āhāraṃ indriyaṃ. Sahajātā nīvaraṇasampayuttā khandhā ca mahābhūtā ca cittasamuṭṭhānānaṃ . . . Pacchājātā nīvaraṇasampayuttā khandhā ca kabaḷiṃkāro āhāro ca imassa kāyassa atthipaccayena paccayo. Pacchājātā nīvaraṇasampayuttā khandhā ca rūpajīvitindriyañ ca kaṭattā rūpānaṃ atthipaccayena paccayo.

          pacchājāte dve,                vigate cattāri,
          āsevane dve,                     avigate satta.

                               316
                               [XXXVI.
                NĪVARAṆO-CEVA-NĪVARAṆIYA-DUKAṂ.]
     1. Nīvaraṇaṃ ceva nīvaraṇiyaṃ dhammaṃ paṭicca nīvaraṇo ceva nīvaraṇiyo ca dhammo uppajjati hetupaccayā.
     Kāmacchandanīvaraṇaṃ paṭicca thīnamiddha-, uddhacca-,
avijjānīvaraṇaṃ . . . (Evaṃ sabbe gaṇanā vibhajitabbā nīvaraṇadukasadisā. Ninnānākaraṇā Āsavadukasadisā2.)
     1. Nīvaraṇo ceva nīvaraṇiyo dhammo nīvaraṇassa ceva nīvaraṇiyassa ca dhammassa hetupaccayena paccayo.
     Nīvaraṇā ceva nīvaraṇiyā ca hetū sampayuttakānaṃ nīvaraṇānaṃ hetupaccayena paccayo.
     2. Nīvaraṇo ceva nīvaraṇiyo ca dhammo nīvaraṇiyassa ceva no ca nīvaraṇassa dhammassa hetupaccayena paccayo.
     Nīvaraṇā ceva nīvaraṇiyā ca hetū sampayuttakānaṃ khandhānaṃ cittasamuṭṭhānānañ ca rūpānaṃ hetupaccayena paccayo.
     3. Nīvaraṇo . . . nīvaraṇassa ceva . . . no ca nīvaraṇassa ca dhammassa . . .
     Nīvaraṇā . . . khandhānaṃ nīvaraṇānañ ca cittasamuṭṭhānānañ ca . . .
     4. Nīvaraṇiyo ceva no ca nīvaraṇo . . .
     Nīvaraṇiyā ceva no ca nivaraṇā hetū . . . (paṭisandhi).


[page 317]
                          Ārammaṇavāro.                     317
     1. Nīvaraṇo ceva . . . nīvaraṇiyassa dhammassa ārammaṇapaccayena paccayo.
     Nīvaraṇe ārabbha nīvaraṇā uppajjanti . . . (mūlaṃ pucchitabbaṃ). Nīvaraṇe ārabbha nīvaraṇiyā ceva no ca nīvaraṇā khandhā uppajjanti . . . (mūlaṃ pucchitabbaṃ).
Nivaraṇe ārabbha nīvaraṇā ca sampayuttakā ca khandhā uppajjanti.
     4. Nīvaraṇiyo ceva no ca nīvaraṇo . . .
     Dānaṃ, sīlaṃ, uposathakammaṃ katvā taṃ paccavekkhati.
assādeti abhinandati, taṃ ārabbha rāgo, diṭṭhi, vicikicchā,
uddhaccaṃ, domanassaṃ uppajjati. Pubbe suciṇṇāni . . .
jhānā . . . ariyā gotrabhuṃ paccavekkhanti, vodānaṃ,
pahīnakilese vikkhambhitakilese . . . pubbe samudāciṇṇe . . . Cakkhuṃ . . . vatthuṃ nīvaraṇiye ceva no ca nīvaraṇe khandhe aniccato vipassati; assādeti abhinandati, . . .
pe . . . domanassaṃ . . . pe . . . dibbena cakkhunā . . . (yāva āvajjanā tāva kātabbā).
     5. Nīvaraṇiyo ceva no ca nīvaraṇo . . . nīvaraṇassa ceva . . .
     Dānaṃ, sīlaṃ, uposathakammaṃ, pubbe suciṇṇāni, jhānā . . . cakkhuṃ . . . abhinandati, taṃ ārabbha rāgo, diṭṭhi,
vicikicchā, uddhaccaṃ, domanassaṃ uppajjati.
     6. Nīvaraṇiyo ceva no ca nīvaraṇo . . . nīvaraṇassa ceva . . . no ca nīvaraṇassa . . .
     Dānaṃ . . . taṃ ārabbha nīvaraṇā ca sampayuttakā ca khandhā uppajjanti . . . (evaṃ itare tīṇi kātabbā ārammaṇasadisā; adhipatipaccayo purejātaṃ pi ārammaṇasadisaṃ.
Upanissaye pi lokuttaraṃ na kātabbaṃ. Saṃkhittaṃ. Evaṃ vitthāretabbaṃ. Yathā nīvaraṇadukaṃ, evaṃ paccavekkhitvā kātabbaṃ.)
                NĪVARAṆO-CEVA-NĪVARAṆIYA-DUKAṂ niṭṭhitaṃ.


[page 318]
                               318
                              [XXXVII.
                NIVARAṆO-CEVA-NIVARAṆASAMPAYUTTA-DUKAṂ.]
     1. Nivaraṇañ ceva nīvaraṇasampayuttaṃ dhammaṃ paṭicca nīvaraṇo ceva nīvaraṇasampayutto dhammo uppajjati hetupaccayā.
     Kāmacchandanīvaraṇaṃ paṭicca thīnamiddha-, uddhacca-,
avijjā-nīvaraṇaṃ . . . (cakkaṃ, sabbe nīvaraṇā kātabbā).
     2. Nīvaraṇañ ceva . . . nīvaraṇasampayutto ceva no ca nīvaraṇo . . .
     Nīvaraṇe paṭicca sampayuttakā khandhā.
     3. Nīvaraṇañ ceva . . . nīvaraṇo ceva . . ṇivaraṇasampayutto ceva no ca nīvaraṇo . . .
     Kāmacchandanīvaraṇaṃ paṭicca thīnamiddha-, uddhacca-,
avijjā-nīvaraṇaṃ sampayuttakā ca khandhā . . . (cakkaṃ).
     4. Nīvaraṇasampayuttaṃ ceva no ca nīvaraṇaṃ . . .
     Nīvaraṇasampayuttañ ceva no ca nīvaraṇaṃ ekaṃ khandhaṃ paṭicca tayo khandhā; dve . . .

     Nīvaraṇasampayutte ceva no ca nīvaraṇe khandhe paṭicca nīvaraṇā.

nīvaraṇo ceva . . . no ca nīvaraṇo ca . . .
     Nīvaraṇasampayuttañ ceva . . . khandhā nīvaraṇā ca;
dve . . .

Sahajātādhipati:-- (a) nīvaraṇasampayuttā ceva no ca nīvaraṇādhipati sampayuttakānaṃ khandhānaṃ adhipatipaccayena paccayo . . . (mūlāni pucchitabbāni).
(b) Nīvaraṇasampayutte ceva no ca nīvaraṇe khandhe garuṃ katvā nīvaraṇā uppajjanti. Sahajātādhipati:-- nīvaraṇasampayuttā . . . sampayuttakānaṃ nīvaraṇānaṃ adhipatipaccayena paccayo . . . (mūlaṃ). Nīvaraṇasampayutte . . . nīvaraṇā ca sampayuttakā ca khandhā uppajjanti.
Sahajātādhipati:-- nivaraṇasampayuttā . . . khandhānaṃ nīvaraṇānañ ca adhipatipaccayena paccayo.

     1. Parāmāso . . . ārammaṇapaccayena paccayo.

     4. No parāmāso dhammo no parāmāsassa . . .
     Dānaṃ, sīlaṃ, uposathakammaṃ katvā, taṃ paccavekkhati,
assādeti, abhinandati, taṃ ārabbha rāgo, diṭṭhi, vicikicchā,

jhānā vuṭṭhahitvā jhānaṃ . . . Ariyā maggā vuṭṭhahitvā maggaṃ, phalaṃ, nibbānaṃ paccavekkhanti. Nibbānaṃ gotrabhussa vodānassa maggassa phalassa āvajjanāya ārammaṇapaccayena paccayo. Ariyā no parāmāse pahīnakilese vikkhambhitakilese pubbe . . . Cakkhuṃ . . . vatthuṃ no parāmāse khandhe aniccato vipassati . . . pe . . .
assādeti, abhinandati, taṃ ārabbha rāgo, diṭṭhi, vicikicchā,

phoṭṭhabbāyatanaṃ kāyaviññāṇassa, no parāmāsā khandhā iddhividhañāṇassa cetopariyañāṇassa pubbenivāsānussatiñāṇassa yathākammūpagañāṇassa anāgataṃsañāṇassa āvajjanāya ārammaṇapaccayena paccayo.
     5. No parāmāso . . . parāmāsassa dhammassa . . .
     Dānaṃ, sīlaṃ, uposathakammaṃ, taṃ assādeti . . . rāgo uppajjati, diṭṭhi . . . pe . . . pubbe jhānā . . . pe . . .
cakkhuṃ . . . vatthuṃ no parāmāse khandhe assādeti,
abhinandati; taṃ ārabbha rāgo diṭṭhi . . . pe . . .
     6. No parāmāso . . . parāmāsassa ca . . .
     Dānaṃ . . . taṃ assādeti, abhinandati, taṃ ārabbha parāmāso ca sampayuttakā ca khandhā uppajjanti. Pubbe

     (a) Purimo purimo parāmāso pacchimassa pacchimassa parāmāsassa anantarapaccayena paccayo . . . (mūlaṃ kātabbaṃ). (b) Purimo purimo parāmāso pacchimānaṃ pacchimānaṃ no parāmāsānaṃ khandhānaṃ anantarapaccayena paccayo. Parāmāso vuṭṭhānassa anantarapaccayena paccayo. Senāsanaṃ upanissāya dānaṃ deti, . . . pe . . . samāpattiṃ uppādeti; pāṇaṃ hanati . . . pe . . . saṃghaṃ bhindati.      Hetupaccayā, nārammaṇe tīṇi, nādhipatiyā pañca:-- evaṃ kātabbaṃ.

     (Sahajātavāro paṭiccavārasadiso.)

     4. Parāmāsavippayuttaṃ . . . parāmāsavippayutto . . .

342                     Parāmāsasampayuttadukaṃ.
     1. Parāmāsasampayutto dhammo parāmāsasampayuttassa dhammassa hetupaccayena paccayo.
     (a) Parāmāsasampayuttā hetū sampayuttakānaṃ khandhānaṃ hetupaccayena paccayo . . . (mūlāni kātabbāni).
(b) Parāmāsasampayuttā hetū cittasamuṭṭhānānaṃ rūpānaṃ hetupaccayena paccayo. (c) Parāmāsasampayuttā hetū . . . (cf. a) cittasamuṭṭhānānañ ca . . . (cf. b).
     4. Parāmāsavippayutto . . . parāmāsavippayuttassa . . .
     Parāmāsavippayuttā hetū . . . (cf. c) paccayo . . .
(paṭisandhi).
     1. Parāmāsasampayutto . . . ārammaṇapaccayena paccayo.
     Rāgaṃ assādeti, abhinandati, taṃ ārabbha rāgo uppajjati diṭṭhi uppajjati. Diṭṭhiṃ assādeti . . . rāgo diṭṭhi uppajjati.
     2. Parāmāsasampayutto . . . parāmāsavippayuttassa . . .
     Ariyā parāmāsasampayutte pahībakilese paccavekkhanti,
vikkhambhitakilese paccavekkhanti, pubbe samudāciṇṇe kilese jānanti, parāmāsasampayutte khandhe aniccato vipassanti . . . assādeti, abhinandati, taṃ ārabbha parāmāsavippayutto rāgo, diṭṭhi, vicikicchā, uddhaccaṃ, domanassaṃ uppajjati. Cetopariyañāṇena parāmāsasampayuttacittasamaṃgissa cittaṃ jānāti. Parāmāsasampayuttā khandhā cetopariyañāṇassa pubbenivāsānussatiñāṇassa yathākammūpagañāṇassa anāgataṃsañāṇassa āvajjanāya ārammaṇapaccayena paccayo.
     4. Parāmāsavippayutto . . . parāmāsavippayuttassa . . .
     Dānaṃ, sīlaṃ, uposathakammaṃ katvā taṃ paccavekkhati,
assādeti . . . uppajjati. Pubbe suciṇṇāni . . . jhānā . . . Ariyā maggā vuṭṭhahitvā maggaṃ paccavekkhanti,
phalaṃ, nibbānaṃ paccavekkhanti. Nibbānaṃ gotrabhussa yodānassa maggassa phalassa āvajjanāya ārammaṇapaccayena paccayo. Ariyā parāmāsavippayutte pahīnakilese vikkhambhitakilese . . . pubbe . . . cakkhuṃ . . .

348                     Parāmāsāsasampayuttadukaṃ.

     8. Parāmāsasampayutto ca . . . parāmāsavippayuttassa . . .
     Sahajātaṃ, pacchājātaṃ, āhāraṃ, indriyaṃ. Sahajātā parāmāsasampayuttā khandhā ca mahābhūtā ca cittasamuṭṭhānānaṃ rūpānaṃ atthipaccayena paccayo. Pacchājātā parāmāsasampayuttā khandhā ca kabaḷiṃkāro āhāro ca imassa kāyassa atthipaccaccayena paccayo. Pacchājātā parāmāsasampayuttā khandhā ca rūpajīvitindriyañ ca kaṭattā rūpānaṃ atthipaccayena paccayo.

          ārammaṇe cattāri,                vipāke ekaṃ,
          adhipatiyā pañca.                ājāre cattāri,
          anantare cattāri,                indriye cattāri,
          samanantare cattāri,           jhāne cattāri,
          sahajāte pañca,                magge cattāri,
          aññamaññe dve,                    sampayutte dve,
          nissaye satta,                    vippayutte tīṇi,
          upanissaye cattāri,               atthiyā satta,
          purejāte dve,                     natthiyā cattāri,
          pacchājāte dve,                vigate cattāri.
          āsevane dve,                     avigate satta.
     1. Parāmāsasampayutto dhammo . . . ārammaṇa-,
sahajāta-, upanissayapaccayena paccayo.
     2. Parāmāsasampayutto dhammo . . . ārammaṇa-, sahajāta-, upanissaya-, pacchājāta-, kammapaccayena paccayo.
     3. Parāmāsasampayutto dhammo . . . sahajātapaccayena paccayo.
     4. Parāmāsavippayutto dhammo ārammaṇa-, sahajāta-,
upanissaya-, purejāta-, pacchājāta-, kamma-, āhāra-, indriyapaccayena paccayo.
     5. Parāmāsavippayutto dhammo . . . ārammaṇa-, sahajāta-, upanissaya-, purejātapaccayena paccayo.

                          Mātikā.                          349
     7. Parāmāsasampayutto ca . . . sahajāta-, purejātapaccayena paccayo.
     8. Parāmāsasampayutto ca . . . parāmāsavippayuttassa dhammassa sahajāta-, pacchājāta-,āhāra-,indriyapaccayena paccayo.
          Nahetuyā satta,                napacchājāte satta,
          nārammaṇe satta,                sabbatthā satta;
          nādhipatiyā satta,                namagge satta,
          nānantare satta,                nasampayutte pañca,
          nasamanantare satta,           navippayutte cattāri,
          nasahajāte pañca,                no-atthiyā cattāri,
          na-aññamaññe pañca,               nonatthiyā satta,
          nanissaye pañca,                novigate satta,
          na-upanissaye satta,           no-avigate cattāri.
          napurejāte cha,
          Hetupaccayā, nārammaṇe           sabbattha cattāri;
           cattāri,                     namagge cattāri,
          nādhipatiyā cattāri,           nasampayutte dve,
          nānantare cattāri,               navippayutte dve,
          nasamanantare cattāri,           nonatthiyā cattāri,
          na-aññamaññe dve,                novigate cattāri.
          na-upanissaye cattāri,
          Nahetupaccayā, ārammaṇe      adhipatiyā pañca (anulo-
           cattāri,                     mamātikā kātabbā).
                          avigate satta.
                PARĀMĀSASAMPAYUTTA-DUKAṂ niṭṭhitaṃ.


[page 350]
                               350
                               [XLII.
                     PARĀMĀSO-CEVA-PARĀMAṬṬHA-DUKAṂ.]
     2. Parāmāsañ ceva parāmaṭṭhaṃ ca dhammaṃ paṭicca parāmaṭṭho ceva no ca parāmāso dhammo uppajjati hetupaccayā.
     Parāmāsaṃ paṭicca sampayuttakā khandhā cittasamuṭṭhānañ ca rūpaṃ.
     4. Parāmaṭṭhañ ceva no ca parāmāsaṃ dhammaṃ paṭicca parāmaṭṭho ceva no ca parāmāso . . .
     Parāmaṭṭhañ ceva no ca parāmāsaṃ ekaṃ khandhaṃ paṭicca tayo khandhā cittasamuṭṭhānañ ca rūpaṃ; dve . . . (paṭisandhi, yāva ajjhattikā mahābhūtā).
     5. Parāmaṭṭhañ ceva no ca parāmāsaṃ . . . parāmāso ceva parāmaṭṭho ca . . .
     Parāmaṭṭhe ceva no ca parāmāse khandhe paṭicca parāmāso.
     6. Parāmaṭṭhañ ceva no ca parāmāsaṃ dhammaṃ paṭicca parāmāso ceva parāmāṭṭho ca parāmaṭṭho ceva no ca parāmāso ca . . .
     Parāmaṭṭhañ ceva . . . khandhā parāmāso ca cittasamuṭṭhānañ ca . . . dve . . .
     8. Parāmāsañ ceva parāmaṭṭhañ ca parāmaṭṭhañ ceva no ca parāmāsañ ca . . . parāmaṭṭho ceva no ca parāmāso . . .
     Parāmaṭṭhañ ceva no ca parāmāsaṃ ekaṃ khandhañ ca parāmāsañ ca paṭicca tayo . . . (saṃkhittaṃ. Sabbe vārā yathā parāmāsadukaṃ, evaṃ kātabbaṃ. Ninnānākaraṇaṃ).


[page 351]
                          Ārammaṇavāro.                     351
     4. Parāmaṭṭho ceva no ca parāmāso dhammo parāmaṭṭhassa ceva no ca parāmāsassa dhammassa hetupaccayena paccayo.
     Parāmaṭṭhā ceva no ca parāmāsā hetū sampayuttakānaṃ khandhānaṃ cittasamuṭṭhānānañ ca rūpānaṃ hetupaccayena paccayo . . . (paṭisandhi).
     5. Parāmaṭṭho ceva no ca parāmāso . . .
     Parāmaṭṭhā ceva no ca parāmāsā hetū parāmāsassa hetupaccayena paccayo.
     6. Parāmaṭṭho ceva no ca parāmāsassa ca . . .
     Parāmaṭṭhā ceva no ca parāmāsā hetū sampayuttakānaṃ khandhānaṃ parāmāsassa ca cittasamuṭṭhānānañ ca rūpānaṃ hetupaccayena paccayo.
     1. Parāmāso ceva parāmaṭṭho ca . . . dhammassa ārammaṇapaccayena paccayo . . . (tīṇi ārabbha kātabbāni;
parāmāsdukasadisaṃ).
     4. Parāmaṭṭho ceva no ca parāmāso . . .
     Dānaṃ, sīlaṃ, uposathakammaṃ katvā taṃ paccavekkhati,
assādeti, abhinandati, taṃ ārabbha rāgo uppajjati, diṭṭhi,
vicikicchā, uddhaccaṃ, domanassaṃ uppajjati. Pubbe . . .
jhānā . . . Ariyā . . . gotrabhuṃ paccavekkhanti, vodānaṃ paccavekkhanti, pahīnakilese, vikkhambhitakilese . . . pubbe . . . cakkhuṃ . . . vatthuṃ parāmaṭṭhe ceva no ca parāmāse khandhe aniccato . . . pe . . . domanassaṃ uppajjati. Dibbena cakkhunā rūpaṃ passati . . . (yāva āvajjanā sabbaṃ kātabbaṃ).
     5. Parāmaṭṭho ceva no ca parāmāso dhammo parāmāsassa ceva parāmaṭṭhassa dhammassa ārammaṇapaccayena paccayo.
     Dānaṃ . . . Pubbe . . . jhānā . . . cakkhuṃ . . . khandhe assādeti, abhinandati, taṃ ārabbha rāgo uppajjati diṭṭhi . . . pe . . .
     6. Parāmaṭṭho ceva no ca . . . parāmāsassa ceva parāmaṭṭhassa ca parāmaṭṭhassa ceva no ca parāmasassa ca dhammassa ārammaṇapaccayena paccayo.


[page 352]
352                Parāmāso-ceva-parāmaṭṭhadukaṃ.
     Dānaṃ, silaṃ, uposathakammaṃ . . . pubbe . . . jhānā cakkhuṃ . . . aniccato vipassati, assādeti abhinandati, taṃ ārabbha parāmāso ca sampayuttakā ca khandhā uppajjanti.
(Evaṃ itare pi tīṇi ārabbha kātabbāni. Imaṃ dukaṃ parāmāsadukasadisaṃ. Lokuttaraṃ yamhi na labbhati, tamhi na kātabbaṃ.)
               PARĀMĀSO-CEVA-PARĀMAṬṬHA-DUKAṂ niṭṭhitaṃ.


[page 353]
                          353
                          [XLIII.
           PARĀMĀSAVIPPAYUTTA-PARĀMAṬṬHA-DUKAṂ.]
     1. Parāmāsavippayuttaparāmaṭṭhaṃ dhammaṃ paṭicca parāmāsavippayuttaparāmaṭṭho dhammo uppajjati hetupaccayā.
     Parāmāsavippayuttaparāmaṭṭhaṃ ekaṃ khandhaṃ paṭicca tayo khandhā cittasamuṭṭhānañ ca rūpaṃ; dve . . .
     4. Parāmāsavippayutta-aparāmaṭṭhaṃ dhammaṃ paṭicca parāmāsavippayutta-aparāmaṭṭho dhammo uppajjati hetupaccayā . . . (saṃkhittaṃ; yathā cūḷantaraduke lokiyadukaṃ evaṃ kātabbaṃ. Ninnānākaraṇaṃ).
           PARĀMĀSAVIPPAYUTTA-PARĀMAṬṬHA-DUKAṂ niṭṭhitaṃ.
